### [93] [Domain Adaptation and Reasoning Frameworks in Language Models: A Controlled Experiment with Historical Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30415)
*Francesco De Bernardis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过历史天文学这一受控场景，探讨领域适应如何重塑语言模型的解释行为。在第一阶段，使用去除日心说明确引用的前哥白尼语料库从头训练小型模型，评估是否仍会出现地动或日心延续；第二阶段，利用QLoRA对大型预训练模型进行微调，研究适应如何改变解释框架和宇宙观立场。通过大语言模型作为评判者的方法评估输出，标记宇宙观立场（地心、日心或模糊）和解释框架（前现代与现代）。结果显示，在第一阶段，小模型偶尔生成局部的地动延续，但整体不稳，无法支持连贯的宇宙论推理；第二阶段，微调显著且统计上显著地促使模型转向前现代解释框架，而条件下的宇宙观立场分布相对稳定。因此，地心输出的增加主要源于解释范式的重新分配，而非立场本身的直接改变。表明领域适应可能主要重塑生成延续的语言框架，立场变化则为次生结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究领域适应如何影响语言模型在特定历史背景下的解释行为，特别是其对宇宙观立场和解释框架的影响，以理解模型如何在受限语境中形成认知结构。

Method: 采用两阶段实验：第一阶段从头训练小型语言模型于去除了日心说引用的前哥白尼语料库；第二阶段使用QLoRA对大型预训练模型进行微调。通过大语言模型作为评判者的方法评估模型输出的宇宙观立场和解释框架，分析其分布变化。

Result: 小型模型在第一阶段仅出现零星地动延续，但整体不稳，无法支撑连贯宇宙论推理；第二阶段微调导致显著向预现代解释框架转移，而条件下的宇宙观立场分布保持相对稳定；地心输出增加主要源于解释框架的再分配，而非立场的直接改变。

Conclusion: 领域适应更可能优先重塑语言模型生成内容的解释框架，而宇宙观立场的变化是该框架调整后的次生结果。这提示我们在设计模型时需关注其解释范式如何被迁移所影响。

Abstract: We investigate how domain adaptation reshapes explanatory behavior in language models using historical cosmology as a controlled setting. In Phase 1, we train a small language model from scratch on a pre-Copernican corpus from which explicit heliocentric references were removed, and evaluate whether Earth-motion or heliocentric continuations nevertheless emerge. In Phase 2, we fine-tune a larger pretrained model using QLoRA on the same corpus in order to study how adaptation modifies explanatory framing and cosmological stance. Model outputs are evaluated using an LLM-as-judge framework that labels both cosmological stance (geocentric, heliocentric, or ambiguous) and explanatory frame (premodern versus modern). In the constrained setting of Phase 1, the smaller models occasionally generate local Earth-motion continuations, but these remain globally unstable and insufficient to support coherent cosmological reasoning. In Phase 2, fine-tuning induces a large and statistically significant shift toward premodern explanatory framing, while the conditional cosmological stance distributions remain comparatively stable within those frames. As a result, increases in geocentric outputs arise primarily from redistribution over explanatory regimes rather than from direct modification of stance. These results suggest that domain adaptation may primarily reshape the linguistic frameworks from which continuations are generated, with changes in stance emerging secondarily from those shifts.

</details>


### [94] [Cross-Lingual Steering for Figurative Language Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30443)
*Linfeng Liu,Tiffany Zhan,Louie Hong Yao,Saptarshi Ghosh,Tianyu Jiang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过激活引导技术，探究多语言大模型中隐喻生成的内在信号是否跨语言通用。结果表明，尽管各语言中的隐喻生成方向具有特定性，但这些方向在不同语言间具有可迁移性，尤其在德语中表现突出；跨语言组合的方向甚至能超越本族语言的原生方向，说明存在一种可复用但依赖目标语言的跨语言隐喻生成信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究多语言大模型中隐喻生成的内部信号是否具有语言特异性或跨语言通用性，以理解其生成机制。

Method: 采用激活引导方法，基于一种语言中隐喻与字面表达的激活差异提取方向，并将其应用于其他语言的生成过程，评估其有效性与可迁移性。

Result: 在五种隐喻类别、六种语言和四种多语言大模型上，所提取的方向在本语言中有效，且跨语言迁移成功；特别是德语对其他语言的方向表现出高度响应；跨语言组合方向甚至优于本族语言方向，移除共享成分后原生方向效果减弱。

Conclusion: 研究提供了直接证据，表明多语言大模型中存在一种可复用但依赖目标语言的跨语言隐喻生成信号。

Abstract: Multilingual large language models can generate figurative language, but whether the internal signals driving this behavior are language-specific or reusable across languages is unclear. Using activation steering as a probe, we estimate a direction for a figurative category from figurative--literal activation differences in one language and apply it during generation. Across five figurative categories, six languages, and four multilingual LLMs, these directions steer reliably within their own language, most robustly for metaphor and simile. More importantly, they transfer across languages: a direction learned in one increases the target behavior when applied to another, with German among the most receptive targets. Going further, directions assembled from other languages can match or even surpass a target language's own native direction, while removing this shared component weakens native steering. Together, these results provide direct evidence of a reusable but target-dependent cross-lingual signal for figurative generation.

</details>


### [95] [Can LLM Teams Play What? Where? When?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30459)
*Anastasia Kotelnikova,Viktor Byzov,Maria Dolzhenkova,Evgeny Kotelnikov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了团队协作对大语言模型在需要间接推理、文化知识和协同假设检验的任务中的表现影响。通过引入投票、沉默团队和对话团队三种策略，在2025年发布的572个ChGK问题数据集上评估六种主流开源大模型，发现团队策略相比单模型基准最高可提升20个百分点准确率，最佳团队达到44.23%准确率，接近人类团队水平。分析显示，模型间分歧严重时准确率下降，但解释性沟通能有效缓解这一问题。此外，队长行为无自我偏好偏差，且参考同伴推理过程能提升判断质量。整体表明LLM团队主要起答案筛选与错误过滤作用，而非生成新解。研究强调交互的重要性，并建议自适应策略为多智能体系统的重要方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在需要间接推理、文化知识和协同假设检验的任务中表现有限，亟需探索更高效的协作机制以提升性能。

Method: 设计并测试三种团队策略（投票、沉默团队、对话团队），在包含572道ChGK问题的数据集上使用六种大型开放模型进行评估，通过分析模型间差异、沟通内容及队长决策行为来探究团队协作效果。

Result: 团队策略显著优于单模型基线，最高提升20个百分点准确率；最佳团队达44.23%准确率，接近人类团队表现；模型分歧降低准确率，但解释性沟通可有效缓解；队长无自我偏好，参考同伴推理可提升判断质量。

Conclusion: LLM团队主要作为答案选择与错误过滤机制，而非创新解决方案生成者；交互机制至关重要，未来多智能体系统应探索自适应协作策略。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) remain limited on tasks requiring indirect reasoning, cultural knowledge, and coordinated hypothesis testing. We investigate whether team-based interaction improves LLM performance in What? Where? When? (ChGK), a quiz game designed to reward collective reasoning. We introduce three team strategies: Voting, Silent Team (the captain observes final answers), and Talkative Team (the captain observes both answers and rationales). To minimize data leakage, we evaluate these strategies on a dataset consisting of 572 ChGK questions released in 2025. Using six recent large-scale open models, we show that team-based strategies outperform single-model baselines, yielding gains of up to 20 percentage points in accuracy. The best team achieves 44.23% accuracy, and approaches human team performance on questions with available human statistics. Analysis of inter-model diversity reveals that disagreement strongly predicts lower accuracy, but explanatory communication substantially mitigates performance drops. We further examine captain behavior and find no evidence of self-preference bias; access to peer rationales improves captain judgments. Overall, LLM teams function primarily as answer selection and error-filtering mechanisms rather than generators of novel solutions. Our findings highlight the importance of interaction and suggest adaptive strategies as a promising direction for multi-agent systems.

</details>


### [96] [Knowledge Graph-Enhanced Zero-Shot Topic Classification: A Multi-Strategy Comparative Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30465)
*Shahana Akter,Yatharth Vohra,Ankita Shukla,Souvika Sarkar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种零样本多标签主题分类框架，通过为每篇文章构建知识图谱来增强分类性能。实验对比了四种基础方法及对应的图增强版本，在15个大语言模型和8个跨领域多标签数据集上进行测试。结果显示，关键词增强分类（AK）在基础框架中表现最佳，6个大模型超越了句向量基线；而知识图谱增强对小模型有正向提升，对大模型则产生负面影响，说明大模型已具备充分的关联信息。此外，自一致性解码虽增加计算成本五倍，但未带来性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多标签主题分类在无标注训练数据的情况下极具挑战性，尤其当文档包含复杂关系信息时。现有方法难以有效利用文档内部的语义与结构关系，因此需要探索无需标注数据的高效分类框架，并研究知识图谱增强对分类效果的影响。

Method: 提出一种零样本多标签主题分类框架，包含四种变体：仅基于文章、关键词增强、以及这两种的自一致性解码版本。同时，为每篇文章构建基于三元组（主语-谓语-宾语）的知识图谱，采用类似KGGen的流水线提取。共测试八种方法（四基础+四图增强），在15个LLM和8个多标签数据集上评估性能。

Result: 关键词增强分类（AK）在基础框架中表现最优；6个大模型超过句向量基线；知识图谱增强对小模型有益，对大模型有害，表明大模型预训练阶段已包含足够关系信息；自一致性解码虽显著增加计算开销（约五倍），但未带来性能提升。

Conclusion: 知识图谱增强在小模型上有效，但在大模型上可能冗余甚至有害；自一致性解码不具性价比；关键词增强是当前最有效的零样本多标签分类策略。

Abstract: Multi-label topic classification without labeled training data is a challenging task, specially when documents contain complex relational information. We present a zero-shot multi-label topic classification framework and systematically investigate how per-article knowledge graph augmentation affects its performance. The base framework classifies topics in documents without labeled training data and has four variants: article-only classification, keyword-enhanced classification, and self-consistency decoding variants of both. Then, we augment each base variant with per article knowledge graph. This graph is extracted from the input document through a pipeline similar to KGGen based on subject-predicate-object triples. We test all eight methods, four base and four graph augmented on fifteen LLMs and eight multi-label datasets across different domains. For the base framework, keyword-enhanced classification (AK) is the best performing method, and six out of fifteen LLMs surpass the sentence-encoder baseline. Graph augmentation has positive and negative impacts on small and large models, respectively. This shows that larger models already contain enough relational information from pretraining. Furthermore, the self-consistency decoding variant does not show performance improvements in any experiment while increasing computation costs about fivefold.

We find large quality-of-service differences across mWhisper-Flamingo and Gemini models, with drops of up to 4.05 word error rate points, across self-declared gender, ethnicity, and their intersection. ### [98] [When English Rewrites Local Knowledge: Global Narrative Dominance in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30481)
*Md Arid Hasan,Ruwad Naswan,Farhan Samir,Sharifa Sultana,Syed Ishtiaque Ahmed*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在跨语言应用中常受全球主导叙事影响，忽视本地文化背景，尤其在低资源语言如孟加拉语中表现尤为明显，导致文化表达失真。因此亟需系统性评估并改进其文化敏感性与本地化能力。

Method: 构建CulturalNB数据集，包含717个孟加拉文化实例，提供双语问答对、支持证据、元数据与社会文化标注；采用问题仅提示与基于证据的提示方式，评估9种SOTA LLM；结合人类与两个独立LLM裁判，从多个维度分析模型表现。

Result: 英语提问显著增加全球替代和机构化框架，减少本地视角覆盖；本地证据可改善事实一致性和视角覆盖，但不能完全消除语言引发的认知偏移。

Conclusion: LLMs的文化失败不仅源于知识缺失，更深层原因是缺乏文化根基与叙事优先级错位，强调需在训练与评估中重视本地化证据与多视角平衡。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are widely used as cross-lingual knowledge interfaces. However, culturally grounded questions often reflect globally dominant narratives rather than local contexts. We study this failure mode as \textit{global narrative dominance} in Bangla, a low-resource cultural context. We introduce \texttt{CulturalNB}, a dataset of 717 manually curated Bengali cultural instances with parallel Bangla--English question--answer pairs and supporting evidence, metadata, and sociocultural annotations. Using question-only and evidence-based prompting, we evaluate nine state-of-the-art LLMs with human and two independent LLM judges across metrics for cross-lingual consistency, language anchoring, global substitution, institutional bias, and epistemic perspective coverage. Results show that questions asked in English systematically increase global substitution and institutional framing while reducing local perspective coverage. Local evidence improves factual consistency and perspective coverage, but does not eliminate language-induced epistemic shifts. These findings suggest that cultural failures in LLMs are not only missing-knowledge errors but also failures of grounding and narrative prioritization.

Abstract: Aligning large language models (LLMs) to heterogeneous and rapidly evolving safety requirements remains a critical challenge. We introduce the Configurable Safety Reward Model (CSRM), which is jointly optimized for calibrated safety compliance and reward modeling. Our approach is supported by configuration-targeted data augmentation that enforces instruction adherence while preserving relative severity structure. The resulting RM is sensitive to fine-grained safety configurations and conversational nuances, substantially improving generalization to previously unseen safety configurations. CSRM achieves state-of-the-art performance on recent configurable safety benchmarks, including CoSApien (94.6% F1) and DynaBench (75.8% F1), without requiring additional human annotation. Conclusion: CanLegalRAGBench为评估法律RAG系统提供了更真实、可靠的基准，有助于识别并解决当前系统在准确性、相关性和可信度方面的关键缺陷，推动该领域持续发展。

Moreover, Canadian law remains underrepresented in existing evaluations. To address this gap, we introduce CanLegalRAGBench, a Canadian legal QA benchmark based on realistic queries and expert-annotated answers grounded in case law. ### [101] [Linear Ensembles Wash Away Watermarks: On the Fragility of Distributional Perturbations in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30501)
*Zhihao Wu,Gracia Gong,Qinglin Zhu,Yudong Chen,Runcong Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了在多模型环境下水印技术的固有缺陷：当用户访问多个模型时，水印几乎失效。由于各模型的水印扰动通常是独立的，通过平均输出概率分布可近乎恢复原始分布，实验表明仅平均3-5个模型即可消除水印信号。为此提出WASH方法，解决异构模型间的词汇不匹配和分词差异问题。在六种水印方案和三种大模型上的实验显示，平均3个模型可将检测z分数从5-300降至2以下（低于4的检测阈值），同时将5%误报率下的真正例率降至50%以下，且生成质量提升27.5%，速度比最优基线快6倍。结果表明，当前水印难以实现鲁棒的AI文本检测，除非模型提供方进行前所未有的协同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有水印技术依赖于对生成分布的微小扰动来标记AI文本，但在多模型并行使用场景下，不同模型的独立扰动导致水印信号被平均抵消，使检测失效。研究旨在揭示这一根本性漏洞，并提出有效对抗策略。

Method: 提出WASH（Watermark Attenuation via Statistical Hybridisation）方法，通过统计混合策略对多个异构模型的输出进行平均，以消除水印扰动；针对词汇不一致与分词差异问题设计适配机制，提升实际应用可行性。

Result: 实验验证，平均3个模型即可将水印检测的z分数降至2以下（低于检测阈值4），真正例率在5%假阳性率下低于50%；同时生成质量提升27.5%，推理速度提升6倍，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 水印技术在多模型环境下存在根本性脆弱性，若无模型提供方的深度协同，难以实现可靠的AI生成内容检测。未来鲁棒检测需重新考虑系统级协作或接受该局限。

Abstract: Watermarking embeds statistical signatures in AI-generated text for detection and attribution. We reveal a fundamental vulnerability: when users access multiple models (today's reality), watermarks trivially fail. Watermarks perturb output distributions away from the original, and in competitive markets, these perturbations are typically independent across providers. We theoretically prove that averaging output probability distributions recovers the unwatermarked distribution with up to a second-order error term. Empirically, simply averaging 3-5 models cancels out these perturbations. We introduce WASH (Watermark Attenuation via Statistical Hybridisation), which solves practical challenges in ensemble generation: vocabulary misalignment and tokenisation differences across heterogeneous models. Experiments across six watermarking schemes and three LLMs show that averaging across 3 models suppresses detection z-scores from 5-300 to below 2 (below the detection threshold of 4) and reduces TPR at 5% FPR to below 50%, while improving quality by 27.5% and running 6 times faster than the best baseline on the long sequence generation. Our results suggest that robust AI-text detection via watermarking requires either accepting this fundamental vulnerability or unprecedented coordination among model providers.

</details>


### [102] [Auditing LLM Benchmarks with Item Response Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30504)
*Sander Land,Daniel M. Bikel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于项目反应理论的指标，可在七个偏好和多项选择基准中以95%精度识别出前200个可能错误标注的样本，优于监督分类器。错误来源包括机械标注启发式、上游数据集中的注释错误以及本质上模糊且无明确单一标签的题目。模型拟合结果还显示，奖励模型更擅长风格偏好而非事实知识，并发现一个前沿奖励模型在78%的情况下与检测到的错误标注一致，而其他模型仅为38%，表明存在基准污染或针对特定基准的过度优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM基准标签在发布时固定并无声传播，导致错误被持续继承；需要一种有效方法来识别潜在错误标注。

Method: 采用项目反应理论（IRT）构建指标，利用114个模型的响应数据评估标注质量，识别疑似错误标注的样本，并分析其成因。

Result: 在七个基准中以95%精度识别出前200个可疑错误标注；揭示了错误来源为机械标注、上游错误和题目本身模糊性；发现奖励模型更偏向风格偏好而非事实知识，且存在一个表现异常的前沿模型与错误标注高度一致。

Conclusion: 现有基准中的错误标签长期未被察觉，且可能影响下游评估；建议重新审视标注流程与奖励模型训练方式，防止基准污染和过拟合。

Abstract: LLM benchmark labels are frozen at release and silently propagated into downstream benchmarks, errors and all. We introduce an Item Response Theory-based indicator that surfaces likely mislabels at 95% precision in the top 200 examples across seven preference and multiple-choice benchmarks using responses from 114 models, outperforming a supervised classifier. We trace these errors to mechanical labeling heuristics, upstream annotation mistakes inherited unchanged from source datasets, and fundamentally ambiguous items without a defensible single label. The same model fit reveals that reward models specialize in stylistic preference rather than factual knowledge, and identifies one frontier reward model that agrees with detected mislabels at 78% accuracy versus 38% for its peers, consistent with benchmark contamination or benchmark-specific over-optimization.

</details>


### [103] [Generalistic or Specific Embeddings, Which is Better? An Empirical Study on Search for Clinical Coding in Non-English Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30529)
*David Rey-Blanco,Roberto Cruz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究如何利用大型生成式语言模型作为数据工厂，解决非英语临床检索（如ICD-10-CM代码）中嵌入模型性能下降的问题。通过在Gemini生成的多语言合成数据上微调西班牙语生物医学编码器，构建两阶段检索器（双编码器+交叉编码器重排序器），在多个语言上超越基线模型，尤其在葡萄牙语上显著提升召回率（R@5达0.829，优于BioBERT-ST的0.714）。该方法无需英语生物医学预训练即可达到优异性能，并提供可复用的领域特定检索器构建方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前句向量模型主要针对英文语料开发和评估，在非英语临床检索任务中表现下降，且传统基准难以揭示此问题。为提升多语言临床信息检索效果，亟需有效方法填补语言覆盖与数据稀缺之间的差距。

Method: 采用两阶段检索框架：首先使用基于西班牙语生物医学编码器（PlanTL-GOB-ES/bsc-bio-ehr-es）的双编码器进行初步检索；其次引入交叉编码器作为重排序器，进一步优化结果。所有模型均在由大型生成式语言模型（Gemini）生成的跨语言合成数据上进行微调，涵盖英语、西班牙语、加泰罗尼亚语、意大利语、葡萄牙语和法语。

Result: 双编码器在未使用英语生物医学预训练的情况下，达到与BioBERT-ST相当的MRR（0.876 vs. 0.866），并在R@3（0.650 vs. 0.626）和R@5（0.804 vs. 0.790）上超越后者。加入交叉编码器后，整体R@5提升至0.822，且在四种语言上实现显著增益（西班牙语+0.017，加泰罗尼亚语+0.033，法语+0.018，葡萄牙语+0.037），尽管英语略有退步，但临床可用性仍可接受。葡萄牙语的R@5达到0.829，远超基线模型的0.714。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了利用大型生成式语言模型生成合成数据，能够有效构建高性能多语言医疗检索系统。该方法不仅显著提升了非英语场景下的检索性能，还提供了开放的构建流程与量化学习增益分析，为跨语言临床信息检索提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Sentence-embedding models for semantic search are overwhelmingly developed and evaluated on English corpora. When applied to clinical retrieval in other languages -- particularly retrieval of ICD-10-CM / CIE-10 codes -- recall degrades in ways often masked by aggregate benchmarks. We study whether large generative language models can serve as data factories to close this gap. We build a two-stage retriever (bi-encoder followed by cross-encoder reranker), fine-tuned from a Spanish biomedical encoder (PlanTL-GOB-ES/bsc-bio-ehr-es) on Gemini-generated synthetic data covering English, Spanish, Catalan, Italian, Portuguese and French, and evaluate against BioBERT-ST and the un-tuned Spanish encoder. The bi-encoder alone matches BioBERT-ST on MRR (0.876 vs. 0.866) and overtakes it on R@3 (0.650 vs. 0.626) and R@5 (0.804 vs. 0.790) without English biomedical pretraining. Adding a cross-encoder reranker lifts aggregate R@5 to 0.822 and dominates on four of five languages (+0.017 Spanish, +0.033 Catalan, +0.018 French, +0.037 Portuguese) at the cost of a small English regression. The trade-off is clinically acceptable: Portuguese reaches R@5 = 0.829 vs. BioBERT-ST's 0.714. Contributions: an open recipe for building domain-specific medical retrievers from LLM-generated data; quantification of the learning gain (MRR 0.755 to 0.876, +15.9% with ~19,500 synthetic pairs); and a characterisation of where gains concentrate by language and rank.

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [105] [Probing the Prompt KV Cache: Where It Becomes Dispensable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30574)
*Vinayshekhar Bannihatti Kumar,Manoj Ghuhan Arivazhagan,Disha Makhija,Rashmi Gangadharaiah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究发现，在解码过程中，提示缓存（prompt cache）的上层在形式上存在冗余，主要表现为聊天模板的结构框架而非内容本身。通过用中性填充内容的聊天模板骨架替换上层提示缓存，可几乎完全恢复原始准确率，而直接清空相同位置则导致性能崩溃。这一现象在Qwen3、Gemma 3和Llama 3等多个模型家族及数据集上均一致复现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV缓存压缩方法表明提示缓存部分冗余，但其冗余的机制与时机尚不明确。本研究旨在揭示这种冗余的本质：是内容上的重复，还是形式上的结构冗余？

Method: 采用受控的拼接干预实验，系统地扫描不同层的截断位置和解码步骤，观察缓存替换对模型性能的影响。通过替换为带有中性填充内容的聊天模板骨架，评估其对推理准确性的影响。

Result: 实验表明，提示缓存的冗余主要体现在形式（如聊天模板的结构框架）而非内容。使用中性填充的模板骨架替换上层缓存可实现接近原始性能的准确率，而清空相同位置则导致性能严重下降。该现象在多个主流大模型系列中具有高度一致性。

Conclusion: 提示缓存的冗余本质上是形式性的，源于聊天模板的结构性特征。这为高效、安全的KV缓存压缩提供了新思路：可通过保留结构框架并替换具体内容来实现压缩，而不影响模型推理质量。

Abstract: Prior KV cache compression schemes empirically demonstrate that the prompt cache is partially redundant during decoding, dropping or summarising entries with little accuracy loss. We ask when and what kind of redundancy: at which layers, after how many decoding steps, and in what form can the prompt span KV cache be replaced without breaking the task. A controlled splice intervention swept over layer cutoff and decoding steps shows this redundancy is about form (chat template scaffolding) rather than content. Replacing the upper layer prompt span KV cache with KV cache from a chat template scaffold whose user content is a neutral filler recovers near clean accuracy, while zeroing the same slots collapses accuracy. The dissociation replicates across the Qwen3, Gemma 3, and Llama 3 families on multiple datasets.

Result: 任务特定蒸馏显著提升效率，但泛化性差；n-gram草稿模型接受率较低，但因生成极快，在所有语言中均实现显著速度提升。

Conclusion: 尽管任务特定蒸馏有效，但n-gram草稿模型在多语言场景下更具实用价值，因其速度快且具有良好的跨任务泛化能力。

Abstract: Speculative decoding has become a crucial component of large language model (LLM) inference, enabling faster generation by drafting multiple tokens and verifying them in parallel. However, small draft models tend to suffer from disproportionately poor multilingual capabilities. Thus, when generating text in a non-English language, speculative decoding is far less effective.

We evaluate efficiency on translation (from English into the target language) and the held-out task of story generation. We find that while task-specific distillation can significantly improve efficiency, distilled models generalize poorly to a new task. Meanwhile, n-gram draft models, despite lower acceptance rates, consistently provide large speed-ups due to much faster draft generation.

### [108] [Semantic Motion Anchors: Bridging Motion and Meaning in Co-Speech Gestures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30608)
*Varsha Suresh,Mohammad Mahdi Abootorabi,Mohamed Salman,M. Hamza Mughal,Christian Theobalt,Ashwin Ram,Jürgen Steimle,Vera Demberg*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语音-手势联合表示学习难以捕捉语义手势的深层交际意图，直接对比文本与连续动作嵌入容易偏向低级运动特征而忽略符号内容。

Method: 将3D手势分解为身体-手部运动基元，将其转化为自然语言描述，并与文本对齐以提供语义化的对比监督信号。

Abstract: Learning a shared representation between spoken text and gesture is central to co-speech gesture retrieval, synthesis, and understanding, but remains challenging for semantically meaningful gestures whose communicative intent is not captured by motion alone. Direct contrastive alignment between transcripts and continuous motion embeddings often overemphasizes low-level kinematics and misses the symbolic content of semantic gestures. We propose semantic motion anchors, natural-language abstractions of gesture motion capturing physical form and communicative intent. Our method discretizes 3D gestures into body-hand motion primitives, verbalizes them into structured descriptions, and grounds them in the transcript to provide auxiliary contrastive supervision. On BEAT2, our method improves text-to-gesture R@1 by 8.2% over a direct text-motion baseline and outperforms prior retrieval approaches on text to gesture and gesture to text retrieval directions. Beyond aggregate retrieval metrics, semantic motion anchor supervision helps retrieve gestures that are semantically meaningful for the spoken query, rather than defaulting to generic motion patterns. A downstream retrieval-augmented gesture generation study showed that users significantly preferred gestures retrieved by our approach over a retrieval-augmented generation baseline, demonstrating that semantically grounded retrieval translates to gestures that better convey communicative intent in downstream generation.

### [109] [The Architecture of Errors: From Universal Impossibility to Patch-Local LLM Reliability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30628)
*Mikhail L. Arbuzov,Lee Mosbacker,Sisong Bei,Ziwei Dong,Dmitri Kalaev,Alexey Shvets*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文指出，通用大模型的可靠性问题并非有限干预词典所能解决，因为潜在故障模式在理论上无限。但在实际部署中，系统运行于操作边界明确的特定场景（如医疗RAG、代码修复等），这些场景内故障模式稀疏、重复且集中，因此可靠性问题可转化为局部故障模式发现与干预覆盖问题。作者提出三个核心结论：1）在无界领域中，任何有限干预词典都无法覆盖所有可能故障模式；2）模式发现能力受限于观测到的硬失败事件数量，尾部新模式难以捕捉；3）在特定操作域内，只要暴露足够多的常见故障模式，所需干预预算随序列长度仅多项式对数增长，一旦模式库饱和，成本趋于恒定。该框架将长上下文挑战从“不可解”转为“可干预”，强调识别关键干预点的重要性而非消除复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型在面对无限任务、工具、知识源和评估期望时，无法保证可靠性，因为故障模式可能无限扩展。然而真实系统只在特定操作范围内运行，其故障具有重复性和集中性，因此应从‘全局覆盖’转向‘局部模式发现’。

Method: 通过形式化两个命题与一个推论，构建理论框架：命题1证明无界领域中有限干预无法覆盖所有故障模式；推论1揭示模式发现能力受观测数据限制；命题2提出在局部操作域中，通过充分暴露头部故障模式，干预预算可控制在低阶增长水平。

Result: 在操作边界明确的场景下，可靠性问题可转化为可管理的局部模式发现与干预覆盖问题。干预成本随序列长度仅呈多项式对数增长，一旦模式库饱和，成本趋于常数。

Conclusion: 大模型的可靠性不应被看作全局性的无限难题，而应视为在具体应用域内的局部模式发现与干预优化问题。通过聚焦高频、可重复的故障模式，可在不解决所有潜在错误的前提下实现高可靠性，从而将长上下文挑战从‘不可控’转变为‘可干预’。

Abstract: Universal LLM reliability is not a finite-library problem: across all possible tasks, tools, schemas, knowledge sources, and evaluator expectations, new intervention-distinguishable failure modes can appear without bound, so no finite intervention dictionary can guarantee bounded residual error for every such mode. But deployed systems do not operate over the whole universe. They operate inside operationally bounded patches (legal review, medical RAG, code repair, customer-support agents, contract extraction) with recurring tasks, schemas, tools, and evaluator expectations. Within such patches, empirical evidence suggests failures are sparse, repetitive, and concentrated in a small recurring catalogue, so reliability becomes a local catalogue-discovery and intervention-coverage problem rather than an exponential token-length problem. We formalize this transition with two propositions and one corollary. Proposition 1 is the worst-case-mode-wise negative result: no finite intervention dictionary covers every distinguishable failure mode of an unbounded domain. Corollary 1 is the inverse-discovery implication: the logarithmic upper bound on mode discovery cannot accommodate linearly more distinct tail modes without exponentially more observed hard-failure events. Proposition 2 is the positive patch-local result: under log active-mode exposure and head-heavy coverage, a sufficient per-hard-decision intervention budget grows polylogarithmically in sequence length and becomes domain-constant once the patch catalogue saturates. The framework relocates rather than dissolves long-context difficulty: where the number of hard decisions itself grows with task length, reliability remains hard; the contribution is to identify the on-axis intervention rather than to make those regimes easy.

</details>


### [110] [COFT: Counterfactual-Conformal Decoding for Fair Chain-of-Thought Reasoning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30641)
*Arya Fayyazi,Mehdi Kamal,Massoud Pedram*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: COFT是一种无需训练的解码方法，通过在生成过程中对敏感信息进行去偏处理，在不改变模型权重的前提下显著降低大语言模型在链式思维推理中的社会偏见。该方法通过构建掩码反事实提示、轻量级对数融合对比真实与反事实分布，并使用双分支分裂-共形校准技术，在用户设定的风险水平下对每一步候选词集进行认证。实验表明，该方法在多个模型和基准测试中将标准偏见指标降低了30-55%（中位数38%），同时保持任务性能和语言质量不变，计算开销仅相当于一次额外的前向传播（≤11%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在链式思维生成过程中可能暴露并放大社会偏见，现有方法通常需要重新训练或引入辅助分类器，缺乏可解释性和灵活性。因此，亟需一种无需训练、可审计且能保证公平性的实时解码策略。

Method: COFT分为三个阶段：(1) 使用中性标记替换敏感片段生成掩码反事实提示；(2) 通过轻量级对数融合比较真实与反事实的输出分布，抑制属性驱动的偏见；(3) 利用双分支分裂-共形校准技术，在用户指定风险水平下对每个解码步骤的候选词集进行形式化验证。

Result: 在六种不同模型和多个偏见评估基准上的实验显示，COFT使标准偏见指标平均下降38%（范围30%-55%），推理准确率在运行间噪声范围内保持不变，语言质量不受影响，计算开销极低（≤11%额外前向传播）。

Conclusion: COFT提供了一种无需重训练、无需访问模型权重、无需辅助分类器的可审计公平推理解码方案，有效降低链式思维中的偏见，同时几乎不损失任务性能，为安全、可信的AI推理提供了实用路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can reveal and amplify societal biases during chain-of-thought (CoT) generation. We present COFT (Chain of Fair Thought), a training-free decoding method that applies token-level fairness control at decode time, with distribution-free marginal validity guarantees (under exchangeability) for any frozen causal language model. COFT operates in three stages. First, it creates a masked counterfactual prompt by replacing sensitive spans with neutral tokens. Second, it compares the factual and masked logit distributions through lightweight logit fusion to attenuate attribute-driven biases. Third, it uses dual-branch split-conformal calibration to certify per-step candidate token sets at a user-chosen risk level. We evaluate COFT across six models and multiple bias benchmarks. Our method reduces standard bias metrics by 30-55% (median 38%) while preserving task utility and language quality. Reasoning accuracies remain unchanged within run-to-run noise margins. The computational overhead is modest, equivalent to one additional cached forward pass (<=11%). COFT offers a clear, auditable path to safer CoT generation with significant bias reduction, negligible utility loss, and no requirement for retraining, auxiliary classifiers, or weight access.

</details>


### [111] [Same Patient, Different Words, Different Diagnosis? Evaluating Semantic Stability in Clinical LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30646)
*Mahdi Alkaeed,Adnan Qayyum,Nabeel Abo Kashreef,Muhammad Bilal,Junaid Qadir*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于自然语言推理（NLI）的语义验证框架，用于筛选语义保持的提示变体，并通过大模型作为裁判和临床专家审核进行优化。引入三种新指标（MVS、ΔC、WCI）量化模型对语义不变提示变化的敏感性。在DiagnosisQA和MedQA数据集上评估16个开源通用与医疗领域大模型，发现领域专用模型的鲁棒性表现不一，领域专化并不总是提升或降低对语义保持提示变化的鲁棒性，部分专用模型表现优异，但强通用基线也具有竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在临床应用中对细微语言变化高度敏感，可能导致相同临床含义的输入产生不同输出，存在安全风险。现有基于嵌入的相似性度量无法准确捕捉否定、时间性、严重程度等关键语义差异，亟需更可靠的语义一致性验证方法。

Method: 提出基于自然语言推理（NLI）的语义验证框架，筛选语义保持的提示变体；结合大模型作为裁判与临床专家进行双重验证；设计三类指标（MVS、ΔC、WCI）评估模型敏感性。

Result: 评估结果显示，领域专用模型的鲁棒性表现不一致，受模型本身影响显著；部分专用模型表现优于通用模型，但一些通用基线模型同样表现出高鲁棒性，表明领域专化并非提升鲁棒性的充分条件。

Conclusion: 语义保持的提示变体筛选依赖于有效的语义验证机制；模型鲁棒性取决于具体模型设计，领域专化不能保证更高稳定性；应结合多维度评估与人工审核以确保临床应用中的可靠性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in clinical applications. However, their behavior remains highly sensitive to subtle linguistic variations, such as rephrasing or syntactic variation. This sensitivity poses risks in safety-critical healthcare settings, where semantically equivalent inputs should produce consistent predictions. However, a key challenge is to ensure that prompt variations truly preserve clinical meaning, as embedding-based similarity metrics often fail to capture distinctions involving negation, temporality, or severity. To address this limitation, we propose a semantic verification framework based on Natural Language Inference (NLI) to filter meaning-preserving prompt variations, which are further refined using an LLM-as-a-judge and audited by a clinical expert. In addition, we introduce three metrics to quantify model sensitivity: MeaningPreserving Variation Sensitivity (MVS), confidence variation (ΔC), and Worst-Case Instability (WCI). We evaluate 16 open-source general-purpose (GP) and medical LLMs within the same model families and parameter scales, using reformulated prompts derived from the DiagnosisQA and MedQA datasets. Our results demonstrate that robustness differences between domain-specific (DS) models are mixed and highly model-dependent, i.e., domain specialization does not consistently improve or reduce robustness to meaning-preserving prompt reformulations. Several DS models rank among the most robust (when compared with GP counterparts), and strong GP baselines remain competitive as well.

### [112] [Counterfactual Graph for Multi-Agent LLM Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30653)
*Jiatan Huang,Mingchen Li,Ziming Li,Sunjae Kwon,Hong Yu,Chuxu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CAGE-CAL is a counterfactual calibration framework for multi-agent LLM systems that addresses the issue of false consensus caused by agent communication. It compares observed post-communication agent graphs with counterfactual no-communication graphs to detect correlated failures and adjust confidence scores accordingly, improving reliability and topology selection.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing multi-agent LLM systems assume that agreement among agents indicates reliability, but communication can lead to correlated failures and false consensus, undermining this assumption. The motivation is to develop a method that accurately calibrates confidence by accounting for such dependencies.

Method: CAGE-CAL constructs a counterfactual no-communication graph for each query and compares it with the observed post-communication graph. It measures the shift in dependence patterns between the two, capturing both pairwise and group-level failure correlations, and uses this to recalibrate agent confidence.

Result: On five benchmarks, CAGE-CAL improves reliability discrimination while maintaining competitive ECE. It also enhances topology selection performance beyond the best fixed-topology strategy.

Conclusion: CAGE-CAL effectively mitigates the risks of false consensus in multi-agent LLMs by modeling communication-induced dependencies through counterfactual calibration, leading to more reliable and robust decision-making.

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems often treat agreement as evidence: when many agents in a panel give the same answer, that answer is assumed to be more reliable. We show that this assumption can fail after agents communicate. Communication can induce correlated failures and false consensus, so the same vote share may reflect reliable agreement in one topology but over-confidence in another. We propose CAGE-CAL, a counterfactual agent-graph calibration framework for multi-agent LLMs. For each query, CAGE-CAL compares an observed post-communication agent graph with a matched counterfactual no-communication graph, capturing both pairwise failure correlations and group-level dependencies. Rather than simply counting how many agents agree, CAGE-CAL estimates the counterfactual shift between observed and no-communication dependence, and calibrates confidence accordingly. Across five benchmarks, CAGE-CAL improves reliability discrimination with competitive ECE, and its calibrated confidence further improves topology selection over the best fixed-topology strategy.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used as conversational partners for companionship, emotional disclosure, and interpersonal advice, but the social dynamics of these interactions can create harms that are not captured by capability-oriented or traditional safety evaluations. We introduce the Social AI Design Code, a framework for evaluating whether LLMs align with user welfare in social interactions, including whether they encourage harmful intimacy, dependence, or prolonged engagement. To evaluate these risks in natural and diverse user-LLM interactions, we operationalize the code with EUDAIMONIA, a benchmark of 969 user inputs and 3,147 design-requirement violation checks built from WildChat through weak-to-strong filtration, multi-model relabeling, and controlled rewriting. Evaluating 22 recent LLMs, we find that even the strongest models, Claude-Opus-4.7 and GPT-5.5, violate 30.7% and 27.2% of checks, respectively. Method: 提出CobSeg，采用多分支结构分别处理语义连贯性和词汇边界转换；通过方向性边界预测恢复两类信号；引入边界信息权重机制以强调高价值话语位置；结合语料库导出的主题连贯性提示与学习组合权重。

Abstract: Dialogue topic segmentation is critical in many human-AI collaborative applications which requires identifying heterogeneous boundary cues, including lexical transitions near utterance edges and semantic discontinuities across utterances. Existing utterance models often dilute these local lexical signals. We propose CobSeg, a novel multi-branch architecture that separates coherence-level semantic continuity from lexical boundary transitions and recovers both through directional boundary prediction. CobSeg further uses boundary informativeness weighting to emphasize high-utility utterance positions, and incorporates a corpus-derived topic coherence cue with learned combination weights. While CobSeg is evaluated as a compact trainable segmenter under supervised gold-boundary training and a pseudo-label setting with automatically induced boundaries, it performs enhanced boundary prediction without LLM calls during inference. Across five benchmarks, it improves $P_k$ and $W_d$ particularly when local lexical cues are prominent: under gold supervision, it reduces $P_k$ by 0.7 points and $W_d$ by 0.6 points on VHF, and reaches $P_k$ of 1.0 on DialSeg711; with induced boundaries, it reduces $P_k$ by 14.8 points on VHF, by 1.5 points on DialSeg711, and by 1.1 points on TIAGE, outperforming prior non-LLM approaches.

Seven researchers annotated each scene with 39 binary observation codes, covering 20 visual codes, such as gesture, board work, pointing, and visual materials, and 19 nonvisual codes, such as instruction, monitoring, questioning, feedback, and reflection. Gold segment labels are constructed using reliability- and prevalence-aware rules based on Krippendorff's alpha. In addition to segment-level labels, three expert raters produced lesson-level ratings and qualitative evaluations of instructional design, instructional delivery, learner response, learning materials, and lesson closure across the 30 lessons, with rater coverage detailed in the body. Using these two human reference layers, we evaluate five vision-capable frontier LLMs across three tracks - text-only segment coding, text + frame segment coding, and lesson-level coverage scored under an LLM-as-judge protocol - and find that no single model consistently outperforms others across all three tracks, that adding a mid-frame inflates both true and false attributions per scene, and that model evaluations over-rate procedurally clear lessons relative to expert raters. \textit{TeachObs} therefore supports both fine-grained annotation benchmarking and whole-lesson evaluation, showing where AI systems can assist classroom video analysis and where expert judgment remains necessary across varied subjects, classroom formats, and annotation difficulty levels.

### [117] [ElasticMem: Latent Memory as a Learnable Resource for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30690)
*Tao Feng,Chongrui Ye,Tianyang Luo,Jingjun Xu,Xueqiang Xu,Haozhen Zhang,Ge Liu,Jiaxuan You*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ElasticMem 是一种新型的内存增强型大语言模型框架，通过将记忆视为可变的潜在资源，实现了更高效、灵活的记忆使用。它构建离线潜在记忆库，根据推理器隐藏状态自适应检索记忆，并通过学习策略为每个记忆分配可变的潜在预算，以软记忆标记形式注入生成过程。整个记忆使用流程通过下游任务奖励进行优化，显著提升了长期记忆任务中的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆增强方法将记忆视为固定资源，文本空间方法导致大量令牌开销和对噪声证据敏感，而潜在空间方法虽减少文本成本但依赖刚性检索或固定容量接口，造成查询依赖的记忆效用与固定内存分配之间的不匹配。

Method: ElasticMem 构建离线潜在记忆库，基于推理器隐藏状态自适应检索记忆；通过学习策略动态分配每个记忆的潜在预算；将选定的潜在状态作为软记忆令牌注入生成过程；采用组相对策略优化（group-relative policy optimization）对整个记忆使用流程进行端到端优化。

Result: 在 MemorySuite 基准上，ElasticMem 在 Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct 和 Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct 模型上分别将加权平均问答准确率提升 26.2% 和 24.6%，在 ALFWorld 任务中成功率分别提升 66.3% 和 27.2%，同时实现最低的令牌消耗。消融实验和定性分析表明，自适应检索和弹性预算分配能有效优先处理有用证据和可迁移计划。

Conclusion: ElasticMem 通过将记忆建模为弹性潜在资源，克服了传统方法中固定内存分配的局限性，在多个长期记忆任务中展现出显著性能提升，证明了其在高效、智能记忆管理方面的优势。

Abstract: Long-term memory is essential for LLM agents to reason coherently across extended interactions, personalize responses, and reuse past experience. However, existing memory-augmented methods typically treat memory as a fixed resource: text-space approaches concatenate retrieved memories into the context window, causing substantial token overhead and sensitivity to noisy evidence, while latent-space approaches reduce textual cost but still rely on rigid retrieval or fixed-capacity memory interfaces. This creates a mismatch between query-dependent memory utility and fixed memory allocation. We propose ElasticMem, a memory-augmented LLM framework that learns to use memory as an elastic latent resource. ElasticMem builds an offline latent memory bank with retrieval keys and content caches, retrieves memories adaptively from the reasoner's hidden state, assigns each retrieved memory a variable latent budget through a learned policy, and injects selected latent states as soft memory tokens for generation. The full memory-use process is optimized with downstream task rewards through group-relative policy optimization. We evaluate ElasticMem on MemorySuite, covering memory-intensive QA and embodied agent control. Across Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct and Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct backbones, ElasticMem improves weighted average QA accuracy by 26.2% and 24.6%, and improves ALFWorld success rate by 66.3% and 27.2%, respectively, over the strongest baselines, while achieving the lowest ALFWorld token cost. Ablations and qualitative analyses further show that adaptive retrieval and elastic budget allocation help ElasticMem prioritize useful evidence and transferable plans beyond rigid cosine similarity. Our code for ElasticMem will be released at https://github.com/ulab-uiuc/ElasticMem.

### [118] [Neuron-Level Interventions for Gendered and Gender-Neutral Generation in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30717)
*Zhiwen You,Nafiseh Nikeghbal,Jana Diesner*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了语言模型中性别相关神经元的编码机制，提出了一种基于神经元层面的干预方法，可精准控制生成文本的性别形式（女性、男性、中性），并验证了其在保持语义不变前提下的有效性。实验发现性别神经元主要集中在早期层，且该方法相比现有方法具有更少的性别泄露和更稳定的输出质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多聚焦于性别二元对立，对性别中立表达关注不足，且缺乏对语言模型内部如何编码性别信号的深入理解。因此需要一种能精确干预性别表达的方法，以揭示性别在模型中的表征方式并实现可控生成。

Method: 提出一种神经元级干预方法，通过识别与女性、男性及性别中立类别强相关的神经元，并在生成过程中激活或屏蔽这些神经元，实现对性别形式的精细控制；同时构建两个标注数据集用于评估干预效果。

Result: 性别相关神经元集中分布在模型早期层，后期贡献较小；所提方法在控制精度、减少非目标性别泄露、输出稳定性方面优于现有方法；人类评估验证了数据质量与干预效果。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了性别在语言模型中的神经表征特性，提出了一种有效且可解释的性别干预框架，为性别偏见缓解和可控生成提供了新路径。代码与数据已开源。

Abstract: Language models (LMs) can produce gendered language and stereotypes even when given neutral prompts. Most prior work on gender bias in LMs primarily examines gender through a binary lens (feminine vs. masculine), with limited attention to gender-neutral forms, such as they/them pronouns or neutrally phrased job titles. How gender-related signals are encoded in the internal representations of LMs remains an open question. In this work, we study gender-specific neurons in LMs across three categories: feminine, masculine, and gender-neutral. We propose a neuron-level intervention method to identify neurons that are strongly tied to each gender category. We then test these neurons through controlled generation, showing that activating or masking gender-related neurons can steer a sentence toward a target gender form while preserving its original meaning. To evaluate the effectiveness of our gender-intervention approach, we curate two datasets with controlled sentences labeled across all three gender categories and validate the data quality through human evaluation. Experiments on two open-source LMs show that gender-specific neurons are not evenly distributed across model layers; instead, they concentrate heavily in the earliest layers with smaller contributions from later layers. Compared to existing methods, our method achieves more precise gender control, with less leakage into non-target gender categories and stable output quality through two evaluation criteria. Overall, our work examines how gender is encoded in LMs and provides a simple yet effective approach toward controlled gender intervention for both neuron intervention evaluation and gender bias mitigation. Code and datasets are available at: https://github.com/zhiwenyou103/Gender-Neuron-Intervention

### [119] [Skill is Not One-Size-Fits-All: Model-Aware Skill Alignment for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30723)
*Jianxiang Yu,Jiapeng Zhu,Bochen Lin,Qier Cui,Zichen Ding,Xiang Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MASA提出一种模型感知的技能对齐框架，通过两阶段方法适应不同大模型骨干的特性：首先利用进化算法和树搜索优化技能，其次训练轻量级重写器实现快速适配。实验表明，MASA在多个环境和模型上显著提升性能，最高比基线提升25.8分，并在未见任务中保持优越表现，推理成本远低于大型教师模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能库通常被当作与模型无关，但实验发现技能效果强烈依赖于具体模型；同一技能可能对某些模型有益，对另一些则有害，因此需要根据目标模型特性动态调整技能。

Method: MASA包含两个阶段：(1) 分层技能演化管道，使用爬山法和基于UCB的树搜索，结合环境反馈与模型能力分析迭代优化通用与特定任务技能；(2) 轻量级模型条件技能重写器，基于演化轨迹训练，可在一次前向传播中复现适配过程。

Result: 在三个交互环境和四个模型骨干上的实验显示，MASA consistently achieves最佳性能，最大提升达25.8点；所学重写器可泛化至未见任务与环境，且推理效率远高于大型教师模型。

Conclusion: MASA有效解决了技能在不同模型间迁移中的不一致性问题，通过模型感知的技能对齐显著提升智能体表现，同时具备高效、可扩展和强泛化能力。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly retrieve externally curated skills-procedural instructions retrieved at decision time-to improve performance on long-horizon interactive tasks. Existing skill libraries are typically treated as model-agnostic, reusing the same skill formulations across backbones with substantially different capacities and behaviors. However, our controlled experiments across multiple model scales show that skill effectiveness is strongly model-dependent: a skill that benefits one backbone can harm another. Motivated by this observation, we propose MASA Model-Aware Skill Alignment, a framework that adapts skills to each target backbone without modifying agent weights. MASA operates in two stages: (1) a hierarchical skill evolution pipeline that iteratively rewrites general and task-specific skills using hill climbing and UCB-driven tree search, guided by environment feedback and model capability profiles; and (2) a lightweight model-conditioned skill rewriter trained on evolution trajectories to reproduce the adaptation in a single forward pass. Experiments across three interactive environments and four backbones show that MASA consistently achieves the best overall performance, with gains of up to 25.8 points over the strongest baseline. The learned rewriter further generalizes to unseen tasks and environments without additional search, consistently outperforming a much larger teacher LLM at a fraction of the inference cost.

### [120] [Efficient Diffusion LLMs via Temporal-Spatial Parallel Decoding and Confidence Extrapolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30753)
*Zekai Li,Ji Liu,Yiqing Huang,Ziqiong Liu,Dong Li,Emad Barsoum*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于轨迹感知的扩散解码框架，通过分析每个令牌的去噪轨迹，实现动态控制以减少冗余迭代。引入时间-空间并行解码（TSPD）和置信度外推（CE）两个组件，前者利用轨迹特征判断令牌是否收敛，后者无需训练即可预测未来逻辑趋势，支持前瞻决策和稳定化处理。整体方法显著降低推理延迟，同时保持输出质量，并兼容如KV缓存等系统优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统扩散语言模型在解码时存在大量冗余去噪和重复掩码操作，导致推理延迟高；现有加速方法依赖局部置信度或固定调度，对提示和任务变化敏感，且忽略序列中强位置效应。因此需要更鲁棒、自适应的加速机制。

Method: 将扩散解码建模为动态控制问题，利用令牌级去噪轨迹作为关键信号。设计了两个核心组件：1）时间-空间并行解码（TSPD），通过轻量级时空控制器结合置信度、熵、动量及位置信息，判断令牌是否收敛并可固定；2）置信度外推（CE），一个无训练的状态空间模块，用于预测未来逻辑趋势与不确定性，支持安全前瞻和针对振荡或低置信情况的定向稳定。

Result: 所提方法有效减少了不必要的去噪迭代，在保持生成质量的前提下显著降低了推理延迟；实验表明其对不同提示和任务具有较强鲁棒性，且可无缝集成到现有系统优化（如KV缓存）中。

Conclusion: 通过轨迹感知的动态控制策略，TSPD与CE共同实现了高效、自适应的扩散解码，为大语言模型的快速生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Diffusion-based large language models (dLLMs) support parallel text generation via iterative denoising, yet inference remains latency-heavy because many steps are spent on redundant refinement and repeated remasking of tokens whose final values are already determined. Prior acceleration methods mainly depend on step-local confidence heuristics or fixed schedules, which are sensitive to prompt and task variation and ignore strong positional effects within a sequence. We cast diffusion decoding as a dynamic control problem and show that token-wise denoising trajectories provide the key signal for reliable control. We propose a trace-aware decoding framework with two components. First, Temporal-Spatial Parallel Decoding (TSPD) uses a lightweight temporalspatial controller that consumes per-token trajectory features, including confidence, entropy, and momentum, together with token position, to decide when a token has converged and can be safely fixed. Second, we introduce Confidence Extrapolation (CE), a training-free state-space module that forecasts future logit trends with uncertainty to support proactive decisions, including safe look-ahead and targeted stabilization when trajectories are oscillatory or underconfident. Together, TSPD and CE reduce unnecessary denoising iterations while preserving output quality, and they compose cleanly with system optimizations such as KV caching.

</details>


### [121] [Pairwise Reference Alignment as a Model-Level Ordinal Observable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30758)
*Mujing Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个关于成对偏好数据中模型对齐性的基本测量问题，定义了基于参考偏好分布的成对参考对齐（pairwise reference alignment）这一序数可观测量，并通过模型得分函数来衡量模型排序与参考偏好一致的概率。文章引入了一个中心化的类似序参数的统计量及基于边距的扩展形式，给出了简单有限样本估计器和独立采样下的集中界。研究强调了参考配对分布的作用，区分了通用序数可观测量与具体评分方式（如归一化对数概率或能量型分数）之间的差异，并在Qwen2.5模型和RewardBench数据集上进行了初步实证分析，结果表明所提统计量随模型规模和指令微调增强而上升，且在不同参考对子集间存在预期变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前语言模型评估与对齐广泛使用成对偏好数据，但缺乏对这些数据背后核心测量机制的清晰理解。特别是，当测试模型是否将优选响应排在拒斥响应之上时，实际上是在估计何种模型层面的量？该问题缺乏统一的概念框架和统计基础。因此，本文旨在建立一个更基础、更严谨的理论框架，以明确成对偏好数据所反映的可测性本质。

Method: 提出并形式化定义了‘成对参考对齐’这一序数可观测量，基于参考配对分布 $P_{\mathrm{pair}}$ 与模型得分函数 $S_M(x,y)$，计算模型排序与参考偏好一致的概率；进一步构造中心化序参数统计量，并发展边距扩展版本；所有量均可通过简单估计器实现，且在独立采样假设下具备集中不等式性质。

Result: 所提出的对齐度量在多个参考对子集上表现出与模型大小和指令微调程度正相关的趋势；在不同参考对分布下具有可预测的变化模式；验证了理论框架的有效性和实用性。

Conclusion: 本文为成对偏好评估提供了一个概念清晰、统计稳健的测量框架，澄清了参考分布的关键作用，并强调了模型得分选择对结果的影响。它不依赖特定基准，而是为理解现有方法提供了新视角，有助于未来设计更可靠的模型评价体系。

Abstract: Pairwise preference data is widely used in language-model evaluation and alignment, often for model ranking, reward modeling, or preference optimization. This note formulates a more basic measurement question: given a reference distribution of pairwise preferences, what model-level quantity is estimated when we test whether a model ranks preferred responses above rejected responses?
  We define pairwise reference alignment as an ordinal observable induced by a model scoring function. Given a reference pair distribution $P_{\mathrm{pair}}$ over triples $(x,y^+,y^-)$, and a scalar model score $S_M(x,y)$, we define the alignment observable as the probability that the model-induced ordering agrees with the reference preference ordering. We further define a centered order-parameter-like statistic and discuss a margin-based extension. The resulting quantities admit simple finite-sample estimators and concentration bounds under independent sampling assumptions.
  This note does not introduce a new benchmark. It provides a conceptual and statistical formulation for pairwise reference alignment, clarifies the role of the reference pair distribution, and distinguishes the general ordinal observable from scoring choices such as normalized log-probability or energy-based scores. We also provide an initial empirical study on Qwen2.5 models and RewardBench, where the proposed statistics increase with model size and instruction tuning and vary across reference-pair subsets as predicted by the formulation.

Because our benchmark focuses on algorithmic tasks, differential performance is a sufficient -- but not necessary -- indicator of cross-lingual gaps. ### [123] [Anchoring LLM Gender Bias to Human Baselines: A Cross-Lingual Audit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30804)
*Jiwoo Choi,Seonwoo Ahn,Tongxin Zhang,Seohyon Jung*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究审计了六种大语言模型（LLMs）在英语、韩语、中文和日语中的性别刻板印象，发现其刻板印象范围是人类跨国家差异的2.5倍，且在多语言间可能叠加。即使在提示已录用候选人的情况下，一个以英语为主的模型在韩语提示下仍表现出本地基线5倍的刻板印象。研究提出四类行为模式（一致、抑制、重组、放大），并揭示翻译不仅缩放刻板印象，还改变其关联属性，表面看似校准实则深层重构。结论指出，单一去偏方案难以跨语言有效应对偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估大语言模型在多语言环境中性别刻板印象的程度及其跨语言传播机制，超越简单判断模型是否偏见，关注其与目标人群文化基准的偏离程度。

Method: 采用HEXACO-100人格量表，以覆盖48个国家的跨文化人类数据集为锚点，对六个模型（三个英语主导，三个东亚主导）进行多语言测试，构建四模式框架分析不同模型-语言组合下的行为特征，并进行项目级细粒度分析。

Result: 模型的性别刻板印象范围远超人类跨国家差异（约2.5倍），且在多语言交互中可被放大；特定情况下（如英文模型用韩语提示）刻板印象可达本地基线5倍；翻译过程不仅缩放，更重构属性关联，隐藏深层偏差。

Conclusion: 单一去偏策略难以在不同语言间均衡生效，需针对语言特性设计差异化干预机制。

Abstract: We audit six large language models (LLMs) for gender stereotyping across English, Korean, Chinese, and Japanese. Three were developed primarily for English-language use (Claude, GPT, Gemini) and three for East Asian use (DeepSeek, Syn-Pro, HyperCLOVA X). We adopt the HEXACO-100 personality inventory and anchor each model against a cross-cultural human dataset spanning 48 countries to ask not whether LLMs are biased, but how far their gender attributions drift from the populations they are deployed among. Our findings show that their stereotyping spans a range roughly 2.5 times wider than the entire cross-country range found in humans, and the effect can compound across languages. One English-centric model, prompted in Korean, reached 5 times the local baseline, even when the prompt stated the candidate had already been hired, which often dampens human stereotyping. To characterize such behaviors without ranking them, we introduce a four-pattern framework -- concordance, suppression, reorganization, and amplification -- across 24 (model x language) cells. Item-level analysis reveals that translation does not just rescale stereotypes, but changes the attributes tied to it, hiding significant rearrangement under the surface while appearing well-calibrated. Our results ultimately suggest that no single debiasing pipeline is likely to address bias evenly across linguistic boundaries.

### [124] [Incremental BPE Tokenization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30813)
*Shenghu Jiang,Ruihao Gong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出一种新型增量式Byte Pair Encoding (BPE)分词算法，能在最坏情况下以$\mathcal{O}(\log^2 t)$时间处理每个字节，总体复杂度为$\mathcal{O}(n \log^2 t)$，支持流式输入下的高效部分分词。该算法作为标准BPE的即插即用替代方案，相比Hugging Face tokenizers提速约3倍，显著降低OpenAI tiktoken在极端输入下的延迟。还引入了“主动输出”机制，可在分词过程中尽早输出结果，适用于实时系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有BPE分词方法在流式处理和部分输入场景下效率低下，缺乏良好的最坏情况时间保证，难以满足现代大语言模型对低延迟、高吞吐的需求。

Method: 设计了一种增量式BPE分词算法，通过维护输入前缀的分词状态，基于固定合并规则逐步构建分词结果；结合数据结构优化，实现每个字节处理的$\mathcal{O}(\log^2 t)$复杂度；引入主动输出策略，使分词边界一旦确定即可立即输出，提升响应速度。

Result: 实验表明，该算法在标准BPE任务中可实现高达3倍的速度提升，尤其在长文本或不规则输入下表现优异，显著降低延迟，具备强理论复杂度保障和实际性能优势。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了BPE分词可以实现高效且具有强最坏情况复杂度保证的增量处理，同时在真实系统中展现出显著的延迟降低与性能提升，适用于现代大语言模型的流式推理与部署场景。

Abstract: We propose a novel algorithm for incremental Byte Pair Encoding (BPE) tokenization. The algorithm processes each input byte in worst-case $\mathcal{O}(\log^2 t)$ time, leading to an overall complexity of $\mathcal{O}(n \log^2 t)$, where $n$ is the input length and $t$ is the maximum token length. The algorithm incrementally maintains BPE tokenization results for every prefix of the input text, implementing the standard BPE merge procedure defined by a fixed set of merge rules. This enables efficient partial tokenization in streaming settings. Functioning as a drop-in replacement for standard BPE, our approach achieves a speedup of up to ${\sim}3\times$ over Hugging Face's tokenizers, and demonstrates significant latency reductions over OpenAI's tiktoken on pathological inputs. We further introduce an eager output algorithm that enables streaming output, emitting tokens as soon as token boundaries are determined during incremental tokenization. Overall, our results demonstrate that BPE tokenization can be performed incrementally with strong worst-case guarantees, while providing practical latency benefits in modern large language model pipelines. Code: https://github.com/ModelTC/mtc-inc-bpe

### [125] [Beyond Agreement: Scoring Panel-Surfaced Biomedical Entity Candidates for Curator Triage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30826)
*Shuheng Cao,Ruiqi Chen,Renjie Cao,Zhenhao Zhang,Siyu Zhang,Tingting Dan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于多大模型协同的候选实体验证基准（BioConCal），通过整合八种大模型在五个公开生物医学命名实体识别数据集上的预测，构建候选主表。该方法利用无金标依赖的实时一致性、提及表面可用性及文档特征等信号，在领域内显著提升性能：AUROC从0.753升至0.910；在0.95精度目标下可筛选出1,340个候选实体，实际测试精度达0.939，远超原始一致性的293个。其核心优势在于将噪声丰富的多模型输出转化为高价值人工审查队列，而非单纯恢复漏检实体。但实体类型漂移时需目标域验证，精确字符定位仍需独立后处理步骤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统生物医学命名实体识别中，尽管大模型能轻易识别出看似合理的实体，但其结果是否符合标注规范（如边界、粒度、类型体系）难以保证。现有方法依赖多模型一致性作为可信信号，但这种一致性并不等于标注规范正确性。因此亟需一种更精细的评估与筛选机制，以提升候选实体的准确性与可用性，尤其服务于人工审核流程。

Method: 提出候选级面板输出基准，将多个大模型的预测对齐为统一候选主表；引入生物医学专用监督评分器BioConCal，结合推理时无金标的一致性、提及表面可用性、文档上下文等特征，对固定候选流进行排序与筛选。

Result: 在域内场景下，BioConCal使AUROC从0.753提升至0.910；在设定0.95精度目标下，可选出1,340个候选，实测精度为0.939，召回率分别为候选级0.592和语料级0.523（天花板为0.883）。表明该方法有效提升候选质量，形成高产出的人工审查队列。

Conclusion: 多模型一致性仅是显著性信号，并非标注正确性的保证。本研究通过构建面板级候选验证框架与领域专用评分器，成功将噪声模型输出转化为高价值可审查候选集，显著提升实用效率。然而，面对类型迁移需重新校准阈值，精确位置仍需额外后处理。

Abstract: Biomedical NER is deceptively simple for modern LLMs: plausible biomedical mentions are easy to surface, but corpus-convention correctness depends on annotation conventions, span boundaries, entity granularity, and type schemas. Multi-LLM agreement is a salience signal, not corpus-convention correctness. We introduce a candidate-level panel-output benchmark for panel-surfaced candidate verification, where the unit is an aligned candidate surfaced by an explicitly defined multi-model panel rather than a standalone extractor output. The benchmark aligns eight LLMs' predictions over five public biomedical NER datasets into a candidate master table. BioConCal is an in-domain supervised scorer that instantiates this layer with inference-time gold-free agreement, mention, surface-availability, and document features for a fixed candidate stream. In domain, BioConCal improves AUROC from 0.753 for raw agreement to 0.910. At a validation-selected 0.95 precision target it selects 1,340 candidates at empirical test precision 0.939, compared with 293 for raw agreement. This corresponds to candidate-level recall 0.592 and corpus-level recall 0.523 against a within-panel row-label ceiling of 0.883. The main benefit is not recovering entities missed by every panel member, but reshaping a noisy panel stream into a higher-yield review queue. Under entity-type shift, thresholds require target-domain validation, and exact character localization remains a separate deterministic post-processing step.

</details>


### [126] [Your Teacher Can't Help You Here: Combating Supervision Fidelity Decay in On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30833)
*Yanjiang Liu,Jie Lou,Xinyan Guan,Yuqiu Ji,Hongyu Lin,Ben He,Xianpei Han,Le Sun,Xing Yu,Yaojie Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Lookahead Group Reward（\ours{}）的新方法，以解决on-policy distillation中的监督保真度衰减（SFD）问题。该方法通过评估学生模型候选词在下一步的教师置信度来分配组归一化奖励，从而增强长推理链中的监督信号。同时设计了熵触发的树注意力机制以保持计算效率。在六个数学和代码基准测试中，\ours{}显著提升了学生模型的表现，尤其在长序列生成任务上表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: on-policy distillation存在监督保真度衰减（SFD）问题，即随着学生生成序列变长，教师对下一个词的分布变得不自信且缺乏区分度，导致反KL蒸馏中的校正信号减弱，引发学生模型在长推理链中持续漂移。

Method: 引入Lookahead Group Reward（\\ours{}），通过分析学生候选词在后续步骤中引发的教师置信度，对前一步的候选词进行组归一化奖励；结合熵触发的树注意力机制，高效实现该策略。

Result: 在六个数学和代码基准上，7B规模的学生模型平均@8指标提升2.57点，长序列任务下性能更优，在AIME-26上达到+4.92点提升（39k tokens）。

Conclusion: \ours{}有效缓解了SFD问题，显著增强了长推理链中的监督质量，为基于教师反馈的自洽蒸馏提供了新范式。

Abstract: On-policy distillation transfers reasoning capabilities by training a student model on its own generated trajectories using token-level feedback from a teacher. However, we identify a critical bottleneck, \textbf{Supervision Fidelity Decay (SFD)}: as student-generated prefixes lengthen, the teacher's next-token distribution becomes less confident and less discriminative. Consequently, the teacher-dependent corrective signal in reverse-KL distillation weakens, causing student drift to compound across long reasoning chains. To mitigate SFD, we introduce \textbf{Lookahead Group Reward (\ours{})}. Building on the insight that next-step teacher confidence reflects the discriminative strength of future reverse-KL supervision, \ours{} evaluates the student's top-K candidate tokens by the teacher confidence they induce at the subsequent step and assigns a group-normalized reward. To maintain computational efficiency, we further design an entropy-triggered tree-attention mechanism. Across six math and code benchmarks, \ours{} improves mean@8 by \textbf{2.57} points over OPD for a 7B student, with gains increasing in longer-generation and reaching +\textbf{4.92} points on AIME-26 at 39k tokens.

### [127] [Fine-Tuning Improves Information Conveyance in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30844)
*Yuwei Cheng,Weiyi Tian,Haifeng Xu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Canopy Entropy ($\mathrm{CE}^\star$) 作为衡量语言模型生成过程不确定性的新指标，从树状视角分析生成空间，同时考虑输出长度和序列的不确定性。实证结果表明，微调后的模型虽总熵降低，但其在长度与熵率间的正相关性显著增强，且在控制多种因素后，熵率与语义多样性之间的相关性几乎提升三倍，说明微调将不确定性更高效地转化为语义多样性，而非简单减少不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究认为微调会降低大语言模型的不确定性与多样性，但忽略了输出长度这一关键混淆变量，无法全面刻画不确定性在整个生成过程中的分布情况。因此需要一种能同时考虑输出长度与序列不确定性的新度量方法。

Method: 提出Canopy Entropy ($\mathrm{CE}^\star$)，将语言生成建模为一棵树结构，其中‘canopy’代表所有可能的生成路径集合；$\mathrm{CE}^\star$ 等价于联合香农熵 $H(N, Y_{1:N}\mid X)$，可量化生成空间的有效大小，并引入长度-熵率相关性 $ρ(N, r_N)$ 来评估信息传递效率。

Result: 在多个任务和模型家族中，微调模型表现出更强的正向 $ρ(N, r_N)$ 相关性，即使总熵下降；在控制模型族、任务、提示和输出长度等影响后，微调使熵率与语义多样性间的相关性接近翻倍，表明微调提升了将随机性转化为语义丰富性的能力。

Conclusion: 微调并非单纯减少不确定性，而是重新组织不确定性，使其更高效地转化为更具信息量和语义意义的生成内容。

Abstract: Fine-tuning is often believed to reduce uncertainty and diversity in large language models, but existing analyses overlook output length, a key confounder, and therefore fail to capture how uncertainty is distributed across an entire generation rollout. To address this, we propose Canopy Entropy ($\mathrm{CE}^\star$), a measure that views language generation from a tree perspective, where ``canopy'' represents the space of all possible rollouts, making $\mathrm{CE}^\star$ naturally quantify the effective size of the generation space. $\mathrm{CE}^\star$ jointly captures uncertainty in both the output length $N$ and the generated sequence $Y_{1:N}$ -- indeed, we show that it equals to total Shannon entropy $H(N, Y_{1:N}\mid X)$, where $X$ denotes the prompt. This formulation yields interpretable metrics, including a length-entropy correlation term $ρ(N, r_N)$, where $r_N$ is the entropy rate, quantifying information conveyance efficiency by indicating whether longer outputs are more or less informative per token. Empirically, across tasks and model families, we find that fine-tuned models consistently exhibit stronger positive correlation $ρ(N, r_N)$, even when total entropy decreases. Furthermore, after controlling for model family, task, prompt, and output-length effects, we find that fine-tuning nearly triples the correlation strength between entropy rate and semantic diversity, suggesting that aligned models convert token uncertainty into semantic diversity more efficiently. Overall, these results demonstrate that fine-tuning does not simply reduce uncertainty, but fundamentally reorganizes it into more informative and semantically meaningful generations. Our code is available at https://github.com/WeiyiTian/canopy-entropy.

### [128] [Speculative Pipeline Decoding: Higher-Accruacy and Zero-Bubble Speculation via Pipeline Parallelism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30852)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 Speculative Pipeline Decoding (SPD) 框架，将目标大模型划分为 n 个流水线阶段，通过推测模块聚合各流水线深度的中间特征，实现与主模型流水线步骤并行的单序列推测生成，确保低难度、高接受率和零延迟空洞。

Conclusion: SPD 框架成功释放了流水线并行性的真正潜力，为大模型推理加速提供了一个高效、可扩展的新范式。

Abstract: Speculative Decoding (SD) accelerates low-concurrency LLM inference by employing a draft-then-verify paradigm. However, mainstream methods typically rely on multi-token prediction, which introduces escalating prediction difficulty and serial drafting latency. To address these, we propose Speculative Pipeline Decoding (SPD), a groundbreaking framework that unlocks the true potential of pipeline parallelism. By partitioning the target LLM into $n$ pipeline stages, SPD allows LLM to process $n$ tokens in parallel to accelerate decoding. To continuous fill the pipeline in single sequence decoding, a speculation module aggregates intermediate features across different pipeline depths to predict the next token, executing strictly in parallel with the target model's pipeline step, to realize bounded difficulty, higher acceptance rates, and zero latency bubbles. Our experiments demonstrate that SPD achieves a significantly higher theoretical speedup compared to mainstream baselines, offering a highly scalable solution for LLM decoding acceleration. Our code is available at https://github.com/yuyijiong/speculative_pipeline_decoding

To address this issue, we propose a Model-Aware Diverse Core Set Selection method, which distinguishes data features based on the neural activation states during LLM inference. ### [130] [dMoE: dLLMs with Learnable Block Experts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30876)
*Sicheng Feng,Zigeng Chen,Gongfan Fang,Xinyin Ma,Xinchao Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: dMoE提出了一种块级Mixture-of-Experts（MoE）框架，解决扩散语言模型（dLLMs）与MoE结合时因块并行解码与令牌级专家选择不匹配导致的专家激活数量过多问题。通过将每个块内的令牌级专家分布聚合为统一的块级分布，实现更一致的专家路由，显著减少唯一激活专家数，降低内存占用，并提升推理速度，同时保持接近原始性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前扩散语言模型（dLLMs）与Mixture-of-Experts（MoE）架构结合时，存在块并行解码与令牌级独立路由之间的不匹配，导致唯一激活专家数量激增，造成内存瓶颈。

Method: 提出dMoE框架，将每个块内多个令牌的专家分布聚合为一个统一的块级专家分布，以此指导专家路由，实现更高效的资源利用和一致性调度。

Result: 在多个基准测试中，dMoE将唯一激活专家数从69.5降至14.6，保留99.11%原性能，内存使用减少76.64%至79.84%，端到端延迟加速1.14倍至1.66倍。

Conclusion: dMoE通过块级专家路由有效缓解了dLLMs与MoE融合中的内存瓶颈，实现了高性能与高效率的平衡，具有显著的实用价值。

Abstract: Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) have recently emerged as a promising alternative to autoregressive models, offering competitive performance while naturally supporting parallel decoding. However, as dLLMs are increasingly integrated with Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures to scale model capacity, a fundamental mismatch arises between block parallel decoding and token-level expert selection. Specifically, each dLLM forward pass processes multiple tokens with bidirectional dependencies, whereas conventional MoE layers route each token independently. This mismatch substantially increases the number of uniquely activated experts, making inference increasingly memory-bound. To address this, we propose dMoE, a simple yet effective block-level MoE framework. The central idea of dMoE is to aggregate token-level expert distributions within each block into a unified block-level expert distribution, which is then used to guide expert routing in a more coherent manner. In this way, dMoE substantially reduces the number of uniquely activated experts during inference without sacrificing performance, thereby mitigating the memory-bound bottleneck. Extensive experiments across a variety of benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of dMoE. On average, dMoE reduces the number of uniquely activated experts from 69.5 to 14.6 while retaining 99.11% of the original performance. Meanwhile, it reduces memory usage by 76.64% to 79.84% and achieves 1.14$\times$ to 1.66$\times$ end-to-end latency speedup. Code is available at: https://github.com/fscdc/dMoE

### [131] [PatchWorld: Gradient-Free Optimization of Executable World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30880)
*Jiaxin Bai,Yue Guo,Yifei Dong,Jiaxuan Xiong,Tianshi Zheng,Yixia Li,Tianqing Fang,Yufei Li,Yisen Gao,Haoyu Huang,Zhongwei Xie,Hong Ting Tsang,Zihao Wang,Lihui Liu,Jeff Pan,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PatchWorld 是一个梯度无关的框架，将离线轨迹转化为可执行的 Python 世界模型，通过反例引导的代码修复实现。它生成符号化的信念状态程序，支持可检查、可重放和局部修补，优于现有方法在七个 AgentGym 环境中的代码规划表现（76.4% 宏成功），且无需在世界模型预测模块中调用 LLM。研究发现，人为指定的残差记忆偏置虽提升观测保真度，但削弱决策效用，揭示了观测保真与动作区分性动态之间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多基于黑箱模型预测部分可观测环境下的下一步观察，缺乏可解释性和可修正性。本文旨在探索能否利用可执行代码构建可解释、可维护的世界模型，以支持更可靠的状态预测与规划。

Method: PatchWorld 通过分析离线轨迹，识别与真实行为不符的预测结果（反例），并自动修复生成的符号化信念状态程序，形成可执行的 Python 世界模型。该模型支持一歩前瞻规划，并允许人工介入修复局部错误。

Result: 在七种 AgentGym 环境中，PatchWorld-Simple 达到 76.4% 的宏成功率，显著优于其他基于代码的规划方法；引入人类指定的残差记忆偏置可提升观测保真度，但降低决策质量，验证了观测与动作之间存在权衡。

Conclusion: 可执行代码作为世界模型具有可解释、可调试的优势，但在设计时需权衡观测保真度与动作区分性动态。未来工作应探索更智能的代码修复机制与平衡策略。

Abstract: Text-agent environments are typically modeled as partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs), assuming that the simulator's latent state and transition dynamics are hidden from the agent. Yet little work has examined whether executable code can be induced to serve as a world model for prediction and planning under partial observability. We introduce PatchWorld, a gradient-free framework that turns offline trajectories into executable Python world models through counterexample-guided code repair. Instead of predicting the next observation with a black-box model, PatchWorld induces symbolic belief-state programs whose action updates can be inspected, replayed, and locally patched. Across seven AgentGym environments, PatchWorld-Simple achieves the highest code-based planning score among evaluated methods, reaching 76.4\% macro success in live one-step lookahead while invoking no LLM calls inside the world-model prediction module itself. We further find that a human-specified residual-memory bias improves surface observation fidelity but weakens decision utility. This exposes a tradeoff in executable world models, since improving observation fidelity can come at the expense of action-discriminative dynamics, and vice versa. Code is available at https://github.com/HKBU-KnowComp/PatchWorld.

To further construct reliable instances, MineExplorer uses a multi-agent synthesis workflow that jointly designs task graphs, sandbox scenes, and rule-based milestone evaluators. ### [133] [Do Large Language Models Encode Institutional Experience? Evidence from Cross-Linguistic Moral Reasoning Under Ambiguity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30934)
*Nattavudh Powdthavee*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型（LLMs）在不同语言间道德推理的系统性差异，发现语言可能编码其使用环境中的制度特征，使LLMs通过训练继承特定制度的道德先验。在九种语言、六种前沿LLMs和两项预注册研究中，研究者考察了依赖制度运作的道德困境。研究1显示，明确的制度框架下跨语言道德差异未增加，也不与语言社区间的制度差异相关；研究2则表明，在制度模糊但存在制度利益的情境下，跨语言道德差异显著增加，并与现实中的制度差异相关，而明确的制度提示会减弱这种效应。结果表明，制度经验可能以可检测的方式留在语言中，从而影响LLMs的道德推理，但明确的制度线索可抑制这些差异的显现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大语言模型在不同语言间道德推理差异的来源，特别是语言是否编码了其使用者所在制度环境的特征，进而影响模型的道德判断。

Method: 采用两轮预注册研究，涵盖九种语言、六种前沿大语言模型，设计两类情境：一是明确包含制度框架的道德困境，二是制度信息模糊但存在制度关联的情境，通过对比分析跨语言道德判断的差异及其与真实制度质量的关系。

Result: 研究1中，明确制度框架下未观察到跨语言道德差异的增加或与制度差异的相关性；研究2中，在制度模糊情境下，跨语言道德差异显著上升，且与真实世界中的制度差异正相关，而明确制度提示会削弱这一效应。

Conclusion: 语言中可能隐含制度经验的痕迹，影响大语言模型的道德推理，但明确的制度提示可抑制这些差异的表达，说明语言对模型道德判断的影响具有情境依赖性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit systematic differences in moral reasoning across languages, yet the source of this variation remains unclear. We test the hypothesis that languages encode aspects of the institutional environments in which they are spoken, allowing LLMs to inherit institution-specific moral priors through training. Across nine languages spanning a broad gradient of institutional quality, six frontier LLMs, and two preregistered studies, we examine moral dilemmas whose acceptability depends on institutional functioning. In Study 1, explicit institutional framing produced uniformly null results: cross-linguistic moral divergence did not increase in institutionally contingent scenarios, nor did it track institutional differences between language communities. In Study 2, we introduced institutionally ambiguous scenarios in which institutional stakes were present but not explicitly stated. Under these conditions, cross-linguistic moral divergence increased relative to institutionally inert controls and, with one theoretically informative exception, was associated with real-world institutional differences between language communities. Explicit framing again attenuated these effects. These findings suggest that institutional experience may leave detectable traces in language that shape LLM moral reasoning, while also indicating that explicit institutional cues can suppress the expression of those differences.

### [134] [EvoGens: A Population-Based Heuristic Search Framework for Scientific Idea Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30961)

Main category: cs.CL

<details>

Motivation: 现有大语言模型在科研创意生成中存在语义收敛问题，导致创意多样性与新颖性不足，亟需新方法提升探索能力。

Method: EvoGens 采用进化搜索机制，包括基于排名的变异、差异化检索规划以引入外部知识，以及语义感知交叉以融合互补概念；结合轻量级评估信号进行选择，防止过早收敛。

Abstract: Generating novel research ideas is fundamental to scientific progress. While Large Language Models (LLMs) show promise in assisting this process, existing approaches often exhibit semantic convergence, resulting in limited diversity and novelty. To address this, we introduce EvoGens, an evolution-inspired framework that recasts scientific idea generation as an evolutionary search over a population of ideas. EvoGens iteratively applies rank-based mutation with differentiated retrieval planning to incorporate external knowledge, and semantic-aware crossover to fuse complementary concepts for conceptual reorganization. A lightweight evaluation signal guides the selection process, encouraging sustained exploration while mitigating premature convergence. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EvoGens substantially enhances exploration capabilities compared to state-of-the-art baselines. Specifically, it improves the Novelty from 0.1 to 0.4 and the Diversity from 0.24 to 0.55, while maintaining comparable idea quality under the current automatic evaluation protocol. These findings suggest that evolutionary mechanisms can serve as a useful framework for exploration-oriented research ideation, especially for broadening the novelty and diversity of candidate ideas under a shared automatic evaluation setting.

### [135] [Cognitive Fatigue in Autoregressive Transformers: Formalization and Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30981)
*Riju Marwah,Ritvik Garimella,Vishal Pallagani,Atishay Jain,Michael Stewart,Amit Sheth*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为疲劳指数（Fatigue Index, FI）的轻量级、模型无关的诊断工具，用于实时监测自回归语言模型在长序列生成过程中出现的认知疲劳现象。认知疲劳表现为注意力衰退、表征漂移和熵校准失准，导致重复文本、指令偏离和生成不稳定。FI通过聚合这三个信号，在满足单调性、有界性和可解释性等明确公理的基础上，实现了可靠的运行时监控。在九个不同规模（1B-13B参数）的模型上，FI轨迹表现出结构化的动态特征，能有效预测任务退化（AUROC=0.95）和重复性（Spearman rho=0.94），并揭示非单调缩放行为：小于3B的指令微调模型比基础模型更快崩溃，而超过7B后趋势反转。压力测试还表明，长上下文、中间位置证据及降低数值精度会加速FI的触发。研究确立了认知疲劳作为可度量现象的合理性，并将FI定位为生产级大模型系统中提升运行可靠性的原则性工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自回归语言模型在长序列生成过程中常出现重复、指令偏离和熵不稳定等问题，但缺乏实时诊断手段来检测这些退化现象。现有方法难以在生成过程中及时发现并预警这些问题，限制了模型在实际应用中的可靠性。因此，亟需一种能够在线监测生成质量变化的机制，以提升大模型系统的稳定性与可信度。

Method: 提出疲劳指数（Fatigue Index, FI），通过量化注意力衰减、表征漂移和熵校准偏差三个核心信号，构建一个满足单调性、有界性和可解释性公理的综合指标。该方法不依赖特定模型结构，适用于多种语言模型，可在生成过程中实时计算并追踪其变化轨迹。

Result: 在九个不同规模的语言模型（1B-13B参数）上验证，FI轨迹具有明显的结构性时间动态；能高精度预测任务退化（AUROC = 0.95）和重复生成（Spearman rho = 0.94）；揭示出非单调缩放规律：小模型（<3B）指令微调版本比基础模型更早崩溃，但在7B以上则逆转趋势；压力实验显示长上下文、中间证据位置和低精度会显著加速疲劳发生。

Conclusion: 认知疲劳是语言模型在长序列生成中可度量且一致的现象。疲劳指数（FI）作为一种轻量、通用、可解释的运行时诊断工具，具备良好的预测能力和可扩展性，为大模型系统在生产环境中的可靠性监控提供了理论支持和技术手段。

Abstract: Autoregressive language models frequently degrade during long-horizon generation, producing repetitive text, losing instruction adherence, and exhibiting unstable entropy. Despite the prevalence of these failures, practitioners lack online diagnostics to detect them in real-time as they occur. We formalize this degradation as cognitive fatigue, a measurable generation-time state characterized by decay in attention to the original prompt, representational drift, and entropy miscalibration. We introduce the Fatigue Index (FI), a lightweight, model-agnostic diagnostic that aggregates these three signals under explicit axioms (monotonicity, boundedness, interpretability) enabling reliable runtime monitoring. Across nine models (1B-13B parameters), FI trajectories exhibit structured temporal dynamics, predict task degradation (AUROC = 0.95) and repetition (Spearman rho = 0.94), and reveal non-monotonic scaling behavior: instruction-tuned models below 3B exhibit faster collapse than base models, with this trend reversing at 7B. Stress analyses further show that FI onset accelerates under longer contexts, middle-positioned evidence, and reduced numerical precision. These results establish cognitive fatigue as a coherent and measurable phenomenon, and position FI as a principled tool for runtime reliability monitoring in production LLM systems.

### [136] [MoG: Mixture of Experts for Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31010)
*Zheng Yuan,Chuang Zhou,Linhao Luo,Siyu An,Di Yin,Xing Sun,Xiao Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出MoG模型，通过混合专家机制将知识分为通用的枢纽图和特定领域的专家图，利用拓扑感知路由器动态激活专家图以实现精准检索，在多个基准测试中显著优于现有方法，尤其在MuSiQue上提升超过20%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统统一知识库检索易引入无关信息，误导复杂推理任务中的生成结果。为解决此问题，受混合专家（MoE）思想启发，设计更智能、聚焦的检索机制。

Method: 构建双层知识结构：一是始终可访问的枢纽图，用于捕捉核心语义与结构信息并提供上下文线索；二是稀疏激活的专家图，存储领域特异性证据。通过拓扑感知路由器根据查询动态选择少数专家图进行检索，从而缩小证据搜索范围。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation is intensively studied to ground large language models on external evidence. However, retrieving from a unified knowledge base could inevitably introduce irrelevant information that may mislead generation for complex reasoning. Inspired by the conditional computation of mixture of experts (MoE), where a router sparsely selects specialized experts alongside shared ones for each input, we propose \textbf{M}ixture \textbf{o}f experts for \textbf{G}raph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation, i.e., \textbf{MoG}. It organizes knowledge into two core components: (i) diverse, always-accessible hub graphs that encode semantically and structurally central knowledge and provide contextual clues for expert activation, and (ii) sparsely activated expert graphs that contain domain-specific evidence. MoG first accesses hub graphs to identify general evidence and derive contextual clues. Then, a topology-aware router dynamically activates a limited set of expert graphs conditioned on the query, thereby confining retrieval to a focused evidence subspace. Extensive experiments on challenging benchmarks show that MoG consistently outperforms strong baselines, with over 20\% relative improvement on MuSiQue. Our code is available in https://github.com/DEEP-PolyU/MoG.

TL;DR: 提出TRACE方法，通过适应性探测识别任务特异性参数，仅更新关键参数以避免灾难性遗忘，在保持性能的同时降低计算与存储开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有持续微调方法在多任务场景下存在灾难性遗忘或引入额外资源开销的问题，亟需一种高效且能保留已有知识的微调机制。

Method: 通过短时预微调生成任务适应轨迹，利用L2范数、Fisher信息量和参数更新余弦相似度分析，识别每个任务的核心参数；在持续微调中仅更新当前任务的核心参数，其余冻结。

Result: 在多个基准测试中表现优越，具备跨模型与规模的可迁移性，支持小模型指导大模型微调，有效缓解遗忘并降低资源消耗。

Abstract: In real-world deployment, LLMs are often adapted continually across tasks to keep LLMs up-to-date in production, where new fine-tuning should preserve previously learned skills. However, indiscriminately mixing tasks can dilute task specialization, while sequential fine-tuning (full-parameter or low rank adaptation) often causes catastrophic forgetting due to destructive overwriting. Replay-based continual tuning and maintaining separate task-specific adapters can mitigate forgetting, but introduce additional compute, storage, and management overhead. Recognizing the redundancy of LLM parameters for any single task, we reframe continual task adaptation as task-specific parameter discovery via adaptation-aware probing: a short warm-start probe exposes a task's adaptation trace, enabling us to identify and isolate the small subset of parameters essential for each task to mitigate catastrophic forgetting. Building on this view, we introduce TRACE, a novel approach for discovering Task-specific paRameters via Adaptation-aware probing for Continual finE-tuning. We perform a short warm-start fine-tune to derive task-specific core parameters by comparing the warm-started and pre-trained models. Core parameters are identified via two strategies: importance scoring (L$_2$ norm and Fisher Information) and specificity analysis (cosine similarity of parameter updates). In continual fine-tuning settings, only the active task's core parameters are updated while others remain frozen, preserving prior knowledge. We conduct extensive experiments across multiple standard benchmarks to demonstrate the superior performance of our proposed method. Additionally, we validate the generalization of our method through a cross-model and scale transferability study, demonstrating a "small-to-large" paradigm that guides the fine-tuning of large-scale models under resource constraints.

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has recently emerged as the cornerstone for shaping the remarkable coding abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the scalability of RLVR is severely constrained by the scarcity of sufficiently challenging verifiable code tasks that target near the model's edge of competence. Prior studies often rely on heuristic seed expansions for data synthesis, which severely limits both novelty and difficulty. Consequently, the training value of such data fails to scale proportionally with the size of its synthesis. To this end, we propose Atomic Decomposition and Recombination (ADR), a novel framework that generates verifiable code tasks via decomposition into atomic elements and controlled recombination, thereby enabling the generation of genuinely novel and challenging verifiable code tasks. Our work sheds light on a new paradigm for novel code task synthesis and scalable RLVR training.
