### [140] [AdaptR1: Reinforcement Learning Based Adaptive Interleaved Thinking in Multi-hop Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31062)
*Yuxin Wang,Jiahao Lu,Qifeng Wu,Shicheng Fang,Chuanyuan Tan,Yining Zheng,Xuanjing Huang,Xipeng Qiu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AdaptR1 是一种基于强化学习的自适应交错思考框架，用于多跳问答任务，通过动态分配每一步的推理预算，显著减少不必要的推理令牌（如在 HotpotQA 上减少 90.35%），同时保持或提升性能。其核心创新在于无需监督微调即可冷启动，并利用质量门控效率奖励机制实现精细化控制。分析表明，过度思考主要集中在初始规划阶段，验证了分步自适应策略的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于链式思维（CoT）的方法在简单任务上容易产生‘过度思考’，导致推理成本增加；而现有自适应方法仅在查询级别做决策，忽略了多步任务中不同中间阶段对推理需求的动态变化。因此需要一种能按步骤动态调整推理预算的机制。

Method: 提出 AdaptR1 框架，采用完全基于强化学习的方法，设计质量门控的效率奖励函数，在每一步动态决定是否进行显式推理，实现细粒度的推理预算分配，无需监督微调即可冷启动。

Result: 在 Graph-R1 设置下，平均思考令牌减少 69.71%，在 HotpotQA 上更是达到 90.35% 的降幅，同时模型性能与标准基线相当甚至更优。分析显示过度思考主要集中于初始规划阶段，证明分步自适应的有效性。

Conclusion: AdaptR1 通过强化学习实现细粒度、动态的推理预算控制，在大幅降低推理开销的同时保持高质量输出，为复杂多步任务中的高效推理提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable performance in complex reasoning tasks through Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting. However, this approach often leads to ``over-thinking,'' where models generate unnecessarily long reasoning traces for simple queries and incur avoidable inference cost. While recent work has explored adaptive reasoning, existing methods typically make a single query-level decision about whether to reason. This overlooks the dynamic nature of multi-step tasks, where the need for explicit reasoning varies across intermediate stages. To address this limitation, we introduce AdaptR1, a Reinforcement Learning (RL) based framework for adaptive interleaved thinking in multi-hop Question Answering (QA). Unlike previous approaches that require Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) for cold-start initialization, AdaptR1 uses a fully RL-based strategy with a quality-gated efficiency reward to dynamically allocate reasoning budgets at each step. Under the Graph-R1 setting, AdaptR1 reduces average think tokens by 69.71\%, with a 90.35\% reduction on HotpotQA, while maintaining performance comparable to or better than standard baselines. Furthermore, our analysis reveals that overthinking in multi-hop reasoning is not uniformly distributed but occurs predominantly during the initial planning stages, highlighting the effectiveness of step-wise adaptive budget allocation.

</details>


### [141] [ConsisGuard: Aligning Safety Deliberation with Policy Enforcement in LLM Guardrails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31073)
*Yan Wang,Zhixuan Chu,Zihao Xue,Zhen Bi,Bingyu Zhu,YueFeng Chen,Zeyu Yang,Jungang Lou,Longtao Huang,Ningyu Zhang,Kui Ren,Hui Xue*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ConsisGuard解决推理型大模型护栏中的决策一致性问题，通过策略到决策的轨迹蒸馏和功能耦合对齐，提升安全政策执行的可靠性，减少安全误判。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理型大模型护栏虽生成显式推理过程，但推理与最终决策之间存在不一致，导致安全策略未能忠实执行，形成‘思辨-执行间隙’，影响安全防护效果。

Method: 提出ConsisGuard框架，包含政策到决策的轨迹蒸馏和功能耦合对齐机制，强化推理与决策间的内在一致性。

Result: 在提示和响应有害性检测基准上，ConsisGuard不仅提升了检测性能，还显著降低了政策执行失败率。

Conclusion: 可靠的推理型护栏不仅需要合理的推理，更需确保推理与最终决策在安全政策上保持一致，实现政策的忠实执行。

Abstract: Reasoning-based LLM guardrails improve safety moderation by generating explicit rationales before issuing final decisions. However, their rationales do not always lead to faithful enforcement: a model may recognize a harmful intent in its reasoning but still predict a safe label, or issue an unsafe decision without policy-grounded justification. We identify this safety-critical failure mode as the deliberation-to-enforcement gap. Unlike general chain-of-thought faithfulness, guardrail reliability requires policy execution consistency: the generated reasoning should be grounded in the safety policy, and the final decision should be entailed by that reasoning. We propose ConsisGuard, a consistency-aware framework for reasoning-based LLM guardrails. ConsisGuard performs Policy-to-Decision Trajectory Distillation and Functional Coupling Alignment, aligning the internal coupling between safety deliberation and decision enforcement. Experiments on prompt and response harmfulness detection benchmarks show that ConsisGuard improves detection performance while reducing policy execution failures. These results suggest that reliable reasoning-based guardrails require accurate faithful execution of safety policies.

Abstract: Science news is an important medium to communicate discoveries between the research communities and the public. ### [144] [GRKV: Global Regression for Training-Free KV Cache Compression in Long-Context LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31105)
*Junjie Peng,You Wu,Haoyi Wu,Jialong Han,Xiaohua Xie,Kewei Tu,Jianhuang Lai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: GRKV是一种无需训练的KV缓存压缩方法，通过岭回归减少压缩缓存与完整缓存注意力输出之间的差异，有效缓解了传统方法中因跨段合并导致的信息失衡和过度合并问题。在LongBench和RULER基准测试中表现最优，几乎无额外开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV缓存压缩方法在结合段落保留与合并时，导致合并集中在少数边界载体令牌上，造成信息损失和过量合并，亟需一种更均衡的合并策略。

Method: GRKV采用基于岭回归的合并步骤，将被丢弃令牌的信息分布到保留令牌中，并通过正则化防止过度平滑，实现全局优化。

Result: 在LongBench和RULER长上下文基准测试中，GRKV是唯一在压缩后仍提升整体性能的方法，且计算和内存开销极小。

Conclusion: GRKV提供了一种高效、无需训练的KV缓存合并机制，显著改善了长上下文语言模型中的缓存压缩效果，为未来长序列处理提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) with extended context lengths rely on the key-value (KV) cache to support attention over prior tokens. However, maintaining the KV cache incurs substantial memory overhead, motivating KV-cache compression methods that enforce a fixed budget through eviction and merging. Modern eviction methods increasingly adopt span-based retention because preserving contiguous spans is empirically effective and better preserves semantic coherence. Yet, when combined with post-eviction merging, span-based retention concentrates merges onto a small set of span-boundary carrier tokens, producing a highly imbalanced merge pattern that exacerbates over-merging and increases information loss. To address this imbalance, we propose GRKV (Global Regression for KV Cache), a training-free KV-cache merging method that directly minimizes the discrepancy between compressed-cache and full-cache attention outputs. GRKV uses ridge-regression-based merge steps to distribute information from evicted tokens across retained tokens, while regularizing the updates to prevent over-smoothing. Across the LongBench and RULER long-context benchmarks, GRKV is the only merging method that improves overall performance with minimal overhead.

To address this gap, we present a meta-study of multilingual model performance robustness in MTEB, applying a diverse set of multi-criteria decision-making ranking schemes and introducing two robustness indicators: dataset-composition robustness (sensitivity of rankings to changing dataset compositions) and ranking-scheme robustness (sensitivity to aggregation method change). ### [147] [D$^3$: Dynamic Directional Graph-Constrained Data Scheduling for LLM Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31164)
*Yuanjian Xu,Jianing Hao,Guang Zhang,Zhong Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出D^3框架，通过动态方向图约束数据调度，建模训练单元间的损失依赖关系，优化训练顺序以提升学习效率。理论驱动且在预训练和微调阶段均表现优越，具备高效近似算法以保证可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据调度方法多关注整体数据分布，忽视样本间在训练过程中的相互影响。真实数据常存在方向性影响，训练顺序至关重要，因此需优先处理具有更大影响力的样本以提高学习效率。

Method: 将训练单元间的复杂交互建模为动态影响图，其中边表示基于损失的依赖关系；在此图上求解带约束的优化问题，获得尊重信息流演变的训练顺序；采用高效近似算法控制额外计算开销。

Result: 在预训练和后训练阶段均显著优于现有数据调度方法，有效提升模型性能，同时保持较低的计算成本。

Conclusion: D^3通过建模样本间的动态方向性影响，实现了更高效的训练序列规划，为大规模语言模型的数据调度提供了新的理论与实践路径。

Abstract: Training data plays a central role in large language models (LLMs) optimization, motivating extensive research on data scheduling strategies. Most existing approaches concentrate on adjusting the overall data distribution but neglect the underlying interactions between samples during training. However, we argue that such interactions cannot be overlooked, as real-world data samples frequently exhibit directional influences on each other, making the training order crucial. Intuitively, we can prioritize train-units with greater influence to improves learning efficiency. In this work, we propose $D^3$, a Dynamic Directional graph-constrained Data scheduling framework. $D^3$ formulates the complex interactions among train-units as a dynamic influence graph, where edges represent loss-based dependencies. It then solves a constrained optimization problem over this graph to derive the training order, which ensures that the data sequence respects the evolving information flow throughout training. Our approach is theoretically motivated and yields consistent improvements over existing data scheduling methods across both pre-training and post-training phases. Furthermore, for scalability, $D^3$ also employs an efficient approximation algorithm that keeps the additional computational overhead within a manageable range. For future research, the code is available at https://github.com/xuyj233/D3.

### [148] [Towards Efficient LLMs Annealing with Principled Sample Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31175)
*Yuanjian Xu,Jianing Hao,Wanbo Zhang,Zhong Li,Guang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出DiReCT框架，通过分析损失曲面的谱几何特性，在模型预训练的退火阶段将数据选择建模为约束优化问题，以实现方向性约束下的最优收敛，显著提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前模型预训练中的退火阶段依赖经验启发式策略进行数据选择，缺乏优化理论基础，难以有效提升模型质量。

Method: 基于损失曲面的谱几何分析，将数据选择转化为满足不同特征方向上梯度约束的优化问题，提出方向性受限的约束训练（DiReCT）框架，通过引入基于海森矩阵谱特性的方向性约束，引导梯度沿曲率感知的最优下降路径更新。

Result: 在多种模型规模下，DiReCT均取得领先性能，验证了其有效性与普适性。

Conclusion: DiReCT通过引入谱几何指导的数据选择机制，为退火阶段提供了可解释、可优化的数据筛选方法，显著提升了大模型预训练的质量。

Abstract: The annealing phase is a pivotal convergence stage in LLM pre-training that ultimately determines final model quality. However, effectively selecting training data during this phase remains a key challenge. Current strategies rely on empirical heuristics, such as domain filtering or context extension, which lack a principled grounding in optimization theory. In this work, we characterize the annealing phase through the lens of the loss landscape's spectral geometry. We argue that optimal convergence requires gradient updates to satisfy heterogeneous constraints across different eigen-directions. Building on this insight, we formulate data selection as a problem of satisfying these directional constraints. To this end, we propose DiReCT (Directionally-Restrained Constrained Training), a novel framework that reformulates sample selection in the annealing stage as a constrained optimization problem. By imposing explicit directional constraints on per-sample gradients based on the spectral properties of the Hessian, DiReCT identifies samples that align with the optimal curvature-aware descent path. Extensive experiments across various model scales demonstrate that DiReCT consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance. For future research, code is available at https://github.com/xuyj233/Direct.

### [149] [Steering LLMs? Actually, Sparse Autoencoders can outperform simple baselines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31183)
*Mikkel Godsk Jørgensen,Lars Kai Hansen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究为稀疏自编码器（SAEs）提供部分反驳，表明在使用监督式特征选择与标注管道后，SAEs在AxBench基准测试中的性能可接近甚至媲美参考的LoRA方法。研究发现所选特征与其标签之间具有高度因果性，且高稀疏性（低l0）并非实现有效控制的关键因素，挑战了先前研究的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明稀疏自编码器在模型控制任务中表现不佳，但本研究旨在重新评估其潜力，探索是否通过更优的特征选择方法能提升其性能，并验证其解释性组件的有效性。

Method: 提出一种基于监督的特征选择与标注管道，用于筛选和标记稀疏自编码器中的关键特征；利用解释性组件分析特征与输出之间的因果关系；在AxBench基准上对比SAEs与LoRA等基线方法的控制性能。

Result: SAEs在采用新管道后性能显著提升，接近或达到LoRA水平；所选特征表现出强烈的因果性；高稀疏性并非成功控制的必要条件。

Conclusion: 稀疏自编码器在合适的特征选择与标注策略下具备强大的模型控制能力，其潜力被早期研究低估，且高稀疏性并非必须，这为理解大语言模型内部机制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) have been seen as a promising avenue for exploring the internals of Large Language Models (LLMs) and for steering model output generation. When AxBench - a model steering benchmark - was introduced in Wu et al. (2025), SAEs did not seem to live up to their original hype due to poor steering performance relative to a set of simple baselines. This work serves as a partial rebuttal for Sparse Autoencoders and suggests that the results of Wu et al. (2025) did not do them full justice. We find that Sparse Autoencoders can, in fact, perform close to on par with the reference LoRA performance on the AxBench benchmark, when features are selected and labelled with our supervised pipeline. We also find that our pipeline selects features that are surprisingly causal of their identified labels when using only its interpretability-based components. Lastly, we present evidence that high sparsity (low l0) may not be crucial for successful steering based on interpretability, which is in contrast to the earlier findings in Wang et al. (2025).

</details>


### [150] [Learning Whom to Trust: Market-Feedback Adaptive Retrieval for Frozen LLMs in Event-Driven Financial RAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31201)
*Zijie Zhao,Roy E. Welsch*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统金融RAG系统依赖文本相关性排序证据，但在金融市场中，有效信息取决于事件类型、预测时间范围和市场背景。因此需要更智能的检索机制以适应动态市场情境。

Method: 采用冻结大语言模型（LLM）阅读器，通过外部贝叶斯源记忆持续更新检索层，结合点位时间市场上下文卡片与新闻及SEC文件片段，进行多时域残差收益预测。

Result: 在89只纳斯达克股票的测试集上，使用原始新闻和EDGAR文件片段，所提方法使宏F1从0.438升至0.471，下游投资组合夏普比率从0.52增至0.84；监督式LoRA阅读器改进有限，未超越冻结源记忆方案。

Conclusion: 对于金融RAG系统，学习如何选择检索来源的重要性不亚于如何理解内容，基于市场反馈的源记忆机制提供了一种简单且模块化的适应路径。

Abstract: Financial retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems typically rank evidence by textual relevance, but in financial markets the useful evidence source depends on event type, forecast horizon, and market context. We study news-triggered event-impact prediction as a point-in-time financial RAG problem. For each company-news anchor, the system retrieves related financial news and SEC filing passages, appends a pre-decision market-context card, and predicts multi-horizon residual-return signals. Our method keeps the large language model (LLM) reader frozen and adapts the retrieval layer through an external Bayesian source memory updated from matured residual-return feedback. On a fixed 89-stock Nasdaq-oriented universe derived from the FinRL-DeepSeek/FNSPID task, using original FNSPID news and point-in-time EDGAR filing passages, Frozen Reader with Source Memory improves held-out macro-F1 from 0.438 to 0.471 and downstream portfolio Sharpe from 0.52 to 0.84 relative to Frozen Reader with No Memory. A supervised LoRA reader improves static RAG modestly, but does not improve over the frozen source-memory reader. These results suggest that, for financial RAG, learning where to retrieve from can be as important as learning how to read, offering a simple, modular route to market-feedback adaptation.

### [151] [Shared Doubt: Zero-shot Cross-Lingual Confidence Estimation for Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31220)
*Athina Kyriakou,Dennis Ulmer,Ivan Titov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究多语言大模型中是否存在可跨语言迁移的置信度特征，提出一种轻量级线性探测器，仅通过单语训练即可零样本泛化到未见的、类型多样的语言，且无需目标语言监督。实验发现置信度特征集中于各语言的中间层，表明存在共享的置信度子空间。该方法在跨语言场景下表现良好，无需重训练，优于其他主流置信度估计方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用轻量级线性探测器，直接从多语言大模型的中间表示中预测答案正确性；在单语数据上训练后，零样本测试其在多种未见语言上的表现；通过层权重分析与消融实验揭示置信度特征分布规律。

Result: 探测器在未见语言上实现零样本泛化，表现出良好的跨语言能力；置信度特征集中在中间层，支持存在共享置信度子空间的假设；性能优于其他常见置信度估计方法。

Conclusion: 多语言大模型中存在可跨语言迁移的置信度特征，通过简单线性探测即可实现高效、无监督的跨语言置信度估计，为多语言场景下的可靠性评估提供有效解决方案。

Abstract: Confidence estimation (CE), i.e. quantifying the reliability of a model's prediction, has attracted great interest in the context of large language models (LLMs). However, most studies focus on English, ignoring the multilingual reality of LLM usage, while many CE methods degrade or require retraining across languages. To address this gap, we investigate whether multilingual LLMs encode shared, language-transferable confidence features. We use a lightweight linear probe that predicts answer correctness directly from intermediate representations. Trained monolingually, the probe generalizes zero-shot to unseen, typologically diverse languages without target-language supervision. Learned layer weights and multiple ablations reveal that confidence features concentrate in middle layers across languages, suggesting a shared confidence subspace. While zero-shot cross-lingual performance depends on similarity to the source language, the probe provides a strong baseline without any retraining and compares favorably to other popular confidence estimation methods.

### [152] [Scaling Multi-Hop Training Data via Graph-Constrained Path Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31238)
*Pengyu Chen,Yonggang Zhang,Mingming Chen,Jun Song,Wei Xue,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新方法，通过将推理路径枚举与教师模型的语义生成解耦，解决大规模多跳训练数据构建在结构化文档中的挑战。利用图结构约束（五种几何可接受性条件）预先验证路径，仅在有效路径上调用教师模型生成问答对，显著提升合成数据的可生成性。实验表明，在相同训练规模下，有无约束的链路表现相近，但全规模下性能提升主要源于可用语料扩展4.4倍，而非单条路径质量提高。在CUAD法律合同数据集上微调Qwen3-32B，闭书Token F1从21.66%提升至38.58%。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法依赖单一教师模型联合发现证据路径并生成问答对，但在具有重复模板和密集交叉引用的现实专业文档中表现不佳，因缺乏对路径有效性的先验控制。

Method: 将路径搜索与语义生成分离：离线构建基于上下文关键词聚类的图结构，施加五种几何可接受性约束（如局部相似性与上限），仅对经验证的有效路径调用教师模型进行问答生成。

Result: 在80K个由CUAD合同文本构造的样本上微调Qwen3-32B，闭书Token F1从21.66%提升至38.58%；消融实验显示性能提升主要来自语料规模扩大（4.4倍），而非路径质量提升。

Conclusion: 图结构约束的核心作用是提升教师模型的合成可行性，而非优化路径内容本身；该方法为大规模专业化文档上的多跳推理训练提供了高效、可扩展的数据构建范式。

Abstract: Endowing large language models with compositional reasoning over specialized documents requires multi-hop training data at scale, where such data rarely exists outside of curated benchmarks built on structured sources. To construct it directly from plain, unannotated text, existing methods ask a single teacher model to jointly discover an evidence path through a document and verbalize it as a question-answer pair. However, these methods degrade sharply when documents are structured around repetitive templates and densely cross-referencing clauses, conditions that characterize most real-world specialized corpora. In this work, we decouple the two operations: reasoning paths are enumerated offline over a graph of contextual keyword centroids, and the teacher is invoked only to verbalize pre-validated paths. The graph enforces five geometric admissibility constraints, for which we provide Gram-matrix arguments establishing that local similarity bounds alone admit endpoint drift up to ${\sim}91^{\circ}$, and that an upper similarity bound is necessary to exit dense embedding cliques formed by boilerplate text. A matched-size ablation isolates the mechanism: at equal training scale, constrained and unconstrained chains yield indistinguishable downstream performance, and the gain at full scale comes from a 4.4$\times$ expansion of the usable corpus rather than from higher per-chain quality -- reframing the role of graph constraints, in this setting, as raising teacher synthesizability rather than improving chain content. Fine-tuning Qwen3-32B on 80K examples constructed from the CUAD legal contract corpus improves closed-book Token F1 from 21.66% to 38.58%. We have released our codes at https://github.com/hkgai-official/GCSCS.

</details>

Result: 成功结构化超过70%的16,316条维护日志数据；解决了变桨系统故障未分类、系统代码缺失等常见问题；构建了基于实证的故障模式、症状、机制和原因词典，显著减少人工FMEA的主观性；实现了从定性观察向定量可靠性指标的转化。

Abstract: As wind turbine fleets age, data-driven reliability engineering is essential to optimise their operation and maintenance for service life extension and levelised cost of energy reduction. Failure event descriptions within historical maintenance logs are a source of valuable reliability intelligence. However, they typically appear as unstructured natural language entries, rendering them inaccessible for quantitative analysis. This paper presents a novel methodology leveraging a large language model (LLM) to systematically standardise and structure maintenance logs based on their free-text descriptors. Operating on a dataset of 16,316 maintenance logs from 280 turbines monitored over nine years, the developed model-agnostic framework autonomously corrected hierarchical system codes and extracted evidence-based taxonomies of maintenance actions and failure modes. The automated pipeline successfully structured over 70% of the dataset. It resolved pervasive misclassification issues, such as isolating previously unclassified pitch system faults and restoring missing system codes, and enriched the records by applying empirical taxonomies to label specific actions taken and failure modes addressed. By using system-based log batches to construct empirical dictionaries of failure modes, observable symptoms, dominant mechanisms, and candidate causes, this approach reduces the inherent subjectivity of manual failure modes and effects analysis (FMEA). Ultimately, the methodology provides a highly scalable, cost-effective blueprint for translating large sets of qualitative field observations into quantitative reliability metrics, laying the foundation for integrated root-cause analysis across the renewable energy sector, improved FMEA, and advanced predictive maintenance.

### [154] [Divergence Decoding: Inference-Time Unlearning via Auxiliary Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31293)
*Humzah Merchant,Bradford Levy*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Divergence Decoding（DD）机制，利用小型辅助模型在推理时调整大型语言模型的logits，避免生成敏感数据。该方法训练简单，效果优于现有最先进方法，且可将调整后的分布轻松蒸馏回主模型。该方法具有通用性，不仅适用于文本生成，还在图像领域展现出良好的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型容易记忆训练数据中的敏感信息，带来隐私和版权风险。现有的去记忆（unlearning）方法往往导致性能严重下降或对复杂查询无效，亟需一种高效且不损害模型性能的解决方案。

Method: 提出Divergence Decoding（DD），通过小规模辅助模型在推理阶段调节大模型的输出分布，使其避开特定敏感内容。辅助模型采用标准预训练与微调流程进行训练。随后，通过知识蒸馏将调整后的分布迁移到原模型中。

Result: DD在多个未学习基准测试中显著优于现有最先进方法，无论模型规模或训练数据量如何，均表现出优异的去记忆效果。同时，该方法在图像生成任务中也展现出良好泛化能力。

Conclusion: Divergence Decoding是一种高效、低成本且通用的去记忆方法，能够在不显著损失模型性能的前提下有效消除敏感知识，适用于多种概率模型及任务场景。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) frequently memorize sensitive training data thereby creating significant privacy and copyright risks. Addressing these risks, i.e., removing such knowledge from an existing model checkpoint, has proven challenging as many unlearning methods lead to catastrophic utility loss or are ineffective for complex queries. We introduce Divergence Decoding (DD), a mechanism that uses small auxiliary models to steer the logits of the LLM away from specific data during inference. Training these models is straight forward, i.e., we use standard pre-training and fine-tuning setups. We find the method decisively outperforms state-of-the-art (SOTA) baselines on unlearning benchmarks across a variety of model and training dataset scales consistent with DD being an effective and inexpensive solution to unlearning. We then demonstrate that this steered distribution can be trivially distilled back into the base model. Since the method is generally applicable to any probabilistic model, we explore its efficacy outside of text generation and find evidence of generalization to the domain of images.

### [155] [Reinforcement Learning Amplifies Emergent Misalignment from Harmless Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31328)
*Magnus Jørgenvåg,David Kaczér,Lasse Ruttert,Marvin Gülhan,Lucie Flek,Florian Mai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在强化学习（RL）微调过程中，小型开源语言模型出现的新兴错位（EM）现象。研究发现，奖励狭隘且明显的错误行为会导致比样本匹配的监督微调（SFT）更高的整体领域错位；此外，自然可能产生的奖励信号（如不受欢迎的审美偏好或拙劣的修辞）也能引发EM；最后，评估了用于缓解SFT导致的EM的训练中缓解策略，发现它们大多可迁移，其中交错使用在线安全数据效果最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要集中在监督微调（SFT）场景下的新兴错位（EM），而对强化学习（RL）中EM的研究受限于大型封闭源代码模型，难以复现和成本高昂。因此，亟需在小型、开放权重的模型中系统性地研究RL诱导的EM，以推动其可访问性和可重复性。

Method: 在小型、现成的开源语言模型上，通过设计不同的奖励信号（包括狭隘的明显错误行为、自然可能存在的非主流审美偏好和低效修辞）进行强化学习微调，系统评估其对整体领域错位的影响。同时，测试了为SFT设计的多种训练中缓解策略在RL设置下的表现，并比较其有效性。

Result: 1. RL微调下，奖励狭隘错误行为所导致的错位显著高于样本匹配的SFT；2. 即使是自然可能产生的非主流偏好或低效表达，也能诱发显著的普遍错位；3. 多数为SFT设计的缓解策略在RL设置中仍有效，其中交错使用在线安全数据的策略表现最优。

Conclusion: 强化学习同样会引发新兴错位现象，且其影响在小型开源模型中可被观察与验证。该研究揭示了即使看似合理的奖励信号也可能导致广泛错位，提示需要更谨慎地设计奖励机制。同时，已有缓解SFT诱导错位的方法在RL中具有良好的泛化能力，尤其是在线安全数据的交错使用，为未来构建安全可控的强化学习语言模型提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Emergent misalignment (EM) is the surprising tendency of language models to become broadly misaligned after fine-tuning on narrowly misaligned examples. While EM has been extensively studied in the supervised fine-tuning (SFT) setting, evidence that it also arises from reinforcement learning (RL) is limited to large, closed-source models, leaving the phenomenon expensive to study and difficult to reproduce. We characterize EM from RL in small, off-the-shelf open-weight models along three axes. First, we show that rewarding narrow, overtly misaligned behavior produces substantially higher general-domain misalignment than sample-matched SFT. Second, we show that EM from RL can be induced by reward signals that could plausibly arise naturally, such as unpopular aesthetic preferences or poor rhetorical appeals. Third, we evaluate in-training mitigations developed for SFT-induced EM and find that they broadly transfer, with interleaving on-policy safety data performing best.

### [156] [Bundesrecht: An Open Library and Corpus for German Statutory Reference Processing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31338)
*Harshil Darji,Martin Heckelmann,Christina Kratsch,Gerard de Melo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: bundesrecht 是一个针对德语法律引用处理的开源资源，包含软件库和结构化语料库，可实现从原始引用字符串到法定条款的端到端解析、标准化与解析。它能处理缩写、复合引用及细粒度层级结构，并在2,944个标注引用上验证了其性能，显著优于传统字符串匹配方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 德语法律引用形式紧凑多变，常含缩写、多重目标和低层级指向，现有工具仅覆盖部分流程，缺乏统一处理方案，因此需要一个完整且开放的处理管道。

Method: 构建bundesrecht软件库与结构化语料库，实现对德语法律引用的解析、标准化、归一化与链接，将原始引用映射为结构化对象并扩展为标准形式，同时保留法规内部层级关系。

Result: 在2,944个标注引用上，解析与标准化模块在精确匹配和微信息提取指标上表现良好；归一化引用显著提升对实际引用变体的分组准确性，优于传统字符串匹配。

Conclusion: bundesrecht是首个覆盖德语法律引用处理全流程的开源资源，支持从原始引用到具体法条的端到端处理，已在PyPI发布，具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Statutory references are central to legal language understanding, but are difficult to process automatically, as they appear in compact and variable surface forms, may combine multiple targets, use special abbreviations, and often point to lower-level units. Existing tools for German focus either on parsing references from legal documents or accessing statutory text once citations are explicit. This paper introduces bundesrecht, an open resource for German statutory reference processing, consisting of a software library and a structured corpus of German federal law. The library parses, normalizes, and resolves German statutory references, mapping raw citation strings to structured objects, expanding compact references into canonical forms, and linking them to statutory provisions. The accompanying dataset preserves the internal hierarchy of statutes from laws to fine-granular subclauses. We evaluate the parser and normalizer on 2,944 annotated German legal references using strict exact-match and micro information extraction metrics. We further evaluate canonical reference deduplication and show that normalized references group real citation surface variants far more reliably than string matching. bundesrecht is the first open resource that covers German statutory reference processing as an end-to-end pipeline, from raw citation string to resolved statutory provision, and is available on PyPI.

</details>


### [157] [FBHM: Functional Benchmarking and Steering of VLMs for Hateful Meme Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31349)
*Paramananda Bhaskar,Naquee Rizwan,Daksh Jogchand,Saurabh Kumar Pandey,Animesh Mukherjee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有仇恨模因检测基准存在结构性偏差，混淆修辞仇恨机制与目标群体特征，导致无法对模型漏洞进行因果评估，亟需一个更科学、可解释的评测框架和改进方法。

Method: 构建沿25种修辞功能与10个目标群体正交设计的FBHM基准；采用可学习的引导向量（LSV）方法，在极低数据条件下通过因果干预目标优化模型，实现对仇恨语义的精准识别。

Result: 主流视觉-语言模型在标准数据集上表现良好，但在FBHM上性能急剧下降，表明其依赖数据集特定启发式；应用LSV后，FBHM上的宏平均F1得分提升约30点，且不损害源域性能，优于上下文学习与参数高效微调（PEFT）。

Conclusion: FBHM为仇恨模因检测提供了可解释、因果驱动的评估基准，而LSV作为一种高效低数据策略，有效缓解了模型泛化能力不足的问题，推动视觉-语言模型向更鲁棒的方向发展。

Abstract: Hateful meme detection remains a formidable challenge for vision-language models, as existing benchmarks are structurally observational - confounding rhetorical hate mechanisms with target community features and preventing causal evaluation of model vulnerabilities. To address this, we introduce FBHM, a systematically curated benchmark of Functionality Based Hateful Memes constructed along two orthogonal axes: 25 distinct rhetorical functionalities and 10 target communities (5,000 memes total). Benchmarking state-of-the-art VLMs reveals a severe generalization gap: models highly accurate on standard datasets catastrophically drop to near-random performance on FBHM, proving they exploit dataset-specific heuristics rather than robust multimodal reasoning. To efficiently close this gap, we propose LSV (learnable steering vectors), an ultra-low data regime strategy that applies a causal intervention objective on as few as 500 steering samples (50 unique base memes), boosting FBHM performance by ~30 Macro-F1 points while outperforming in-context learning and PEFT without degrading source-domain performance.

### [158] [A Visually Impaired Assistance Benchmark for VLM-as-a-Judge Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31351)
*Yi Zhao,Siqi Wang,Zhe Hu,Yushi Li,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出VIABLE基准，用于评估视觉语言模型（VLM）在视障辅助（VIA）任务中作为评判者的能力。研究发现现有模型在有效性、公正性和稳定性方面均不可靠，最强模型GPT-5.4诊断准确率仅52.6%，且存在高自我偏好。为此，作者提出VIA-Judge-Agent，一种模型无关的推理时增强框架，通过视觉证据提取和分类引导流程提升判断准确性与用户偏好。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: AI-based Visually Impaired Assistance (VIA) remains challenging, largely due to the high cost of human evaluation. The VLM-as-a-Judge paradigm may offer a promising alternative, although it has mostly been studied in general domains. We therefore ask whether such judges can be trusted for VIA tasks. To investigate this question, we introduce VIABLE (Visually Impaired Assistance Benchmark for VLM-as-a-Judge Evaluation), the first benchmark for VLM-as-a-Judge evaluation in VIA. VIABLE contains over 300K judgment samples across three scenarios and introduces an Effectiveness--Impartiality--Stability framework with a 12-mode failure taxonomy. Based on VIABLE, our systematic study of seven judges across different model scales shows that existing models are largely unreliable across all evaluation axes. The strongest judge, GPT-5.4, achieves only 52.6% single-failure diagnostic accuracy, yet exhibits the highest self-preference rate at 94.2%; while open-source judges are strongly biased and adversarially fragile. To address these issues, we propose VIA-Judge-Agent, a model-agnostic inference-time harness that augments judges with visual evidence extraction and a taxonomy-guided workflow. ### [159] [Unlocking Fine-Grained Translation Quality Estimation in LRMs through Synergistically Evolving Implicit and Explicit Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31378)
*Renfei Dang,Xinye Wang,Zhejian Lai,Weilu Xu,Shimin Tao,Daimeng Wei,Min Zhang,Shujian Huang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大推理模型在细粒度翻译质量评估任务上表现不佳，尽管具备强多语言能力，但核心挑战在于任务本身的复杂性，需同时增强隐式与显式推理能力。

Method: 设计两阶段训练框架：(1) NonThinking-SFT，无推理链的监督微调以强化隐式推理；(2) Thinking-RLVR，基于可验证奖励的强化学习以增强显式推理。通过分解任务使隐式推理可行，并实现两种推理能力的协同进化。

Result: 在WMT测试集上，基于Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507的RIEQE在显式推理性能上超越所有基线，隐式推理能力也达到当前编码器类模型最佳水平，且二者存在相互促进的协同效应。

Conclusion: RIEQE框架有效实现了隐式与显式推理的协同进化，为提升大模型在细粒度翻译质量评估中的表现提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) still struggle with fine-grained translation quality estimation (QE), even with long reasoning chains. We argue that LRMs already possess strong multilingual capabilities, while the core challenge stems from the intrinsic difficulty of learning the fine-grained QE task. In this paper, we propose RIEQE (Reasoning both Implicitly and Explicitly for QE), a simple two-stage training framework that enables the co-evolution of implicit (layer-wise) and explicit (token-wise) reasoning capabilities. To make implicit reasoning feasible, we first decompose the complex QE task into straightforward subtasks. Based on this, our two-stage approach applies: (1) NonThinking-SFT, Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) without reasoning chains to directly boost the model's implicit reasoning tendency and capability; and (2) Thinking-RLVR, standard Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Reward (RLVR) to subsequently strengthen explicit reasoning. Results demonstrate that implicit and explicit reasoning synergistically co-evolve under our framework. On the WMT test sets, RIEQE based on Qwen3-4B-Thinking-2507 surpasses all baselines in explicit reasoning performance, while its implicit reasoning capability is also comparable to the best current encoder-based models. We further provide evidence for the synergistic collaboration between implicit and explicit reasoning, showing how they mutually benefit each other.

Abstract: We evaluate the consistency of automated judges in conducting a multi-dimensional safety evaluation in a reference-free setup. Conclusion: 这是首个将大语言模型生成的目标侧改写及LLM-as-a-Judge评估应用于符号语言翻译的研究，证明了目标侧增强在改善翻译质量方面的潜力，尤其在语义层面。然而，其效果受数据分布特性制约，未来需结合更鲁棒的建模方式。

Abstract: Sign language translation (SLT) remains constrained by limited paired sign-video/text corpora and heavy-tailed target vocabularies. We study target-side augmentation in which GPT-4o generates controlled paraphrase variants of reference sentences while the sign input remains unchanged. A Signformer-style pose-based Transformer is trained under a two-stage schedule: pre-training on the augmented corpus followed by fine-tuning on the original references.
  We evaluate on three datasets spanning complementary challenges: PHOENIX14T (German Sign Language), with moderate lexical diversity; GSL (Greek Sign Language), with highly ontrolled, repetitive recordings; and LSA-T (Argentinian Sign Language), with severe long-tail sparsity. The semantic evaluation reveals gains in fidelity that lexical overlap metrics understate.

### [163] [The Sword, Shield, and Achilles' Heel: Characterizing the Linguistic Inductive Bias of Large Language Models for Spatial Reasoning in Navigation Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31404)
*Xudong Zhang,Jian Yang,Shengkai Wang,Jiangpeng Tian,Shaowen Chen,Xian Wei,Ke Li,Xiong You*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种双干预框架，用于分离语言结构与不同上下文线索，以评估大语言模型（LLM）在导航规划中的语言归纳偏置。通过表示干预和上下文干预，发现拓扑信息是稳健规划的核心，语言格式具有双刃剑效应，而语义信息若错误则会严重破坏规划过程。研究建议应保持拓扑完整性、适配模型能力的压缩程度，并确保语义正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于大语言模型的导航系统通常将空间表示转换为文本输入，但其语言结构和上下文特征的选择常被视为中立的工程决策，忽视了它们对模型行为的关键影响。因此，亟需系统评估语言结构与上下文线索如何塑造LLM的导航能力。

Method: 提出双干预性框架：表示干预改变语言格式与压缩程度，探究语言表达对导航的影响；上下文干预结合特征组合与冲突探测，揭示模型对拓扑、几何、语义等线索的偏好与弱点。

Result: 实验表明：拓扑信息是鲁棒规划的基石；语言格式的影响取决于模型规模、任务需求和压缩水平；错误的语义信息会系统性破坏规划流程。

Conclusion: 有效的基于文本的空间表示应保留拓扑完整性，根据模型能力调节表示压缩，并确保语义正确性，而非采用单一表示形式。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based navigation systems commonly construct explicit spatial representations (e.g., topological graphs, semantic raster maps) and translate them into textual descriptions as LLMs' inputs. However, the linguistic structures of such text-based spatial representations and the choices of contextual features (e.g., topology, geometry) they contain are often treated as neutral engineering decisions rather than key factors that shape LLMs' behavior. To fill the gap, we propose a dual-interventional framework that disentangles linguistic structures from different contextual cues to evaluate the linguistic inductive bias of LLMs for navigation planning. In the framework, representation intervention varies the linguistic format and the degree of linguistic compression, clarifying when linguistic representations support or inhibit navigation planning. Context intervention, combined with contextual feature combination and conflict probing, explicitly clarifies the preferences and weaknesses of LLMs when processing different contextual cues. Experiments across diverse spatial reasoning tasks and multiple model scales reveal a consistent pattern: topological information is a sturdy shield and the backbone of robust planning; linguistic format is a double-edged sword whose effect depends on model size, task demands, and the compression level; and semantic information is a fatal Achilles' heel -- incorrect semantic cues can systematically derail the planning process. Overall, our study shows that effective text-based spatial representations in LLM-based navigation should preserve topological integrity, calibrate representational compression to model capacity, and ensure semantic correctness, rather than simply adopting a single representation. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/jonesdong150/LLM-Navigation-Inductive-Bias.

### [164] [SCOPE: Self-Play via Co-Evolving Policies for Open-Ended Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31433)
*Wai-Chung Kwan,Aryo Pradipta Gema,Joshua Ong Jun Leang,Pasquale Minervini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SCOPE 是一种无需数据的自洽学习框架，用于开放性任务，通过协同进化挑战者（生成文档驱动的任务）和求解者（多轮检索回答）两个策略，并利用初始模型的冻结副本作为自评者生成任务特定评分标准并评估求解者输出。在三个7-8B指令微调模型上，SCOPE 在八个基准测试中提升开放性任务性能最高达+10.4分，表现媲美甚至超过基于约9000个精心设计提示训练的GRPO_data。即使仅在开放性任务上训练，其在七个保留的短形式问答基准上也提升最高达+13.8分，且在所有三个模型上均超越GRPO_data。消融实验表明：挑战者与求解者的协同进化对维持任务难度在求解者能力边界至关重要；性能提升来自检索与合成两方面的改进，贡献比例因任务而异；评分标准生成质量是自评环节的瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自洽学习方法依赖可规则检查的答案，难以适用于开放性任务；而开放性任务通常需依赖人工设计提示或前沿模型作为评判者，成本高且可扩展性差。因此，亟需一种无需外部标注数据、能自主生成任务与评价标准的自洽学习框架，以推动开放性任务的高效训练。

Method: 提出SCOPE框架，包含两个协同进化的策略：挑战者（Challenger）从文档中生成开放性任务，求解者（Solver）通过多轮检索进行回答；使用初始模型的冻结副本作为自评者，根据源文档生成任务特定评分标准，并对求解者输出进行评分；整个过程无需外部标注数据，实现完全自洽的训练闭环。

Result: 在三个7-8B模型（Qwen2.5、Qwen3、OLMo-3）上，SCOPE在八个开放性任务基准上平均提升达+10.4分，性能接近或超过基于9000个精心设计提示训练的GRPO_data；在七个保留的短形式问答任务上，性能提升最高达+13.8分，全面超越GRPO_data；消融实验证明挑战者协同进化的重要性，以及检索与合成双方面贡献的差异性，同时指出评分标准生成质量是当前主要瓶颈。

Conclusion: SCOPE成功实现了无需外部数据的自洽学习，可在开放性任务上显著提升语言模型性能，且具备泛化能力，可间接提升短形式问答能力。该框架为构建高效、可扩展的自监督训练范式提供了新路径，但评分标准生成质量仍需进一步优化。

Abstract: Self-play can train language models without external supervision. However, existing methods require rule-checkable answers, leaving open-ended tasks dependent on curated prompts or frontier-model judges. We introduce SCOPE, a data-free self-play framework for open-ended tasks that co-evolves two policies: a Challenger that generates document-grounded tasks, and a Solver that answers them through multi-turn retrieval. A frozen copy of the initial model serves as the self-judge, which writes task-specific rubrics from the source document and grades Solver responses against them. Across three 7-8B instruction-tuned models (Qwen2.5, Qwen3, OLMo-3), SCOPE improves open-ended performance by up to +10.4 points on eight benchmarks and matches or exceeds GRPO_data trained on ~9K curated prompts. Although trained only on open-ended tasks, SCOPE also improves held-out short-form QA by up to +13.8 points on seven held-out benchmarks, surpassing GRPO_data on all three models. Ablations show that co-evolving the Challenger is necessary to keep tasks near the Solver's frontier, that gains arise from improvements in both retrieval and synthesis with the relative contribution varying by task, and that rubric generation quality is the bottleneck for self-judging.

</details>


### [165] [Fine-grained Verification via Diagnostic Reasoning Supervision for Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31446)
*Wenna Lai,Haoran Xie,Guandong Xu,Qing Li,S. Joe Qin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出FiVeD框架，用于细粒度验证方面情感三元组提取（ASTE）结果。通过多任务学习，包括有效性分类、质量评分估计、错误类型分类和理由生成，实现对候选三元组的精细筛选与重排序。利用大语言模型结合特定评估标准生成质量分数和诊断理由，支持可调节精度-召回率权衡。实验表明，作为即插即用模块，FiVeD在多个基线模型上将性能提升最高达3.53 F1点。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出FiVeD框架，采用多任务训练策略，包含有效性分类、质量评分估计为主任务，错误类型分类和理由生成为辅助任务；构建基于语义与句法约束的伪错误三元组，利用预训练大模型结合任务专用评分标准生成质量分数与诊断理由。

Conclusion: FiVeD通过细粒度验证与诊断推理监督，有效提升了ASTE系统的可靠性与实用性，为复杂文本理解任务中的输出可信度保障提供了新思路。

Abstract: Aspect Sentiment Triplet Extraction (ASTE) aims to identify aspect terms, opinion terms, and sentiment polarities as structured triplets, providing essential inputs for downstream information system applications such as opinion mining, explainable recommendations, and review summarization. Prior work mainly focuses on end-to-end extraction, while post hoc verification of extracted triplets remains comparatively underexplored. This gap limits the reliability of ASTE systems, since predicted triplets may be locally plausible while being globally invalid. Moreover, candidate invalidity is multi-faceted and candidate usability is inherently graded, motivating a fine-grained verification mechanism that can filter or re-rank outputs from diverse extractors. In this paper, we propose FiVeD, a framework for Fine-grained Verification with Diagnostic reasoning supervision. Specifically, the verifier is trained with multiple complementary objectives, including validity classification and quality score estimation as primary tasks, with error type classification and rationale generation as auxiliary tasks. We define hierarchical error categories and construct plausible incorrect triplets under semantic and syntactic constraints, and leverage an off-the-shelf LLM with task-specific rubrics to produce quality scores and diagnostic rationales. During inference, the resulting quality scores are used to filter candidate outputs, supporting adjustable precision-recall tradeoffs. Experiments across multiple ASTE baselines demonstrate that FiVeD consistently improves extraction performance by up to 3.53 F1 points as a plug-and-play verification module.

Method: 提出BEA-Dialogue+，放宽原语料库中实验者与对话伙伴间的分割限制，同时确保主说话人完全分离；采用Whisper和FastConformer模型进行测试，并引入序列输出训练（SOT）进行微调，系统评估不同数据规模下的模型性能。

Result: BEA-Dialogue+提供200小时自然对话数据，模型在未微调情况下对更大数据更具挑战性，而经过SOT微调后，所有指标（WER、CER、cpWER、cpCER）均获得一致提升，验证了其有效性与实用性。

Abstract: Conversational automatic speech recognition in Hungarian is constrained by the limited amount of publicly available dialogue-style training data. The BEA-Dialogue corpus addresses this need, but its strictly speaker-disjoint train/dev/eval split reduces the usable material to only 85 hours. In this paper, we introduce BEA-Dialogue+, an expanded version of the corpus that relaxes the split criterion for experimenters and dialogue partners while preserving complete separation of the primary speakers. This results in 200 hours of transcribed natural conversations and enables a controlled study of the trade-off between additional training data and speaker overlap across the splits. We evaluate several Whisper- and FastConformer-based models on both corpus versions, including Serialized Output Training (SOT)-based fine-tuning for dialogue transcription. Our results show that the larger corpus is more challenging for models without fine-tuning, whereas SOT-based adaptation yields consistent improvements in WER, CER, cpWER, and cpCER. Overall, BEA-Dialogue+ provides a substantially larger yet still demanding benchmark for Hungarian dialogue ASR, and a practical resource for training and evaluating dialogue transcription systems.

### [168] [Language Models Can Resolve Reference Compositionally, But It's Not Their Native Strength: The Case of the Personal Relation Task](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31480)
*Bart Evelo,Meaghan Fowlie,Denis Paperno*

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在自然语言语义解释中的组合能力，通过个人关系任务评估人类与LLMs在指称性（Extensional）和意向性（Intensional）任务上的表现。结果发现，人类在指称任务上优于意向性任务，而LLMs则相反，表明LLMs缺乏参照性接地，是其模仿人类语言理解的关键缺失部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用个人关系任务（Paperno 2022），要求被试解释如“Amber's parent's friend”这类名词短语，分别评估指称性任务（确定具体所指对象）和意向性任务（生成结构化表达式，如friend(parent(amber))）。对人类与多种大型语言模型进行对比测试。

Result: 人类在指称性任务上表现优于意向性任务，而大型语言模型则在意向性任务上显著优于指称性任务，表明模型在结构化语义表示上较强，但在实际指称推理上存在明显不足。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型缺乏参照性接地，是其无法实现类人语言理解的关键原因；未来模型的发展需引入更有效的指称训练机制以提升真实语义理解能力。

Abstract: Do neural models, such as Large Language Models, genuinely acquire compositional abilities for interpretation of natural language? When we talk about semantic interpretation, we can distinguish two complementary aspects: establishing what an expression refers to in the world (which we call the Extensional task) and representing its sense in a structured way (which we call the Intensional task). We evaluate LLMs and humans on both tasks in the setting of the Personal Relation Task (Paperno 2022) in which, given a universe of people and their relationships with each other, one is asked to interpret a noun phrase such as "Amber's parent's friend". Here, for the Intensional task, the answer is the formula "friend(parent(amber))", and for the Extensional task, the person. We find that humans and LLMs show opposite strengths: humans perform better on Extensional than Intensional tasks, and LLMs vice versa. Our methodology brings greater nuance to the understanding of compositional abilities in modern machine learning models. Our results support the notion that the lack of referential grounding in LLM training is a crucial missing component in mimicking human-like language understanding.

### [169] [BenHalluEval: A Multi-Task Hallucination Evaluation Framework for Large Language Models on Bengali](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31483)
*Shefayat E Shams Adib,Ahmed Alfey Sani,Ekramul Alam Esham,Ajwad Abrar,Ishmam Tashdeed,Md Taukir Azam Chowdhury*

Result: BenHalluScore显示各模型在任务间幻觉校准差异显著（7.72%–55.42%），链式思维提示未能一致改善幻觉识别能力，表明单一评估轨道和仅靠提示的方法不足以准确评估低资源语言模型的幻觉行为。

Conclusion: BenHalluEval是首个面向孟加拉语的幻觉评估基准，揭示了当前评估范式在低资源语言中的不足，强调需要更全面、多维度的评估机制。相关数据与代码已公开。

Abstract: Despite Bengali being the sixth most spoken language in the world, no prior work has systematically evaluated hallucination in large language models (LLMs) for Bengali. We introduce BenHalluEval, a fine-grained hallucination evaluation framework for Bengali covering four tasks: Generative Question Answering (GQA), Bangla-English Code-Mixed QA, Summarization, and Reasoning. We construct 12,000 hallucinated candidates using GPT-5.4 across twelve task-specific hallucination types, drawn from three existing Bengali datasets, and evaluate seven LLMs spanning reasoning-oriented, multilingual, and Bengali-centric categories under a dual-track protocol that independently measures false-positive rate on ground-truth instances (Track A) and hallucination detection rate on hallucinated candidates (Track B). To jointly penalise both failure modes and prevent inflated scores from uniform response bias, we propose BenHalluScore, a dual-track calibration metric that ranges from 7.72% to 55.42% across models and tasks, revealing substantial variation in hallucination calibration. Chain-of-thought prompting, applied as a mitigation strategy, shifts response distributions without consistently improving hallucination discrimination. BenHalluEval establishes the first dedicated hallucination benchmark for Bengali and highlights the inadequacy of single-track and prompting-only evaluation approaches for low-resource language settings. The dataset and code are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/BanglaHalluEval-EB77.

### [170] [Are Full Rollouts Necessary for On-Policy Distillation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31490)
*Yaocheng Zhang,Jiajun Chai,Songjun Tu,Yuqian Fu,Xiaohan Wang,Wei Lin,Guojun Yin,Qichao Zhang,Yuanheng Zhu,Dongbin Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出两种控制滚动视野的简单策略：渐进式有监督蒸馏（POPD）和截断式有监督蒸馏（TOPD），以解决标准有监督蒸馏（OPD）中因生成完整轨迹而导致的计算开销大和后期反馈不可靠的问题。实验表明，POPD可将训练效率提升达3倍，TOPD仅用10%的滚动视野即可达到与完整OPD相当的性能，显著降低运行时间和内存消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准有监督蒸馏（OPD）在训练过程中通常生成完整的轨迹，这不仅计算成本高，且早期训练时后期位置的教师反馈可能不可靠。本文旨在通过控制滚动视野来提升训练效率并改善反馈质量。

Method: 提出两种策略：渐进式OPD（POPD）逐步扩展滚动视野；截断式OPD（TOPD）永久使用可靠的截断轨迹进行蒸馏。

Result: POPD使OPD训练效率提升最多达3倍；TOPD仅需10%的滚动视野即可达到与完整OPD相当的性能，大幅减少墙钟时间与内存占用。

Conclusion: 控制滚动视野是一种简单而有效的提升有监督蒸馏效率的方法，为长时序推理任务中的高效训练提供了可行路径。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) provides dense teacher feedback along rollouts generated by the student and has emerged as a promising post-training paradigm for long-horizon reasoning. However, standard OPD typically generates full rollouts during training, which is computationally expensive and may expose the student to unreliable teacher feedback at late rollout positions, especially during early training. We identify the rollout horizon as a key bottleneck in OPD that substantially impacts training efficiency. Unlike Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), OPD does not require a complete trajectory or a final answer reward to provide learning signals. This observation suggests that full rollouts may not always be necessary for effective OPD. Motivated by this insight, we propose two simple horizon-control strategies: Progressive OPD (POPD), which gradually expands the rollout horizon during training, and Truncated OPD (TOPD), which permanently performs distillation on reliable truncated rollouts. Experiments on mathematical reasoning show that POPD improves the training efficiency of OPD by up to 3$\times$, while TOPD matches OPD performance using only 10\% of the rollout horizon, leading to substantial wall-clock and memory reductions. These results demonstrate that controlling the rollout horizon offers a simple and practical path to more efficient OPD.

### [171] [Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations for LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31494)
*Zheyu Zhang,Shuo Yang,Gjergji Kasneci*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CoRP提出了一种无需梯度的模型整合方法，通过奖励加权聚合和兼容性感知重加权，将多个受奖励的扰动模型合并为单一可部署模型，显著提升性能并减少推理开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如RandOpt虽在匹配计算下表现良好，但依赖多前向传播的预测级集成，不适用于自由生成任务，且效率较低。本文旨在探索如何将奖励的模型集合压缩为单个可部署模型，以实现高效推理。

Method: 提出CoRP（Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations），利用低秩结构进行奖励加权聚合，结合兼容性感知重加权与验证集门控机制，完全避免语言模型中的梯度流动。

Result: 在0.5B至8B的五种语言模型上，针对数学、代码和创意写作等五项任务，CoRP平均提升8.1点；仅使用1/10的扰动预算即超过单次推理的RandOpt 6.5点，并恢复超过50次多数投票集成一半以上的增益，且只需一次前向传播。

Conclusion: CoRP成功将奖励模型集合转化为一个高效、可部署的单一模型，在保持高性能的同时极大降低推理成本，是后训练阶段的一种有效替代方案。

Abstract: Post-training of language models is commonly framed as a sample-score-update loop implemented by gradient descent. A recent line of work, exemplified by RandOpt, relocates this loop to weight space, sampling Gaussian perturbations around a pretrained model and ensembling the top-K rewarded specialists at inference. While competitive with PPO and GRPO under matched training compute, this prediction-level ensemble incurs K forward passes per test example and does not extend cleanly to free-form generation. We ask whether the rewarded population can instead be folded into a single deployable model, replacing the inference-time ensemble with one consolidated update. A split-half analysis over 25 model-task pairs reveals reproducible low-rank structure in every case. We turn this geometry into CoRP (Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations), a gradient-free operator that combines reward-weighted aggregation, compatibility-aware reweighting, and a held-out validation gate, with no gradient flowing through the language model. Across five language models from 0.5B to 8B and five tasks covering math, code, and creative writing, CoRP improves the base model by 8.1 points on average. Using one tenth of RandOpt's perturbation budget, CoRP exceeds single-inference RandOpt by 6.5 points and recovers more than half of the gain of the 50-pass majority-vote ensemble, at one forward pass per test example.

</details>


### [172] [Reliable Multilingual Orthopedic Decision Support from Clinical Narratives: Language-Aware Adaptation and Verification-Guided Deferral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31512)
*Danish Ali,Li Xiaojian,Sundas Iqbal,Farrukh Zaidi*

Main category: cs.CL

Abstract: Multilingual orthopedic decision support remains challenging in low-resource healthcare settings, where clinical narratives contain specialized terminology, mixed scripts, incomplete evidence, label imbalance and language-dependent documentation patterns. This article presents a reliability-oriented framework for classifying free-text orthopedic notes in English, Hindi and Punjabi. We compare task-aligned multilingual transformer encoders, a task-fine-tuned DistilBERT baseline, zero-shot instruction-tuned large language models (LLMs) and a domain-adaptive encoder, IndicBERT-HPA. IndicBERT-HPA augments IndicBERT with language-aware orthopedic adapter heads to support clinically relevant multilingual representation learning. Evaluation extends beyond aggregate accuracy to per-class performance, ROC-AUC, AUPRC, expected calibration error, cross-language stability and robustness under controlled balanced and natural-prevalence distributions. Under natural clinical prevalence, IndicBERT-HPA achieves the strongest overall performance, reaching an averaged Macro-F1 of 0.8792, Macro-AUROC of 0.894 and AUPRC of 0.902. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出语义-声学原型（SAP），将音频分解为语言内容、发音属性和听觉场景原语；设计语义-声学平衡（SAE）机制，通过内容感知门控自适应恢复浅层中的精细声学细节。

Result: UniAudio-Token在保留高质量语音生成能力的同时，学习到全面的通用音频表示，在下游理解和生成任务中显著优于所有单码本基线分词器。

Abstract: Semantic speech tokenizers have become a widely used interface for Audio-LLMs, owing to their compact single-codebook design and strong linguistic alignment. However, their focus on linguistic abstraction induces acoustic blindness, limiting their applicability beyond speech-centric tasks. We propose UniAudio-Token, a framework that empowers semantic tokenizers with general audio perception without compromising speech ability. Instead of altering the semantic paradigm, UniAudio-Token mitigates its information loss through two key innovations: (1) Semantic-Acoustic Primitives (SAP) provide structured supervision by decomposing audio into linguistic content, vocal attributes, and auditory-scene primitives; and (2) Semantic-Acoustic Equilibrium (SAE) introduces a content-aware gating mechanism that adaptively restores fine-grained acoustic details from shallow layers. Extensive evaluations show that UniAudio-Token learns comprehensive universal representations while preserving high-fidelity speech generation. When integrated with downstream LLMs, it outperforms all single-codebook baseline tokenizers on both understanding and generation tasks, effectively serving as a unified audio interface. We publicly release all our code, including training and inference scripts, together with the model checkpoints at https://github.com/Tencent/Universal_Audio_Tokenizer.

### [174] [Preference-Aware Rubric Learning for Personalized Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31545)

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为PARL（Preference-Aware Rubric Learning）的个性化评估框架，将个性化评估视为学习问题而非静态判断。通过从用户交互历史中学习偏好感知的评分标准，并结合判别式强化学习，有效捕捉用户特定的决策边界，实现对个性化文本生成的高保真评估。实验表明，该方法在跨用户和任务上具有良好的泛化能力，能稳定识别用户偏好的响应模式。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法无法有效捕捉用户长期交互历史中嵌入的主观、个性化偏好，导致个性化对齐评估成为瓶颈。因此需要一种更可靠、更具区分性的个性化评估方法。

Method: 提出PARL框架，将个性化评估建模为学习问题；通过从原始用户历史中学习偏好感知的评分标准，并采用自验证机制确保与用户偏好的一致性；结合判别式强化学习，对比用户生成内容与个性化模型输出，以精确捕捉用户决策边界。

Result: PARL在真实个性化文本生成任务中表现出色，能够持续生成高保真度的评分标准，准确识别符合用户偏好的响应，且在不同用户和任务间具有良好泛化能力，可稳定捕捉风格偏好和细微评价模式。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) evolve from general-purpose assistants to user-centric agents, personalization has become central to aligning model behavior with individual preferences, making the evaluation of personalized alignment a critical bottleneck. Existing evaluation methods-ranging from automatic metrics to LLM-as-a-judge approaches-fail to capture subjective, user-specific preferences embedded in long-term interaction histories. We identify three essential principles for reliable and effective personalized evaluation: Representativeness, User-Consistency, and Discriminativeness. To address these principles, we introduce Personalized Evaluation as Learning, a paradigm that formulates personalized evaluation as a learning problem rather than a static judgment. Under this paradigm, we propose PARL (Preference-Aware Rubric Learning for Personalized Evaluation), a framework that learns to induce preference-aware evaluation rubrics directly from raw user histories and performs a self-validation mechanism to ensure consistency with the user's preferences. PARL integrates rubric induction with a discriminative reinforcement learning objective that contrasts user-authored responses against competitive personalized model outputs, enabling the learned rubrics to capture precise, user-specific decision boundaries. Experiments on real-world personalized text generation tasks show that PARL consistently induces high-fidelity rubrics that reliably identify user-aligned responses and generalize across users and tasks, while capturing stable stylistic preferences and fine-grained evaluative patterns. To ensure reproducibility, our code is available at https://github.com/SnowCharmQ/PARL.

### [175] [Semantic Triplet Restoration: A Novel Protocol for Hierarchical Table Understanding in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31550)
*Yibin Zhao,Fangxin Shang,Dingrui Yang,Yuqi Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出Semantic Triplet Restoration (STR)协议，将表格单元格重写为原子事实三元组（项目路径、特征路径、值），并引入轻量级查询感知路由器TripletQL，选择适合问题的三元组子集。在多个中英文表格问答基准上，STR在减少输入标记数的同时达到或超越基于HTML的基线性能，尤其在小型模型和长表格上下文下优势更明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表格问答方法依赖HTML或Markdown等布局序列化表示，导致标记开销大且需大模型推断行列跨度与标题对齐关系。本文旨在通过显式语义三元组表示降低推理复杂度，提升效率与可扩展性。

Method: 提出STR协议，将每个表格单元格转换为结构化三元组 <项目路径, 特征路径, 值>，其中项目路径标识行级实体，特征路径表达层级属性；结合TripletQL查询路由机制，根据问题动态筛选相关三元组，实现高效精准的语义检索。

Result: 在四个中英文表格问答基准上，STR在保持甚至超越基线性能的同时显著减少输入长度；对小型语言模型和长表场景效果提升更明显，验证了显式语义表示在资源受限条件下的有效性。

Conclusion: STR通过显式语义三元组重构表格内容，配合轻量级查询路由，有效降低模型推理负担，提升表格问答的效率与可扩展性，尤其适用于低资源环境。

Abstract: Table question answering requires models to recover semantic relations encoded implicitly by two-dimensional layout, merged cells, and hierarchical headers. Current pipelines typically use HTML or Markdown as intermediate table representations, but these layout-oriented serializations introduce markup overhead and require large language models to infer header-cell alignments from row and column spans. We propose Semantic Triplet Restoration (STR), a protocol that rewrites each cell as an atomic fact <item path, feature path, value>, where the item path specifies the row-wise entity, the feature path specifies the hierarchical attribute, and the value contains the cell content. We also present TripletQL, a lightweight query-aware router that uses STR to select an appropriate rendering or filtered subset of triplets for each question. Across four Chinese and English table-QA benchmarks, STR matches or improves upon HTML-based baselines while reducing input tokens. The relative benefit grows for smaller language models and longer table contexts, suggesting that explicit semantic representations are especially useful under constrained inference budgets. Code and data are available at https://github.com/Phoenix-ni/STR.git .

### [176] [What Am I Missing? Question-Answering as Hidden State Probing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31561)
*Chu Fei Luo,Samuel Dahan,Xiaodan Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型在测试时的推理过程，提出通过提问作为推理干预手段，利用学生-教师框架训练探测器来预测最终答案正确性。结果显示，提问过程中模型自我诊断的信号比从教师获取信息更具预测价值。进一步将提问建模为序列决策问题，设计门控策略以提升正确率，但发现诊断与修正之间存在差距：干预既可能修复错误轨迹，也可能损害正确轨迹，反映出模型在不确定性下自我修正能力的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在测试时推理过程中的可解释性和稳定性仍不明确，尤其在相同输入下多次采样会产生不同答案。如何有效干预并提升推理可靠性成为关键挑战。本文旨在探索通过提问实现模型自我诊断和纠错的可能性，揭示其内在机制与局限性。

Method: 采用学生-教师设置，让学生在推理过程中向教师提问；训练一个探测器分析学生隐藏状态变化，评估其对最终答案正确性的预测能力；将提问建模为序列决策问题，使用探测器输出作为质量评分，设计门控策略决定是否提问以最大化正确性。

Result: 探测器能有效预测答案正确性，且信号主要来自模型自身提问时的自我诊断而非教师反馈；门控策略虽能识别不确定性和错误，但干预行为对正确轨迹有同等破坏风险，表明诊断与修正间存在显著脱节。

Conclusion: 提问作为一种测试时干预手段，虽能反映模型内部状态并辅助判断，但其纠正能力受限于模型自洽性，难以实现有效自我修正，凸显了当前语言模型在不确定性下自我精炼的深层瓶颈。

Abstract: Test-time reasoning has become a significant field of study since the introduction of chain-of-thought reasoning in large language models (LLMs). However, the mechanisms of this reasoning process are still under-explored -- from the same input prompt, and even the same partial solution, LLMs can produce varied answers if sampled multiple times. We propose to leverage question-asking as an inference-time intervention that articulates information about the model's hidden state. To achieve that, we present a student-teacher setting where a student asks questions to a teacher. We train a probe on the student's hidden state before and after asking a question and find it is predictive of the trajectory's final correctness, even before generating the teacher's answer. This suggests there is a meaningful signal from the self-diagnosis that occurs during question generation rather than information transfer from the teacher. We then frame question-asking as a sequential decision problem, using this probe as a quality score, and define a gating policy to ask questions that maximize likelihood of correctness. We find that the success of question-asking as an intervention is largely dependent on the model's self-consistency. Our empirical results show a gap between detection and recovery; while our gating policy captures model correctness and uncertainty, interventions are equally likely to harm correct trajectories as they are to recover incorrect ones. This gap between diagnosis and correction has broader implications on language models' capacity for self-refinement under uncertainty.

### [177] [Disagreeing Rationales: Rethinking Classification and Explainability Evaluation in Hate Speech Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31563)
*Benedetta Muscato,Beiduo Chen,Gizem Gezici,Barbara Plank,Fosca Giannotti*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过系统重实现不同模型与训练策略，将各类方法统一于一个监督框架中；在分类任务中采用预测性和分布性两个核心指标，在可解释性上引入合理性、忠实度与复杂度三个维度；对比硬、中间及软三种标签与理由表示空间下的性能表现。

Result: 实验结果表明，无论是分类还是可解释性指标，软表示均表现更优，证明其能更好地捕捉人类判断的多样性；同时，评估指标对标签与理由表示的选择敏感，提示应摒弃仅依赖硬标签或多数投票的传统做法。

Conclusion: 在主观自然语言处理任务中，软表示能更有效地反映人类判断的多样性，建议重构模型评估体系，避免过度依赖硬标签与简单聚合方式，以更真实反映人类推理的复杂性。

Abstract: Human disagreement is ubiquitous and well-known in labeling. However, variation in explanations, captured through token-level human rationales, remains far less explored. At the same time, it is unclear how to best evaluate human labels and rationales -- or even how to best aggregate rationales beyond majority vote -- in light of this variation. Yet, rationales may provide additional insights into the richness of human reasoning, that may differ in style, values and interpretations -- especially in subjective NLP tasks like hate speech detection. In this work, we unify diverse models, training strategies, loss functions, and existing evaluation metrics under a single protocol by systematically re-implementing them across different label and rationale representation spaces. Classification metrics are organized around two key properties -- predictive and distributional -- while explainability metrics through three complementary dimensions: plausibility, faithfulness, and complexity. In this unified supervision framework, we evaluate model behavior across classification and explainability metrics, as well as metric sensitivity to the choice of label (hard and soft) and rationale representation space (hard, intermediate and soft). Results show that both hard and soft metrics favor softer representations, highlighting their effectiveness in capturing variation and the need to rethink evaluation in subjective NLP.

### [178] [What Gets Unmasked First? Trajectory Analysis of Diffusion Models for Graph-to-Text Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31564)
*Qing Wang,Jacob Devasier,Chengkai Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了用于图到文本生成的掩码扩散语言模型（MDLMs）。研究发现，与自回归语言模型线性生成不同，MDLMs会优先生成实体，随后是关系词和功能词，最后处理结构化标记。此外，研究揭示了监督微调（SFT）的一种未被记录的失败模式：它过早地固定了句尾结构标记，导致输出长度被锁定，从而引发信息遗漏或幻觉。为此，作者提出了一种无需训练的推理时修正方法——lambda缩放结构解码，通过降低结构标记置信度，恢复了+9.4 BLEU-4性能。同时引入Graph-LLaDA，将图变换器编码器集成到LLaDA解码流程中，显式利用图结构关系。跨数据集评估显示，先前基线模型对特定数据集过拟合，而基于LLM和MDLM的方法具有更强泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图到文本生成方法在生成策略和泛化能力上存在不足，特别是监督微调导致生成轨迹异常，且基线模型泛化能力差。需要一种能有效利用图结构、保持自然生成顺序并提升泛化性的新方法。

Method: 提出lambda缩放结构解码（训练-free推理修改），通过降低结构标记置信度来恢复自然生成顺序；设计Graph-LLaDA框架，融合图变换器编码器以显式建模图结构关系。

Result: lambda缩放结构解码使模型性能提升+9.4 BLEU-4；Graph-LLaDA在跨数据集评估中显著优于现有基线，展现出更强的泛化能力。

Conclusion: MDLMs在图到文本生成中具有天然优势，其生成轨迹更符合人类认知逻辑。通过合理干预生成过程（如lambda缩放）和结构建模（如Graph-LLaDA），可有效克服监督微调带来的问题，并显著提升模型泛化能力。

Abstract: We present the first systematic study of masked diffusion language models (MDLMs) for graph-to-text generation. We analyze MDLM generation trajectories -- the order in which tokens are unmasked during iterative decoding -- and find that, unlike autoregressive LLMs which generate text linearly, MDLMs naturally prioritize entities first, followed by relational and function words, with structural tokens resolved last. We further identify a previously undocumented failure mode of supervised fine-tuning: SFT disrupts this strategy by prematurely anchoring structural sentence-ending tokens early in the decoding trajectory, effectively fixing the output length which can lead to omitted or hallucinated information. To address this, we propose lambda-scaled structural decoding, a training-free inference-time modification that downweights structural token confidence and recovers +9.4 BLEU-4. Finally, we introduce Graph-LLaDA, which integrates a Graph Transformer encoder into LLaDA's decoding process to explicitly incorporate relational graph structure. Cross-dataset evaluation on LAGRANGE reveals that previous baselines overfit to dataset-specific patterns, while LLM- and MDLM-based approaches generalize significantly better.

</details>


### [179] [Language Models Learn Constructional Semantics, Not To Mention Syntax: Investigating LM Understanding of Paired-Focus Constructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31586)
*Wesley Scivetti,Ethan Wilcox,Nathan Schneider,Kanishka Misra,Leonie Weissweiler*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了开源语言模型对罕见语法结构（如'let alone', 'much less'）的语义理解能力，发现一些参数量适中的模型能够准确理解这些结构的形式与意义，而大规模人类数据训练的模型表现不佳。研究还发现，语义理解在训练后期才出现，且与世界知识的提升相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究开源语言模型是否具备对罕见语法构造的鲁棒理解能力，以及其背后的学习动态机制。

Method: 构建了一个针对英语中罕见配对焦点结构的新数据集，通过标量形容词语义和通用世界知识测试模型理解能力；对比不同参数量、架构和预训练数据规模的多种模型，并分析开放检查点模型的训练过程以观察学习动态。

Result: 若干中等规模的开源模型能敏感地识别配对焦点结构的形式与意义，但基于人类规模数据训练的模型在所有语义评估中均失败。语义理解出现晚于句法知识，且与世界知识的提升存在关联。

Conclusion: 中等规模的开源模型具备理解罕见配对焦点结构的能力，且其语义掌握与更广泛的世界知识存在联系。

Abstract: Grasping the semantics of rare constructions (form-meaning pairings) has been shown to be a challenging problem that has currently only been solved by the largest LLMs. It remains an open question if open-source models have robust constructional understanding, and if so, what learning dynamics underlie the acquisition of this knowledge. Focusing on a set of rare Paired-Focus constructions in English (e.g. "let alone", "much less"), we construct a novel dataset to test their meanings using both scalar adjectival semantics and general world knowledge. Testing a wide range of models differing in parameter count, architecture, and pretraining dataset size, we find that several modestly sized models are sensitive to both the forms and the meanings of Paired-Focus constructions, though models trained on human-scale data fail at all meaning evaluations. Turning to training dynamics for a set of open-checkpoint models, we find that Paired-Focus understanding emerges later in training than Paired-Focus syntactic knowledge, and that learning of Paired-Focus semantics is correlated with gains in some domains of world knowledge. Overall, our empirical results support the conclusion that modestly sized open-source models can grasp the rare Paired-Focus constructions, and demonstrate a connection between knowledge of Paired-Focus constructions and other meaning domains.

### [180] [Gait2Hip-60: A Unified Deep Learning Benchmark for Predicting Hip Muscle Forces and Joint Moments from Multi-Cadence Gait Kinematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30374)
*Jiaqi Zhang,Ji Hou,Qing Sun,Xianzhi Gao,Bo Huo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种深度学习框架，通过下肢步态运动学数据直接预测髋部肌肉力和关节力矩，比较了LSTM、Transformer和Mamba三种序列模型。在60名健康成年人的多步速数据上训练并评估模型，结果显示Transformer在预测性能上最优，且在无重新训练的外部患者队列（9例股骨头坏死患者）中仍保持一定预测能力，验证了从步态运动学推断髋部动力学的可行性，支持Transformer作为基准模型，但需进一步验证其在更广泛病理情况下的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统肌肉骨骼仿真虽能提供髋部肌肉力和关节力矩信息，但耗时且难以在临床环境中应用。因此，亟需一种高效、可推广的方法来快速估计这些关键生物力学参数。

Method: 采用深度学习方法，使用10个双侧下肢关节角度作为输入，以OpenSim生成的髋部肌肉力和关节力矩为输出标签，对LSTM、Transformer和Mamba三种序列模型进行统一协议下的训练与评估。采用基于受试者的划分策略，并使用相同的预处理流程和评价指标。

Result: 在健康人群基准测试中，Transformer在预测髋部肌肉力（RMSE = 1.33 N/kg, MAE = 0.57 N/kg, R2 = 0.819）和髋关节力矩（RMSE = 0.11 Nm/kg, MAE = 0.07 Nm/kg, R2 = 0.862）方面表现最佳；在零样本外部验证中，对股骨头坏死患者群体仍具备中等预测能力（肌肉力：RMSE = 1.51 N/kg, MAE = 0.70 N/kg, R2 = 0.537；关节力矩：RMSE = 0.17 Nm/kg, MAE = 0.12 Nm/kg, R2 = 0.569）。

Conclusion: 从下肢步态运动学数据中直接预测髋部动力学参数是可行的，Transformer模型展现出优越性能，可作为未来临床应用的有力候选，但其在不同病理状态下的泛化能力仍需更大规模验证，以推动实际应用落地。

Abstract: Estimating hip muscle forces and joint moments during gait typically relies on musculoskeletal simulation, which is informative but time-consuming and difficult to apply in clinical settings. This study developed a deep learning framework to predict these hip dynamics parameters directly from lower-limb gait kinematics and compared three representative sequence models under a unified protocol. Gait data were collected from 60 healthy adults under three metronome-guided cadence conditions. Ten bilateral lower-limb joint angles were used as inputs, and OpenSim-derived hip muscle forces and hip joint moments were used as reference outputs. Three deep learning models of LSTM, Transformer, and Mamba were trained and evaluated using the same subject-level split, preprocessing pipeline, and metrics. The best model was then directly tested on an external cohort of 9 patients with osteonecrosis of the femoral head (ONFH) without retraining. In the healthy-subject benchmark, Transformer achieved the best subject-level mean performance for both hip muscle force prediction (RMSE = 1.33 N/kg, MAE = 0.57 N/kg, R2 = 0.819) and hip joint moment prediction (RMSE = 0.11 Nm/kg, MAE = 0.07 Nm/kg, R2 = 0.862), with similar advantages across walking cadences. In zero-shot external validation, Transformer retained moderate predictive ability in ONFH for hip muscle force prediction (RMSE = 1.51 N/kg, MAE = 0.70 N/kg, R2 = 0.537) and hip joint moment prediction (RMSE = 0.17 Nm/kg, MAE = 0.12 Nm/kg, R2 = 0.569). These findings support the feasibility of estimating hip dynamics from gait kinematics, identify Transformer as a strong baseline, and highlight the need for broader pathological validation and improved generalization before clinical application.

### [181] [Unicorn: Scaling High-Dimensional Time Series Forecasting via Universal Correlation Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30376)
*Haochen Yuan,Yichen Song,Yunbo Wang,Xiaokang Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Unicorn提出了一种新的时间序列建模框架，通过引入潜在原型码本，将不同通道的依赖关系解耦，实现跨数据集、跨维度的可扩展预训练，显著提升了少样本迁移场景下的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间序列模型在可扩展性与表达能力之间存在权衡：独立通道模型虽能处理大量数据但忽略通道间依赖；依赖通道模型虽表达能力强但受限于维度，难以泛化到异构数据集。因此需要一种既能保持可扩展性又能捕捉跨通道交互的新方法。

Method: Unicorn采用潜空间中的原型码本，将不同通道映射到共享的潜在空间中，学习与通道身份无关的通用交互模式，从而实现跨域、跨维度的可迁移特征表示。

Result: 实验表明，Unicorn在多种任务上显著优于现有先进模型，尤其在少样本迁移场景下表现突出，为构建多变量时间序列基础模型提供了可行路径。

Conclusion: Unicorn成功解决了高维时间序列建模中的可扩展性与表达力之间的矛盾，通过无身份依赖的关联建模，实现了跨数据集、跨维度的有效知识迁移，是迈向多变量时间序列基础模型的重要一步。

Abstract: Modern time series architectures face a fundamental trade-off: channel-independent models scale well with increasing data volume but ignore critical inter-channel dependencies, while channel-dependent models are expressive but remain ``dimension-bounded'', struggling to generalize across heterogeneous datasets.To bridge this gap, we introduce Unicorn (Universal Correlation Network), a framework for scalable, multi-dataset pretraining on high-dimensional time series. At the core of Unicorn is a latent prototype codebook that decouples correlation modeling from specific channel identities. By projecting heterogeneous channels into a shared latent space, UniCorN learns identity-agnostic, reusable interaction patterns that transfer across domains with diverse dimensionalities and semantics. Extensive experiments show that Unicorn significantly outperforms state-of-the-art forecasting architectures, particularly in few-shot transfer scenarios, offering a scalable path toward multivariate time series foundation models.

</details>


### [182] [When LLMs Learn to Be Consistently Wrong: A Multi-Model Study of Linear Representations of Synthetic Deception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30381)
*Vahideh Zolfaghari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过在多个Transformer模型（Pythia-1.4B、Gemma-2-2B/9B、Qwen2.5-7B、Llama-3.1-8B）上使用LoRA进行微调，构建了诚实与欺骗变体的多模型范式，探究合成欺骗的表征基础。线性探测器在四类架构的前1-3层即可近乎完美地检测出欺骗行为（AUC ≥ 0.99），而Pythia-1.4B在第1层达到0.705峰值。逻辑回归探测器表现优于或相当甚至超越MLP探测器，支持线性表征假设。在TruthfulQA上的探测结果可泛化至未见的MMLU领域，误差极小（Delta AUC≈0）。深层表示对高斯噪声具有强鲁棒性，尤其以Gemma-2系列最为稳定。机制分析显示，模型呈现两种表征模式：Pythia/Llama/Qwen出现表征坍缩，而Gemma-2保持高维表征；所有模型中欺骗方向随深度逐步强化，且在1-4层即可实现极佳校准（ECE < 0.01，除Pythia外）。结果表明，仅需少量监督微调即可快速建立稳健、跨域一致的欺骗表征，对基于激活的监控具有重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究合成欺骗（synthetic dishonesty）作为学习欺骗的受控实验平台，旨在理解其内部表征基础，为应对更复杂的策略性欺骗提供理论支持和监测方法。

Method: 采用多模型范式，对五种Transformer模型使用LoRA进行微调，生成诚实与欺骗版本；利用线性探针（如逻辑回归、MLP）分析均池化隐藏状态，评估欺骗检测能力；通过跨域泛化测试、噪声鲁棒性实验及机制分析（如Fisher判别比、有效秩、中心点几何、方向稳定性、跨域对齐、校准度量等）深入揭示表征特性。

Result: 线性探针在早期层即可高精度检测欺骗（多数AUC≥0.99）；逻辑回归探测器性能优于或匹配MLP；探测结果在不同任务间高度泛化（Delta AUC≈0）；深层表示对噪声鲁棒性强，尤其是Gemma-2系列；模型表现出两种表征模式：表征坍缩（Pythia/Llama/Qwen）与高维保留（Gemma-2）；欺骗方向在深层持续强化，且1-4层即可实现优异校准（ECE<0.01，除Pythia）。

Conclusion: 通过少量监督微调即可迅速建立稳健、跨域一致的欺骗表征，且其核心信息可在浅层被高效捕捉，表明基于激活的监控具备可行性，同时揭示了不同模型在表征结构上的本质差异，为未来安全机制设计提供了关键线索。

Abstract: Deceptive alignment, in which models maintain accurate internal representations while deliberately producing false outputs, remains a central challenge in AI safety. While strategic deception is the primary long-term concern, synthetic dishonesty - induced via direct optimization on incorrect answers - provides a controlled testbed for studying the representational basis of learned deception. We introduce a multi-model paradigm in which honest and deceptive variants of five transformer models (Pythia-1.4B, Gemma-2-2B/9B, Qwen2.5-7B, Llama-3.1-8B) are fine-tuned using LoRA on the same question distribution. Linear probes trained on mean-pooled hidden states detect synthetic dishonesty with near-perfect AUC (greater than or equal to 0.99) as early as layers 1-3 in four architectures, while Pythia-1.4B reaches a peak of 0.705. Logistic regression probes consistently match or outperform MLP probes, supporting the Linear Representation Hypothesis. Probes trained on TruthfulQA generalize with near-zero loss (Delta AUC approx. 0) to held-out MMLU subjects. Late-layer representations show strong robustness to Gaussian noise, with Gemma-2 models exhibiting exceptional stability. Mechanistic analysis of Fisher Discriminant Ratio, effective rank, centroid geometry, directional stability, cross-domain alignment, and calibration (ECE) reveals two regimes: representational collapse in Pythia/Llama/Qwen versus high-dimensional preservation in Gemma-2. Across all models, the dishonesty direction consolidates progressively in deeper layers, with optimal calibration (ECE less than 0.01 except Pythia) achievable in layers 1-4. These results demonstrate that robust, domain-invariant dishonesty representations can be rapidly entrenched via modest supervised fine-tuning, with implications for activation-based monitoring.

</details>


### [183] [A Novel Evaluation Metric for Unsupervised Learning in AIS-Based Maritime Anomaly Detection: MADQI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30388)
*Ismet Gocer,Zakirul Bhuiyan,Raza Hasan,Shakeel Ahmad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的系统性框架，用于检测海上自动识别系统（AIS）数据中的异常行为，包括速度异常、位置跳跃、时间间隙和转向角异常。针对现有无监督学习方法（如孤立森林）缺乏系统评估指标的问题，作者引入了名为海事异常检测质量指数（MADQI）的新综合评价指标，该指标无需标签数据即可评估模型性能。MADQI由四个相互关联的指标组成：异常率一致性（ARC）、物理合理性评分（PPS）、得分分布分离度（SDS）和极端案例证据（ECE），并通过多块评估与自适应缩放实现自动归一化。实验结果表明，该框架在真实AIS数据集上取得了80.37%的MADQI得分，尤其在检测极端异常和保持异常率一致性方面表现优异（分别达到0.907和1.000）。整体结果验证了该框架在无监督异常检测中具备可靠性和有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无监督学习算法在检测船舶异常行为时虽广泛应用，但普遍缺乏系统且有意义的评估手段，难以客观衡量模型性能。因此亟需一种不依赖标注数据的、可量化评估异常检测效果的综合指标。

Method: 基于哈弗辛距离分析AIS数据，结合空间与行为特征识别异常；提出MADQI作为综合评估指标，整合四类子指标（ARC、PPS、SDS、ECE），通过多块评估与自适应缩放实现自动归一化处理。

Result: 实验结果显示，所提框架在真实AIS数据集上获得80.37%的MADQI得分，其中极端案例证据（ECE）为0.907，异常率一致性（ARC）达1.000，表明其在检测极端异常及维持异常率稳定性方面表现卓越。

Conclusion: 该框架为无监督海事异常检测提供了可靠且具有意义的评估路径，有效弥补了现有方法在评估维度上的不足，具备实际应用价值。

Abstract: This paper introduces a new systematic framework for detecting anomalies in maritime Automatic Identification System (AIS) datasets. These anomalies include abnormal vessel behaviours related to speed, position jumps, time gaps, and turn angles. Although unsupervised learning algorithms such as Isolation Forest are widely used for detecting anomalous vessel movements, they often lack systematic and meaningful evaluation measures. To address this limitation, we propose a novel quality metric called Maritime Anomaly Detection Quality Index (MADQI). The prosed MADQI is a composite index designed to evaluate the anomaly detection performance of machine learning models without requiring labelled data. The proposed framework uses Haversine distance calculations to analyse AIS datasets and identify anomalies based on their spatial and behavioural characteristics. The proposed MADQI evaluation framework integrates four interconnected metrics: Anomaly Rate Consistency (ARC), Physical Plausibility Score (PPS), Score Distribution Separation (SDS), and Extreme Case Evidence (ECE). These metrics are combined through automatic normalisation using multi-chunk evaluation and adaptive scaling techniques. Experimental results on the AIS dataset show that the proposed framework achieved a MADQI score of 80.37%, demonstrating its effectiveness for unsupervised anomaly detection. In particular, the algorithm performed strongly in identifying abnormal vessel behaviour. Among the individual MADQI components, ECE and ARC achieved scores of 0.907 and 1.000, respectively, indicating excellent capability in detecting extreme anomalies and maintaining anomaly rate consistency. Overall, these results are encouraging and demonstrate that the proposed framework provides a reliable and meaningful approach for evaluating unsupervised anomaly detection in maritime AIS data.

### [184] [NumLeak: Public Numeric Benchmarks as Latent Labels in Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30393)
*Anany Kotawala*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出NumLeak框架，用于检测大语言模型在预训练中对公开数值基准的记忆现象。实验发现顶级大模型对Fama-French市场超额收益等经济指标的记忆准确率极高（皮尔逊相关系数0.97-0.99），但新数据集上解析率下降，表明存在记忆偏差。白盒实验验证了剂量-响应关系，且日志概率排名可检测到开放生成难以捕捉的记忆信号，说明黑盒探测低估了记忆通道。通过残差化处理后，模型自回忆显著削弱了其与真实市场情绪的相关性，证明记忆是主要预测因素。此外，仅一行系统提示即可有效防御非自适应攻击，几乎无成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法依赖时间条件测试，可能误将记忆召回当作泛化能力，因此需要一种能区分记忆与推理的新方法。

Method: 结合API边界探测与白盒控制验证，使用开放因果语言模型进行对照实验，并通过日志概率排序和残差分析识别记忆行为。

Result: 前沿大模型在多个宏观经济指标上表现出极强的记忆能力，新数据上解析率下降但相关性仍高；白盒实验复现了剂量-响应模式，日志概率可检测未被生成捕捉的记忆；系统提示可高效防御攻击。

Conclusion: 当前大模型在公开数值数据上存在严重记忆泄露，评估需警惕记忆混淆；简单的系统提示可有效缓解风险。

Abstract: Public numeric benchmarks appear in pretraining, so an evaluation that conditions on a date may be measuring memorized recall rather than out-of-sample skill. We introduce NumLeak, a measurement framework that combines API-boundary probes on production models with a white-box controlled validation on an open causal LM. Top-tier frontier LLMs recall the Fama-French market excess return at 3-seed pooled Pearson r=0.97-0.99 while staying within 0.15 within-25bps on the five sibling factors; comparable fidelity appears on U.S. unemployment, CPI inflation, and NOAA temperature. On a recent-release holdout, parse rate collapses to 21-57% but r stays at approximately 0.99 on months answered, the refuse-or-recall asymmetry a memorized channel predicts. The white-box experiment reproduces the dose-response, and logprob ranking detects memorization that open-ended generation misses, implying closed-API black-box probes understate the channel. A Sonnet "date to market-sentiment" regression that correlates with true Mkt-RF at r=0.74 collapses to r=0.02 once the model's own recall is residualized out. A one-line system-prompt defense blocks 99.8% of a non-adaptive single-turn suffix attack set at near-zero utility cost on conceptual and historical-narrative queries
