### [185] [LongDS-Bench: On the Failure of Long-Horizon Agentic Data Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30434)
*Kewei Xu,Xiaoben Lu,Shuofei Qiao,Zihan Ding,Haoming Xu,Lei Liang,Ningyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LongDS is a new benchmark for long-horizon, multi-turn data analysis that evaluates agents' ability to maintain and update analytical states over extended interactions. It consists of 68 real-world tasks from Kaggle notebooks across six domains, with an average dependency span of 11.3 turns. The benchmark tests complex state-evolution patterns like counterfactuals and rollbacks. Evaluation of five top models reveals low performance (best: 48.45% accuracy), significant decline over time (~47-point drop), and long-horizon errors causing 52–69% of failures. Results suggest the main challenge lies in state maintenance, not interaction depth. Code and data are publicly available.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing benchmarks fail to evaluate agents' ability to handle long-horizon, iterative data analysis tasks, especially tracking evolving analytical context. Real-world data analysis is inherently iterative, requiring agents to manage state changes across many turns, which current evaluations do not adequately test.

Method: LongDS is constructed from real-world Kaggle notebooks, curated into 68 tasks across six domains (Geoscience, Business, Education, etc.). Tasks involve complex state-evolution patterns such as counterfactual perturbation, rollback, and multi-state composition. Each task spans up to hundreds of turns, with an average dependency span of 11.3 turns. The benchmark evaluates model performance across multiple turns, focusing on state consistency and evolution.

Result: The best-performing model achieved only 48.45% average accuracy. Performance dropped nearly 47 points from early to late turns. Long-horizon errors accounted for 52%–69% of all failures. Increasing agent steps did not improve results, indicating that maintaining accurate analytical state is the core challenge.

Conclusion: LongDS effectively exposes the limitations of current agents in long-horizon data analysis, particularly in state maintenance. The benchmark enables future research on building more reliable, context-aware agentic systems for real-world data tasks. The dataset and code are open-sourced to support further progress.

Abstract: Real-world data analysis is inherently iterative, yet existing benchmarks mostly evaluate isolated or short interactive tasks, leaving agents' ability to track evolving analytical context over long horizons untested. We introduce LongDS, a benchmark for long-horizon, multi-turn data analysis where agents must maintain, update, restore, and compose evolving analytical states. LongDS comprises 68 tasks constructed from real-world Kaggle notebooks, spanning 2,225 turns across six domains including Geoscience, Business, and Education. Tasks are designed around state-evolution patterns (e.g., counterfactual perturbation, rollback, multi-state composition), with an average dependency span of 11.3 turns. Evaluating five state-of-the-art models, we find that the best model reaches only 48.45% average accuracy, performance drops nearly 47 points from early to late turns, and long-horizon errors account for 52%--69% of failures. Further analysis shows that additional agent steps do not necessarily improve performance, suggesting that the key bottleneck is maintaining a correct analytical state rather than increasing interaction budget. We release LongDS to support research on reliable long-horizon agentic data analysis. Code and data will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/DataMind.

</details>


### [186] [Calibrated Preference Learning: The Case of Label Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30447)
*Santo M. A. R. Thies,Viktor Bengs,Timo Kaufmann,Sebastian J. Vollmer,Eyke Hüllermeier*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究未正式处理概率标签排序的校准问题，而直接将排序视为类别会忽略其结构信息，无法捕捉成对关系或top-k预测等关键特性，因此需要建立合适的校准框架以支持更可靠的决策。

Method: 提出一个分层校准框架，包括全排序、子排序和top-k排序的校准定义；通过理论分析揭示各层级间的包含关系及不可比较性；设计相应的评估指标并应用于主流标签排序模型和RLHF奖励模型进行实证分析。

Result: 实验表明当前主流标签排序模型普遍存在校准不足，子排序与top-k校准度差异显著；在RLHF奖励模型中，校准性与基准准确率高度相关但非完全一致，说明校准反映的是独立于准确性的重要质量维度。

Conclusion: 校准是概率标签排序中不可或缺的质量指标，应被纳入模型评估体系；未来工作需进一步探索校准偏差的下游影响并发展有效的校准修正方法。

Abstract: Calibration, the alignment of predicted probabilities with true outcome frequencies, is essential for reliable decision-making. While extensively studied for classification and regression, calibration has not been formally addressed for probabilistic label ranking, where the goal is to predict a distribution over orderings of a label set. Naively treating rankings as classes ignores their structure and fails to capture important modalities such as pairwise and top-k predictions. We formalize calibration for label ranking and develop a hierarchy of notions covering full rankings, sub-rankings, and top-k rankings. We prove that full-rank calibration implies the others but not conversely, and sub-ranking and top-k calibration are incomparable. Empirically, we find popular label ranking models are often poorly calibrated, with substantial differences between sub-ranking and top-k metrics. Applying our framework to RLHF reward models, we find that calibration correlates strongly but not perfectly with benchmark accuracy, suggesting it captures a meaningful quality dimension beyond top-1 accuracy. These findings motivate future work on understanding the downstream effects of miscalibration and developing methods to correct it.

### [187] [Bounded Behavioral Indistinguishability for Black-Box LLM Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30448)
*Munawar Hasan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的评估范式——有界行为不可区分性（$(ε,q,t,\mathbb{A})$-behavioral indistinguishability），用于更严格地评估黑盒大模型蒸馏效果。通过在Qwen和Llama师生对上使用5000个受控提示的探测集，研究发现尽管LoRA蒸馏提升了语义相似度（如Qwen从0.788升至0.862），但对抗性评估仍揭示出显著的行为差异，主要集中在风格、格式、鲁棒性和领域技术提示等方面。此外，基于不同家族模型的判别器和一致性过滤验证了蒸馏后仍有可区分性。查询预算实验表明，分歧引导采样并不优于分层随机采样，说明覆盖与多样性仍是强基线。结论：仅追求语义相似性不足，需引入对抗性、类别感知和有界评估以全面衡量蒸馏质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑盒大模型蒸馏评估主要依赖输出相似性或任务一致性，但这种评估方式无法确保学生模型在行为上与教师完全不可区分。为更真实地衡量蒸馏效果，亟需一种能捕捉细微行为差异的评估框架。

Method: 提出有界行为不可区分性形式化定义，并构建5000个受控提示的探测套件；在Qwen和Llama师生对上对比基础学生与LoRA蒸馏学生；采用对抗性判别器、成对分类分析、跨家族判断和一致性过滤等手段评估区分能力；进行查询预算实验比较分歧引导与分层随机采样。

Result: LoRA蒸馏虽提升语义相似度（Qwen: 0.788→0.862；Llama: 0.814→0.874），但对抗性评估显示仍有显著行为差异；判别器保持非零优势，差异集中于风格/格式、鲁棒性及技术类提示；跨家族判别中Qwen的区分优势从0.158降至0.081；分歧引导采样未显著优于分层随机采样。

Conclusion: 语义保真度虽重要但不足以保证蒸馏质量；黑盒大模型蒸馏必须结合有界、对抗性和类别感知的综合评估方法，才能真正实现行为层面的不可区分性。

Abstract: Black-box LLM distillation is usually evaluated as an output-matching problem: a student is considered successful when its responses are semantically similar to, or task-consistent with, those of a teacher. However, output similarity does not imply that the student is behaviorally indistinguishable from the model it imitates. We introduce bounded behavioral indistinguishability, formalized as $(ε,q,t,\mathbb{A})$-behavioral indistinguishability over an explicit prompt distribution, where $ε$ bounds distinguishing advantage, $q$ bounds oracle queries, $t$ bounds computation, and $\mathbb{A}$ denotes the adversary class.
  We instantiate this notion on Qwen and Llama teacher-student pairs using a controlled $5,000$-prompt behavioral probe suite. For each family, we compare the teacher with both the base student and the LoRA-distilled student, measuring whether distillation reduces distinguishability rather than merely improving similarity. LoRA raises semantic similarity from $0.788$ to $0.862$ for Qwen and from $0.814$ to $0.874$ for Llama. Yet adversarial evaluation reveals remaining behavioral differences: learned discriminators retain nonzero advantage, and pairwise category analysis shows artifacts concentrated in style/format, robustness, and domain-technical prompts. A pairwise teacher-identification adversary confirms this trend. With a different-family Llama judge and A/B-swap consistency filtering, Qwen distinguishing advantage drops from $0.158$ for the base student to $0.081$ after LoRA distillation. Query-budget experiments show that disagreement-guided acquisition does not consistently outperform stratified random sampling, indicating that coverage and diversity remain strong baselines. Our results show that semantic fidelity is useful but insufficient: black-box LLM distillation requires bounded, adversarial, and category-aware evaluation.

### [188] [VeriGate: Verifier-Gated Step-Level Supervision for GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30451)
*Aakriti Agrawal,Minghui Liu,Furong Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VeriGate improves GRPO by adding verifier-gated step-level credit assignment, using future-cumulated PRM rewards and token-level advantages to enhance exploration, reduce zero-gradient issues, and resist reward hacking.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO suffers from sparse supervision when all trajectories get the same verifier reward, leading to stalled learning. Outcome-only rewards lack step-level credit assignment, hindering exploration and robust reasoning. VeriGate addresses these issues with a more adaptive and fine-grained reward mechanism.

Method: VeriGate introduces verifier gating: it uses verifier rewards when they provide meaningful preference; otherwise, it switches to process supervision. It converts PRM step scores into future-cumulated rewards and transforms them into group-normalized token-level advantages for better credit assignment and gradient informativeness.

Result: On MATH with 1.5B and 7B Qwen2.5-Instruct models, VeriGate boosts average accuracy by ~20% and ~12% respectively, reduces zero-gradient failures, decreases reward-hacking, and improves reasoning quality compared to outcome-only GRPO and PRM-as-outcome baselines.

Conclusion: VeriGate effectively overcomes the limitations of traditional GRPO by enabling dynamic use of verifier and process rewards, providing fine-grained credit assignment and stable training, making it a superior approach for training reasoning models.

Abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is an effective recipe for training reasoning models with verifier-based outcome rewards, but its supervision is sparse: when all sampled trajectories for a prompt receive the same verifier reward, the group-relative advantage collapses to zero and learning stalls. Outcome-only rewards also provide no step-level credit assignment, limiting exploration and making it harder to learn robust reasoning. We present VeriGate (Verifier-Gated Step-Level GRPO), a verifier-gated extension of GRPO that addresses these limitations with three design choices. First, VeriGate keeps the verifier in charge whenever verifier rewards induce a meaningful preference among sampled trajectories, and uses process supervision only when verifier rewards are degenerate. Second, instead of collapsing Process Reward Model (PRM) step scores into a single trajectory reward, VeriGate converts them into future-cumulated rewards to assign continuation-aware credit. Third, VeriGate transforms these rewards into group-normalized token-level advantages, restoring informative gradients and fine-grained credit assignment while remaining less susceptible to reward hacking than methods that optimize aggregated PRM scores. Empirically, training on MATH with 1.5B and 7B Qwen2.5-Instruct models and evaluating on six reasoning benchmarks, VeriGate improves average accuracy by about 20% and 12% for 1.5B and 7B models respectively, substantially reduces zero-gradient failures, decreases reward-hacking behavior, and improves reasoning quality relative to outcome-only GRPO and PRM-as-outcome baselines.

</details>

Method: 提出统一的梯度聚合框架，引入充分对齐条件，利用对偶锥投影保证可行性，从原始优化角度分析算法关系并设计新方法。

Abstract: Many machine learning problems involve multiple inherent trade-offs that are best addressed by gradient-based multi-objective optimization (MOO) algorithms. Existing methods are often proposed with various motivations, analyzed case by case, and differ algorithmically in how the component gradients are aggregated at each step. In this work, we develop a unifying framework for gradient aggregation in MOO, establishing (optimal) rates of convergence to Pareto stationarity, the standard measure of performance in MOO. Central to our analysis is a sufficient alignment condition, from which we derive a theorem showing that non-conflicting directions, when chosen within the convex hull of gradients, form a fundamental sufficient condition for convergence. We further show that feasibility can be ensured through projection onto the dual cone, broadening the scope of methods that admit convergence guarantees. In parallel, we present a primal optimization perspective of gradient aggregation that encompasses established algorithms, clarifies their theoretical relationships, and enables the design of new variants. As an illustration, we introduce capped MGDA, derived from a CVaR-based formulation, and demonstrate its robustness in adversarial federated learning. Finally, we validate our theory through experiments on synthetic problems and practical benchmarks.

### [190] [Scalable Constrained Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning via State Augmentation and Consensus for Separable Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30461)
*Santiago Amaya-Corredor,Miguel Calvo-Fullana,Anders Jonsson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种分布式约束多智能体强化学习方法，结合状态增强策略学习与对偶变量的分布式一致性机制。该方法适用于具有可分动力学但需协调满足全局资源约束的系统，克服了独立学习因无法确定个体贡献而导致不可行解的问题。核心创新在于证明仅通过轻量级邻居间对偶变量共识即可实现全局约束协调，同时保持独立训练的可扩展性。每个智能体离线学习一个依赖于本地状态和对偶变量（编码约束反馈）的增强策略；执行时通过局部通信达成对偶变量的一致。理论证明在弱连通性假设下，共识误差有界，且约束违反程度随图连通性和共识轮数增加而减小。相比中心化训练、去中心化执行（CTDE）方法，本方法在训练和执行阶段均呈线性扩展，实验表明：无共识则需求被无限推迟，无法满足约束；有共识时，智能体收敛至共享对偶变量，同时满足电网约束与需求，可扩展至数千智能体，而CTDE仅限数十个。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 独立学习在具有全局资源约束的多智能体系统中无法保证可行解，因为智能体无法判断自身对集体约束的适当贡献。需要一种既能保持可扩展性又可实现全局协调的分布式方法。

Method: 结合状态增强策略学习与对偶变量的分布式一致性机制。每个智能体学习一个依赖于本地状态和对偶变量的策略；执行时通过轻量级邻居间通信达成对偶变量一致，从而实现全局约束协调。

Result: 所提方法在智能电网需求响应任务中验证有效：无共识时，系统只能通过无限推迟需求来满足约束，为退化解；有共识时，智能体能收敛到共享对偶变量，同时满足电网容量约束与需求，且可扩展至数千智能体，而传统CTDE方法受限于几十个智能体。

Conclusion: 该方法通过轻量级对偶变量共识实现了全局约束协调，兼具理论保障与实际可扩展性，是解决大规模约束多智能体问题的有效方案。

Abstract: We present a distributed approach for constrained Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) that combines state-augmented policy learning with distributed consensus over dual variables. Our method targets systems where agents have separable dynamics but must coordinate to satisfy global resource constraints, a setting in which, as we demonstrate empirically, independent learning fails to produce feasible solutions because agents cannot determine appropriate individual contributions toward collective constraint satisfaction. The key technical contribution is showing that lightweight neighbor-to-neighbor consensus over Lagrange multipliers suffices for globally coordinated constraint enforcement while preserving the scalability of independent training. Each agent learns a single augmented policy offline, conditioned on both its local state and a dual variable encoding constraint feedback. During execution, agents reach agreement on this dual variable through local communication alone. We prove that under mild connectivity assumptions, the consensus error among agents' multipliers is bounded, and show that this translates to a bounded constraint violation that decreases with graph connectivity and the number of consensus rounds. Unlike centralized training with decentralized execution (CTDE) approaches, whose complexity grows at least quadratically with agent count, our method scales linearly in both training and execution. Experiments on smart grid demand response demonstrate that consensus coordination is \emph{essential for feasibility}: without it, agents satisfy grid capacity constraints only by indefinitely postponing demand, a degenerate non-solution. With consensus, agents converge to a shared dual variable and satisfy both grid constraints and demand fulfillment, scaling to thousands of agents while CTDE baselines are limited to dozens.

### [191] [idSCD: Identifying Training Datasets through Semantic Correlation Descriptors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30462)
*Andrada Gobeaja,Ionut Hodoroaga,Elena Burceanu,Marius Leordeanu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了能否通过模型在训练过程中产生的伪相关性来识别数据集。提出一种基于语义相关性描述符（SCD）的白盒语义指纹方法，能够捕捉模型学习到的语义相关结构，并在不同数据集混合中进行比较。在留一数据集排除的诊断实验中，SCD能完美区分匹配与非匹配的数据集对。进一步提出一种基于SCD的实用成员推理分数，仅需模型的SCD和目标数据集的独立SCD即可判断目标数据集是否属于模型训练集，无需留一模型。在自然语言推理、情绪分类和医疗文本分类三个场景下，该方法平均表现最优，显著优于黑盒基线（RMIA、Attack-P、LiRA）和白盒基线SIF，尤其在数据集间语义差异明显时，ROC-AUC提升超过60%。

Method: 提出语义相关性描述符（SCD），用于刻画模型在训练中形成的语义相关结构；设计白盒成员推理框架，利用模型SCD与目标数据集独立SCD的对比，实现无需留一模型的数据集归属判断；通过留一数据集排除实验和多场景测试验证有效性。

Result: 在多个实验设置中，基于SCD的成员推理方法在平均性能和标准差上均表现最佳，显著超越黑盒与白盒基线方法；当数据集间具有明显的语义差异时，相对性能提升超过60%（以ROC-AUC衡量）。

Conclusion: 模型内部学习的语义相关结构可以作为数据集的“语义指纹”，通过分析这些内部表征，能够有效识别数据集成员身份，且在语义差异较大的情况下效果尤为突出，表明语义相关性是数据集痕迹的重要体现。

Abstract: Can a dataset be recognized from the spurious correlations it induces during training? We argue that datasets leave dataset-specific traces in a model's learned semantic correlation structure: incidental regularities that are predictive within a dataset, but not causal for the underlying task, can be internalized during training. We use this insight to study dataset-level membership inference, moving beyond existing methods that rely on behavioral or distributional evidence such as confidence scores, losses, margins, generated samples, or query responses. We introduce a white-box semantic fingerprinting approach based on semantic correlation descriptors (SCDs), which capture the semantic correlation structure learned by a model and make it comparable across dataset mixtures. In a controlled leave-one-dataset-out diagnostic, SCDs recover dataset-specific changes and perfectly separate matching from non-matching dataset pairs. We then propose a practical SCD-based membership score that tests whether a target dataset is part of a model's training mixture using only the model's SCD and the target dataset's standalone SCD, without requiring leave-one-dataset-out models. Across three diverse experimental settings, with dataset groups for natural language inference, emotion classification, and medical text classification, we test both the advantages and limitations of SCD-based membership inference with different degrees of semantic separation and keyword support between dataset splits. On average, the classifier based on this score achieves the highest performance and the lowest std, outperforming black-box baselines RMIA, Attack-P, and LiRA, as well as the white-box SIF baseline. These results show that dataset membership can be traced through internal semantic correlations, with the largest relative gain exceeding 60% in ROC-AUC when dataset groups expose distinct semantic particularities.

Method: 提出一种基于解释输出的模型提取攻击方法：(1) 利用模型解释结果指导蒙特卡洛边敏感性估计，结合霍夫丁不等式保证估计精度；(2) 通过分析解释子图有效缩小决策边界搜索空间，从而高效重构目标模型。

Result: 在多个领域基准图数据集上的大量实验表明，所提方法在模型提取精度和效率方面均显著优于现有基线，验证了其有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: 可解释性接口虽提升AI透明度，但可能成为模型提取攻击的可利用面。本研究揭示了这一潜在安全威胁，为防御机制设计和可解释AI政策制定提供了重要依据。代码已开源。

Abstract: Graph Machine Learning as a Service (GMLaaS) platforms increasingly implement explainability interfaces to meet regulatory transparency requirements. However, this transparency creates exploitable vulnerabilities for model extraction attacks. We present the first model extraction attack specifically designed for graph classification under strict black-box constraints where the attacker observes only discrete class labels and binary explanation masks (no probability scores, gradients, or confidence values). Our method (1) uses model explanation outputs to guide Monte Carlo edge sensitivity estimation toward decision boundaries, with Hoeffding concentration guarantees on estimation accuracy and (2) exploits explanation subgraphs to efficiently narrow the boundary search space. Extensive experiments on benchmark graph datasets across multiple domains demonstrate our method's superiority over comparable baselines. These findings demonstrate that such explainability interfaces create exploitable attack surfaces, informing both defensive mechanisms and policy frameworks for explainable AI mandates. The implementation code is provided in https://github.com/LabRAI/XSTEAL/.

</details>


### [193] [Universal Multiclass Transductive Online Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30479)
*Steve Hanneke,Hongao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有可能无界标签空间的通用归纳在线分类问题。通过引入新的组合结构“层级受限小石树（LCLL树）”和不变性性质，刻画了该设置下的可学习性。结果表明，可学习类别的最优错误率仅有两种可能：有界或对数增长。研究还扩展到非实化情况及仅知实例序列生成随机过程的情形。

Result: 可学习类别的最优错误率只能是有限或对数增长；提出了有效的可学习性判别标准，并扩展至非实化和部分信息场景。

Abstract: We consider the problem of universal transductive online classification with a possibly unbounded label space. This setting considers online learning, with the sequence of instances (without labels) known to the learner in advance. We say a concept class $\mathcal{H}$ is learnable if there is a learning algorithm $\mathcal{A}$, such that for every realizable sequence, the number of mistakes made by $\mathcal{A}$ grows at most sublinearly with the number of predictions. We characterize the learnability of this setting and show that there are only two possible optimal rates for the learnable classes: either bounded or increasing logarithmically. We introduce a new combinatorial structure, called ``Level-Constrained-Littlestone-Littlestone (LCLL) tree'', which, along with the indifference property, characterizes the learnability. We also extend the learnability result to the agnostic case and the case where only the stochastic process that generates the instance sequence is known.

### [194] [MAAT: Multi-phase Adapter-Aware Targeted Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30514)
*Suryash Yagnik,Shubham Gaur,Saksham Thakur,Vinija Jain,Aman Chadha,Amitava Das*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 现有机器遗忘评估严重失衡，因果类问题（Why）占比极低（<0.06%至1.3%），导致方法在因果知识遗忘上失败却仍能获得高分。为此提出5WBENCH，一个包含5000样本、每类5W问题（谁、什么、何时、何地、为何）各1000例的平衡基准，首次实现对因果遗忘失败的量化。实验表明，现有方法无法同时在因果问题上实现高遗忘与高保留；原因在于多跳推理链（44%的Why问题）和长达40.1词的梯度稀释。提出MAAT框架，基于LoRA适配器权重，通过三阶段策略（梯度投影上升、SVD秩维剪枝、任务向量反向、混合KL-隐藏状态修复），首次实现因果知识的高效遗忘与保留，突破遗忘-保留权衡边界。代码已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘评估中因果类问题（Why）占比极低，导致方法在因果知识遗忘上的失败难以被发现，影响评估的有效性。需要一个平衡的基准来量化因果遗忘能力。

Method: 提出5WBENCH基准，构建5000样本的平衡数据集，每类5W问题各1000例；设计MAAT框架，三阶段操作于LoRA适配器权重：梯度投影上升、SVD秩维剪枝、任务向量反向、混合KL-隐藏状态修复。

Result: 5WBENCH成功量化了因果遗忘失败；MAAT是首个在因果问题上同时实现高遗忘与高保留的方法，显著提升遗忘-保留性能，突破现有权衡边界。

Conclusion: 当前机器遗忘评估存在结构性偏差，忽视因果知识。5WBENCH提供了首个平衡评估基准，而MAAT作为新方法实现了因果知识的高效遗忘与保留，为未来研究提供了新方向。

Abstract: Machine unlearning evaluation is structurally skewed: Why-type questions, which probe causal and relational knowledge, comprise less than 0.06% of CounterFact, 0.6% of ZSRE, and less than 1.3% of TOFU, MUSE, and WMDP-Cyber. This near-zero representation means that methods that fail on causal knowledge can score highly in aggregate, and this failure is undetectable without balanced evaluation. We present 5WBENCH, a balanced 5,000-sample benchmark with 1,000 examples per 5W category (Who, What, When, Where, Why), making causal unlearning failures quantifiable for the first time. Using 5WBENCH, we show that no existing baseline simultaneously achieves high forgetting and high retention on Why-type questions: aggressive forgetting degrades retained knowledge, while conservative methods fail to forget causal facts. Why-type difficulty stems from multi-hop reasoning chains (44% of Why entries vs. less than or equal to 2% for others) and gradient dilution over 40.1-token answer spans. We present MAAT (Multi-phase Adapter-Aware Targeted Unlearning), a three-phase framework operating on LoRA adapter weights, combining gradient-projected ascent, SVD rank-dimension pruning, task vector negation, and hybrid KL-hidden-state retain repair. MAAT is the first method to simultaneously achieve high forgetting and high retention on Why-type causal knowledge, reaching a new operating point on the forget-retain Pareto frontier. We make our code publicly available.

### [195] [Revisiting Padded Transformer Expressivity: Which Architectural Choices Matter and Which Don't](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30523)
*Anej Svete,William Merrill,Ryan Cotterell,Ashish Sabharwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了填充Transformer模型在计算能力上的表现，发现其在多种注意力机制、模型宽度和统一性假设下具有高度鲁棒性。通过引入填充符号（如'...'）来提供多项式空间以实现自适应并行计算，研究证明：在实际假设下，常精度的多项式填充L-统一Transformer等价于L-统一AC⁰；而精度随输入增长的模型则达到L-统一TC⁰，且不受宽度影响。进一步地，循环结构使Transformer具备序列处理能力，使得log^d N次循环的常精度模型可达FO-统一AC^d，而高精度模型可达FO-统一TC^d。值得注意的是，宽度或精度超过对数级别不会提升表达能力，所有结果对softmax与平均硬注意力均成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究虽揭示了Transformer与布尔电路之间的联系，但缺乏精确刻画且对建模选择敏感。为建立更稳健的等价关系，需探索填充Transformer在不同条件下的表达能力，特别是注意力类型、模型宽度和精度的影响。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，构建理想化的填充Transformer模型，结合复杂度类（如AC⁰、TC⁰、AC^d、TC^d）进行形式化推导，系统考察不同注意力机制（softmax、平均硬注意力）、模型深度、宽度及数值精度对表达能力的影响，并通过循环结构模拟电路中的顺序计算过程。

Result: 常精度多项式填充的L-统一Transformer等价于L-统一AC⁰；增长精度的模型达到L-统一TC⁰，且不依赖宽度。使用log^d N次循环的常精度模型可实现FO-统一AC^d，增长精度则达FO-统一TC^d。模型宽度或精度超过对数级无增益。所有结论对softmax和平均硬注意力均成立。

Conclusion: 填充Transformer在合理假设下表现出高度的表达鲁棒性，其计算能力可被精确刻画为经典电路复杂度类。数值精度和模型深度是决定表达能力的关键因素，而宽度和注意力类型影响有限。这为理解Transformer的计算本质提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Recent work describes what transformers can and cannot compute through connections to boolean circuits, but existing results lack exact characterizations and are sensitive to modeling choices. Padded transformers -- to whose input filler symbols such as ``...'' are appended -- emerge as a useful gadget for establishing equivalences to circuit classes by providing polynomial space for adaptive parallel computation. However, only a limited set of padded transformer idealizations has been studied, leaving open how robustly these equivalences hold under changes to attention type, model width, and uniformity. We find that, under practical assumptions, padded transformers are surprisingly robust to all of these, and identify numeric precision and model depth as the main factors affecting expressivity. Concretely, we prove that polynomially padded $\text{L-uniform}$ constant-precision transformers are equivalent to $\text{L-uniform AC}^0$, while growing-precision ones achieve $\text{L-uniform TC}^0$ regardless of width. Furthermore, looping enables sequential processing analogous to circuits: $\log^d N$-looped constant-precision transformers reach $\text{FO-uniform AC}^d$, and growing-precision ones reach $\text{FO-uniform TC}^d$. Interestingly, growing width or precision beyond logarithmic does not increase expressivity, and all our results hold for both softmax and average hard attention transformers.

Abstract: Large language models are now adapted through chains of post-training stages rather than through a single instruction-tuning pass. We define a measurement suite for hidden states, logits, token trajectories, and LoRA updates, and we use it to analyze supervised fine-tuning, preference optimization, safety/refusal tuning, math and code specialization, and long chain-of-thought tuning under controlled stage orderings. We further evaluate lightweight interventions, including mixed-domain replay, feature refresh, representation diversity regularization, and LoRA update decorrelation, as ways to preserve future learnability without giving up the behavioral gains of post-training.

### [197] [Measuring, Localizing, and Ablating Alignment Signatures in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30526)

To this end, we compare human text, base-model generations, and aligned-model generations under matched human-source prefixes. Aligned generations show lower human-corpus affinity and higher AI-detection rates than base generations, suggesting that post-training shifts generated text away from human-corpus style and toward detector-visible AI-like text. We then introduce PASTA (Post-training Alignment Signature Targeted Ablation), a training-free method that estimates a post-training alignment signature from aligned-base residual contrasts and ablates the corresponding direction during decoding. Across 11 aligned models and 6 AI detectors, PASTA lowers the detection rate for most aligned models; this effect transfers well across detectors and is not reproduced by random directions. Qualitative analysis suggests that PASTA generations remain relevant and coherent while exhibiting greater stylistic variation. Together, these results show that AI-like stylistic effects of post-training can be measured, localized, and causally tested through activation ablation.

### [198] [The Long-Term Effects of Data Selection in LLM Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30537)
*Yuxin Yang,Aoxiong Zeng,Xiangquan Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究多阶段微调中数据选择的长期影响，发现短期最优的选择策略可能损害模型未来的适应能力。提出长视野视角下的数据选择，强调应评估选择策略对后续学习速度、遗忘、能力不平衡和分布外鲁棒性的影响。通过对比多种选择方法，揭示了'短视选择'（myopic selection）现象，并提出LHAS目标以平衡即时效用与未来适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前数据选择方法主要关注即时性能提升，但在多阶段微调中，短期优化可能损害模型长期适应能力，因此需要从更长远的角度重新审视数据选择的作用。

Method: 设计统一的多阶段微调协议，对比随机、基于损失、基于梯度、基于多样性、基于质量及效用-多样性等六类选择方法；通过控制实验分析各策略在不同阶段的表现，识别短视行为并提出长视野感知选择（LHAS）目标。

Result: 发现短期表现优异的选择策略在后续阶段反而导致学习速度下降和遗忘加剧，验证了短视选择的存在；LHAS目标能有效缓解该问题，提升模型长期适应能力。

Conclusion: 数据选择不应仅被视为局部的数据效率机制，而应作为塑造模型学习轨迹的训练干预手段，需兼顾短期收益与长期适应性。

Abstract: Data selection is increasingly used to reduce the cost of large language model (LLM) fine-tuning, with recent methods prioritizing samples by current utility, diversity, quality, or influence. This paper studies a different question: when fine-tuning occurs over multiple stages, can selection strategies that look optimal now make the model less adaptable later? We introduce a long-horizon view of LLM data selection in which a selector is evaluated not only by immediate task performance, but also by future adaptation speed, forgetting, capability imbalance, and out-of-distribution robustness. We compare representative random, loss-based, gradient-based, diversity-based, quality-based, and utility-diversity selection families under a unified multi-stage protocol. Through controlled experiments designed to instantiate this protocol, we show how short-term selectors can exhibit rank reversal: they improve the current stage while slowing subsequent learning and increasing forgetting. We formalize this behavior as \emph{myopic selection}, provide a simple local analysis of why it can occur, and propose a diagnostic Long-Horizon Aware Selection (LHAS) objective that augments immediate utility with coverage, future-proxy transfer, and anti-concentration terms. The study argues that data selection should be evaluated as a training intervention that shapes the model's learning trajectory, rather than only as a local data-efficiency mechanism.

### [199] [DisasterLex: An Expert Concept-to-Schema Knowledge Graph for Geospatial Reasoning in Disaster Analytics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30538)
*Yiming Xiao,Ankit Basu,Kai Yin,Sahil Vartak,Christian Swords,Ali Mostafavi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DisasterLex 是一个基于知识图谱的框架，通过引入专家知识图谱（EKG）来提升灾难管理领域文本到SQL查询的性能。该框架在四个阶段（实体识别、领域路由、因果推理规划、SQL生成）中逐步限制模式输入，有效处理异构地理空间模式和因果推理需求，在36张地理空间表的灾难分析数据库上，相比LightRAG、HippoRAG 2、ReFoRCE、CHESS等基线模型，性能提升1.4倍至2.75倍，绝对准确率达1.65至3.56（满分5.0）。错误分析表明，基线模型主要失败于领域路由和多表SQL构建，而DisasterLex通过显式编排解决了这些问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文本到SQL方法在灾难管理领域表现不佳，因灾难数据具有异构地理空间模式和复杂的因果关系，传统方法难以有效处理。需要一种能融合领域知识与结构化推理的框架以提升查询准确性。

Method: DisasterLex采用四阶段流程：1）识别用户查询中的实体；2）将查询路由至相关操作领域；3）基于知识图谱中的因果边进行计划；4）将最终结果映射为SQL语句。整个过程通过概念-表链接桥接知识图谱与数据库模式，逐步约束模型输入，提高推理效率与准确性。

Result: 在包含36个地理空间表、150列的灾难分析数据库上，对75个测试查询进行评估，DisasterLex在所有七种基础模型（涵盖专有与开源权重）上均优于四种最先进的基线方法（LightRAG、HippoRAG 2、ReFoRCE、CHESS），性能提升1.4倍至2.75倍，绝对准确率范围为1.65至3.56（满分5.0）。错误分析显示，基线模型的主要问题集中在领域路由和多表SQL组合，而DisasterLex的分步编排机制有效缓解了这些缺陷。

Conclusion: DisasterLex通过引入专家知识图谱与分阶段编排机制，显著提升了灾难管理领域文本到SQL查询的准确性与鲁棒性，尤其在处理复杂因果关系和异构数据模式方面表现出色，为灾害响应中的智能数据访问提供了可扩展、可复现的解决方案。

Abstract: Disasters are inevitable and increasingly costly, and effective response depends on querying structured tabular data: precise, information-dense records of hazard, exposure, vulnerability, and lifeline infrastructure that underpin disaster management. Current text-to-SQL methods enable natural-language access to such tables but transfer poorly to the disaster domain, where queries span heterogeneous geospatial schemas and require reasoning over causal relations. We introduce DisasterLex, a knowledge-graph-mediated framework that inserts an Expert Knowledge Graph (EKG) of curated concepts and typed causal edges between the user query and the database, bridged to schema by concept-to-table links. The orchestration runs four stages (identifying query entities, routing to the operational domain, planning over causal edges, and grounding the SQL), restricting the schema passed to the model at each step. We instantiate it on a disaster-analytics database (36 geospatial tables, 150 columns) with an EKG of 107 concepts, 117 causal edges, and 52 concept-to-schema links, evaluated on a 75-query test set. On all seven base models spanning proprietary and open-weight families, DisasterLex beats four state-of-the-art baselines (LightRAG, HippoRAG 2, ReFoRCE, CHESS) by 1.4x to 2.75x, with absolute scores of 1.65 to 3.56 (of 5.0). Error analysis shows baseline failures cluster in routing and multi-table SQL composition, the operations our orchestration explicitly addresses. Code, data, and the EKG artifact are available at https://github.com/YimingXiao98/DisasterLex and on Zenodo at https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20388029.

</details>

### [203] [Zeroth-Order Non-Log-Concave Sampling with Variance Reduction and Applications to Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30573)
*M. Berk Sahin,Behzad Sharif,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种方差减少的零阶Langevin采样方法，解决了黑箱设置下高维非对数凹分布采样的挑战。该方法通过改进梯度估计器，显著降低方差并消除批大小的维度依赖性，实现了实际稳定的采样。首次建立了零阶非对数凹采样的非渐近收敛保证，涵盖ε-相对Fisher信息和在Poincaré不等式假设下的平方总变差距离。进一步提出了ZO-APMC算法用于黑箱逆问题的后验采样，首次为这类方法提供了非渐近收敛保证。理论验证通过合成实验完成，并在实际线性和非线性逆问题中表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决高维、非对数凹分布采样在黑箱设置下的挑战，特别是当梯度不可用或计算成本过高时，传统Langevin动力学方法存在高方差且缺乏非渐近收敛保证的问题。

Method: 提出一种方差减少的零阶Langevin采样方法，使用改进的梯度估计器以降低方差并消除批大小的维度依赖；建立非渐近收敛性理论，基于ε-相对Fisher信息和总变差距离；设计ZO-APMC算法用于黑箱逆问题中的后验采样。

Result: 首次实现零阶非对数凹采样的非渐近收敛保证；在合成实验和实际线性与非线性逆问题上展现出优异的性能；证明了所提方法在稳定性和效率上的优势。

Conclusion: 所提出的方差减少零阶采样方法及其应用（ZO-APMC）在黑箱设置下有效解决了高维非对数凹分布采样的难题，具有理论保障和良好实践表现，为复杂逆问题的后验采样提供了新工具。

Abstract: Sampling from high-dimensional, non-log-concave distributions with unnormalized densities remains a fundamental challenge in machine learning, particularly in black-box settings where gradient information is inaccessible or computationally prohibitive. While Langevin dynamics provides a principled framework for sampling when gradients are accessible, its extension to the black-box settings suffers from high variance and lacks non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for non-log-concave sampling. To address these limitations, we propose a variance-reduced zeroth-order Langevin sampling method. Our method employs a gradient estimator that substantially reduces the variance of the classical batched zeroth-order estimator and eliminates the unfavorable dimensional dependence of the batch size required for accurate estimation, enabling practical and stable sampling. We establish the first non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for zeroth-order non-log-concave sampling in terms of $\varepsilon$-relative Fisher information, and, under a Poincaré inequality assumption, squared total variation distance. We further propose ZO-APMC, a posterior sampling algorithm for black-box inverse problems with pre-trained score-based generative priors, establishing the first non-asymptotic convergence guarantees for such methods. We validate our theory through synthetic experiments and demonstrate strong empirical performance on practical linear and nonlinear inverse problems.

### [206] [ScaleMAP: Preserving Local Density and Neighborhood Structure in Low-Dimensional Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30597)
*Rajas Poorna,Marcus T. Cicerone*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ScaleMAP introduces a scale-aware dimensionality reduction method by normalizing pairwise displacements using the geometric mean of local radii, preserving both neighborhood structure and density variations. It outperforms UMAP in capturing sparse structures and matches DensMAP in density preservation without conflicting objectives.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing nonlinear dimensionality reduction methods like UMAP and PaCMAP erase local scale information during graph construction, leading to loss of sparse structures such as bridges between cell types or narrow spectral features in hyperspectral images. DensMAP attempts to fix this with a density penalty, but it conflicts with UMAP's intrinsic forces, causing point scattering. ScaleMAP aims to preserve scale information more naturally by re-injecting it via a change of variables rather than adding competing penalties.

Method: ScaleMAP modifies the embedding process by dividing each pairwise displacement by the geometric mean of the local radii at the two endpoints in the original space. This effectively reintroduces scale information as a transformational correction, maintaining UMAP’s attraction-repulsion dynamics while improving density fidelity. The approach is also applied to PaCMAP, showing consistent improvements.

Result: ScaleMAP achieves superior preservation of sparse structures (e.g., cell type transitions in transcriptomics) compared to UMAP, faithfully represents density across 17 orders of magnitude in flow cytometry, and matches DensMAP in density preservation without compromising neighborhood fidelity. The method generalizes well to PaCMAP, demonstrating broader applicability.

Conclusion: ScaleMAP successfully preserves both local neighborhood structure and global density patterns by incorporating scale information through a change of variables, offering a robust, scalable, and generalizable alternative to existing methods.

Abstract: Nonlinear dimensionality-reduction methods such as UMAP and PaCMAP adaptively normalize local distances during graph construction, erasing neighborhood scale from the data. This distorts more than relative cluster sizes: sparse structures like bridges between transitioning cell types and narrow spectral spikes in hyperspectral images can be suppressed or lost entirely. DensMAP adds a density penalty to correct this, but this penalty competes with UMAP's attraction-repulsion forces, scattering points far from their neighborhoods. ScaleMAP takes a different approach: each pairwise embedding displacement is divided by the geometric mean of the two endpoints' original-space local radii, re-injecting scale information as a change of variables rather than as a competing objective. Across standard benchmarks and scientific datasets from transcriptomics, hyperspectral imaging, and flow cytometry, ScaleMAP matches DensMAP on density preservation while maintaining UMAP-level neighborhood preservation. In transcriptomic data, it recovers sparse bridges between cell populations that UMAP collapses; in flow cytometry, it faithfully represents density structure across 17 orders of magnitude. The same principle applied to PaCMAP yields consistently improved density preservation, suggesting the approach generalizes beyond UMAP.

</details>


### [207] [AMNESIA: A Large Scale Medical Unlearning Benchmark Suite with Disease-Informed Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30599)
*Saeedeh Davoudi,Reihaneh Iranmanesh,Ophir Frieder,Nazli Goharian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AMNESIA 是首个大规模、开源的医学模型遗忘基准，包含来自11种疾病类别的8,820份患者记录的70,560个问答对，涵盖事实性与临床推理问题。该研究评估了四种主流遗忘方法在随机患者和疾病级别上的表现，并引入新指标检测医学术语泄露。结果表明，遗忘单个患者会损害同病患者的知识，提示需发展更优的患者与共享临床知识分离方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘基准多基于合成或小规模通用数据，缺乏对临床场景的充分覆盖，难以真实评估医学大模型的遗忘能力。医学知识持续更新，亟需高效、精准的遗忘机制以移除特定训练数据影响，同时避免误伤共享临床知识。

Method: 构建 AMNESIA 基准：整合真实临床患者记录，生成高质量问答对；设计两类任务（事实性与推理性）；评估四种主流遗忘方法在患者级与疾病级的性能；提出新度量标准检测医学术语泄露。

Result: 遗忘单个患者会显著影响具有相同疾病的其他患者的知识表现，说明当前方法未能有效区分个体患者信息与共享临床知识；新提出的术语泄露检测指标可有效识别潜在隐私泄露风险。

Conclusion: 现有医学模型遗忘方法在处理患者间共享知识时存在缺陷，未来需开发能更好隔离个体信息与共性医学知识的遗忘机制，以支持安全、可更新的医疗AI系统。

Abstract: Medical knowledge is continuously evolving. This creates a need to update or selectively forget information encoded in already-trained medical LLMs. Machine unlearning aims to remove the influence of specific training data from a model without full retraining. Yet, existing unlearning benchmarks rely on synthetic or small-scale general data, leaving clinical unlearning understudied. We introduce AMNESIA, the first large-scale, open source benchmark for medical unlearning, with 70,560 question-answer pairs from 8,820 patient notes across 11 disease categories. AMNESIA includes both factual questions testing direct recall and reasoning questions testing clinical inference. We use it to evaluate four widely used unlearning methods at both random patient and disease-level, and introduce a new metric for detecting leakage of medical terminology. We show that unlearning individual patients erodes knowledge of others with the same condition, calling for methods that can better separate patients from shared clinical knowledge.

### [208] [The Fast Mixing Mechanism for Differential Privacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30600)
*Omri Lev,Moshe Shenfeld,Vishwak Srinivasan,Katrina Ligett,Ashia C. Wilson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于快速变换的新型差分隐私（DP）随机投影机制，能够在特定情况下达到经典快速投影方法的运行时间，同时在有利条件下实现与高斯投影相当的隐私保障（仅差常数因子）。该机制结合最新的基于投影的DP线性回归方法，构建了首个具有强效用和改进运行时间的快速DP普通最小二乘算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于高斯投影的差分隐私线性回归方法虽然具备良好的实用性，但通常无法提升运行效率，难以满足大规模数据场景下的计算需求。因此亟需一种既能保持良好隐私与精度保障，又能显著加速计算过程的新方法。

Method: 设计一种基于快速变换（如哈达玛矩阵等结构化矩阵）的新型差分隐私随机投影机制，利用其高效计算特性，在保证隐私的前提下降低求解复杂度；并将其与最新投影型DP线性回归方法结合，构造出高效的优化算法。

Result: 所提出的算法在隐私保障上达到当前最优水平，且在某些情形下隐私性能接近高斯投影的常数倍；在运行时间上可媲美经典快速投影方法，是首个兼具强效用与快速性的DP普通最小二乘算法。

Conclusion: 本文首次实现了快速、高隐私保障的差分隐私普通最小二乘求解，为大规模隐私保护机器学习提供了新的有效工具。

Abstract: Randomized sketching is a central tool for compressing large-scale optimization problems while preserving accuracy. In particular, sketches that are based on structured matrices, such as the Hadamard matrix, can be applied efficiently and often yield solutions that approximate those of the original problem at much lower computational cost. In differential privacy (DP), Gaussian sketching has been used to solve DP linear regression, beginning with \citet{sheffet2017differentially, sheffet2019old} and later refined by \citet{lev2025gaussianmix, lev2026near}. However, although these methods achieve strong utility guarantees, they usually do not improve runtime over classical DP approaches. In this work, we introduce a new DP sketching mechanism based on fast transforms, which, in certain cases, matches the runtime of classical fast sketching methods. We prove state-of-the-art privacy guarantees for this mechanism and show that, in favorable regimes, they match those of the Gaussian sketch up to a constant factor. As an application, we combine this mechanism with recent sketch-based methods for DP linear regression to obtain a new algorithm with strong utility and improved runtime. We establish privacy and accuracy guarantees for this algorithm, yielding, to the best of our knowledge, the first fast method for DP ordinary least squares.

### [209] [Constrained Flow Optimization via Sequential Fine Tuning for Molecular Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30610)
*Sven Gutjahr,Riccardo De Santi,Luca Schaufelberger,Kjell Jorner,Andreas Krause*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为约束流优化（CFO）的新算法，用于在生成模型中平衡奖励最大化与约束满足之间的关系。该方法基于一个严格的约束生成优化框架，通过将问题转化为一系列可扩展的微调步骤，实现了对分子设计等科学发现任务的有效支持。实验表明，CFO在保持高约束满足率的同时显著提升了奖励得分，具有良好的实际应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成基础模型（如扩散模型和流模型）在科学发现中的应用面临如何可靠且可预测地权衡奖励最大化与约束满足的问题，尤其是在分子设计和蛋白质工程等任务中。尽管已有研究尝试使用强化学习和控制方案进行奖励引导的微调，但缺乏系统性的算法来实现这种权衡。

Method: 提出约束生成优化（Constrained Generative Optimization）的理论框架，并引入约束流优化（CFO）算法，通过将原问题转化为一系列顺序微调过程，利用已有的可扩展方法实现自动、可证明的平衡。

Result: CFO在合成数据和真实分子设计任务上均表现出色，不仅持续提升奖励值，还保证了高水平的约束满足度，且具备收敛性保证。

Conclusion: CFO为生成模型在科学发现中的约束优化提供了有效、可靠的解决方案，展示了其在复杂生成任务中的实用价值。

Abstract: Adapting generative foundation models, in particular diffusion and flow models, to optimize given reward functions (e.g., binding affinity) while satisfying constraints (e.g., molecular synthesizability) is fundamental for their adoption in real-world scientific discovery applications such as molecular design or protein engineering. While recent works have introduced scalable methods for reward-guided fine-tuning of such models via reinforcement learning and control schemes, it remains an open problem how to algorithmically trade-off reward maximization and constraint satisfaction in a reliable and predictable manner. Motivated by this challenge, we first present a rigorous framework for Constrained Generative Optimization, which brings an optimization viewpoint to the introduced adaptation problem and retrieves the relevant task of constrained generation as a sub-case. Then, we introduce Constrained Flow Optimization (CFO), an algorithm that automatically and provably balances reward maximization and constraint satisfaction by reducing the original problem to sequential fine-tuning via established, scalable methods. We provide convergence guarantees for constrained generative optimization and constrained generation via CFO. Ultimately, we present an experimental evaluation of CFO on both synthetic, yet illustrative, settings, and a molecular design task. Across these evaluations, CFO achieves consistent increases in reward while ensuring high constraint satisfaction, showcasing its practical utility for constrained generative optimization.

### [210] [Improving Selective Classification with Pairwise Queries for Binary Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30615)
*Harsh Vardhan,Sunav Choudhary,Natwar Modani,Arya Mazumdar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在选择性分类中，大模型的置信度估计与实际预测之间不一致的问题。为解决该问题，提出通过额外的成对查询来检测高误差样本，并将其融入选择性分类框架，从而降低非拒绝样本上的错误率。理论分析表明，在特定条件下，使用成对查询的算法优于仅依赖原始置信度估计（如LLM的下一个词元logits）的方法。实验验证了该方法在1个合成数据集和4个基于上下文学习的真实二分类数据集上的有效性，均实现了更优的准确率-成本权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在选择性分类中，模型仅对高置信度样本进行预测，而将低置信度样本交由专家标注，但若模型的置信度估计与真实预测误差不一致，则可能导致非拒绝样本上出现高错误率，浪费专家资源。尤其在大模型进行上下文学习时，这种不一致性更为显著。因此需要一种机制来校正置信度，提升非拒绝样本的准确性。

Method: 提出通过向同一模型发起成对查询（pairwise queries），比较两个样本的预测差异，识别出可能出错的样本。这些信息被用于调整选择性分类策略，以减少高误差样本被保留的情况。理论分析给出了该方法优于原始置信度估计的条件。

Result: 在1个合成数据集和4个基于上下文学习的真实二分类数据集上，使用成对查询的方法在保持或降低拒绝率的同时，显著降低了非拒绝样本的错误率，实现了更好的准确率-成本权衡。相比于直接使用LLM的next-token logits作为置信度，该方法表现更优。

Conclusion: 通过引入成对查询机制，可以有效缓解大模型在选择性分类中因置信度估计不一致带来的高错误率问题。该方法不仅具有理论支持，还在多种真实场景中表现出优越的性能，是一种实用且高效的改进策略。

Abstract: In selective classification, a model predicts the labels of data samples where it is confident, and abstains from predicting labels for samples on which it is not confident. The rejected samples are often labeled by an expert, which is expensive. The budget for the expert is best utilized when the model has low error on non-rejected samples. However, the estimate of a model's confidence might be inconsistent with the model's predictions, which can lead to high error on non-rejected points. Such situations can readily occur in in-context binary classification by LLMs. To remedy this, we propose making additional pairwise queries to the same model. These pairwise queries can detect high-error samples and be incorporated into selective classification techniques to reduce the error on non-rejected samples. Theoretically, we establish the conditions under which a simple algorithm using pairwise queries outperforms an inconsistent confidence estimate. We support this insight through extensive experiments for $1$ synthetic and $4$ in-context learning-based real binary classification datasets. In all these cases, we show that our algorithms, using pairwise queries, obtain a better accuracy-cost tradeoff than using only the raw confidence estimates, for instance, the LLM's next-token logits.

</details>


### [211] [CellBRIDGE: Learning Cellular Trajectories via Interaction-Aware Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30635)
*Silas Ruhrberg Estévez,Nicolas Huynh,Tennison Liu,Roderik M. Kortlever,Gerard I. Evan,David L. Bentley,Mihaela van der Schaar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出CellBRIDGE模型，通过引入基于配体-受体活性的定向类型化交互成本，增强基于特征的最优传输（OT）方法，以改进单细胞RNA测序中跨时间快照的细胞耦合与轨迹推断。该模型显式建模细胞间通信，提升生物可解释性，并支持机制可解释的模拟扰动，在肺癌数据中成功再现靶向通路抑制的预期效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单细胞RNA测序中，由于测量具有破坏性，无法直接追踪单个细胞随时间的变化，导致轨迹推断不明确。传统的最优传输方法依赖基因表达距离，忽略了细胞间的结构化通信，因此需要一种能反映真实生物学交互的更优成本函数。

Method: 提出CellBRIDGE模型，将特征基最优传输与基于配体-受体活性的定向、类型化交互成本相结合，构建更符合生物学意义的细胞间耦合关系。

Result: 在合成和真实scRNA-seq数据上，CellBRIDGE相较于仅使用特征的基线方法，显著提升了跨快照耦合质量及下游轨迹估计性能；同时可在模拟扰动中实现机制可解释的结果，如在肺癌数据中沉默特定配体-受体对可重现靶向通路抑制的轨迹变化。

Conclusion: CellBRIDGE通过整合细胞间通信信息，有效提升了单细胞动态推断的准确性与可解释性，为理解复杂生物过程提供了新工具。

Abstract: Inferring dynamics from population snapshots is a fundamental challenge in machine learning and biology. In scRNA-sequencing (scRNA-seq), destructive measurements preclude direct tracking of individual cells across time, making trajectory inference underdetermined. Optimal Transport (OT) provides a principled framework for snapshot alignment, but a long-standing modeling question is which cost functions yield biologically meaningful couplings. Standard OT approaches rely on gene-expression distances, implicitly treating cells as independent points and neglecting structured cell-cell communication mediated by ligand-receptor signaling. We introduce CellBRIDGE (Cell-Based Regularized Interaction-Driven Gene Expression), which augments feature-based OT with a directed, typed interaction cost derived from ligand-receptor activity. By explicitly modeling cell-cell communication, CellBRIDGE improves cross-snapshot couplings and downstream trajectory estimates across synthetic and real scRNA-seq datasets relative to feature-only baselines. Notably, CellBRIDGE enables mechanistically interpretable in silico perturbations: on lung cancer data, silencing specific ligand-receptor pairs induces trajectory shifts that recapitulate expected effects of targeted pathway inhibition.

### [212] [Score Broadcast and Decorrelation: A General Framework for Broadcast-Based Credit Assignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30638)
*Mustafa Uzun,Mete Erdogan,Cengiz Pehlevan,Alper T. Erdogan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出SBD框架，统一了基于广播的信用分配机制，通过输出得分与隐藏层激活之间的正交性原则，为多种可微损失函数提供理论支持，并在CIFAR-10和Tiny ImageNet上验证其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有广播信用分配方法缺乏对一般可微损失的理论支持，且生物合理性不足；需建立统一的理论基础以提升性能并贴近神经科学机制。

Method: 引入输出得分与隐藏层激活间的正交性原则，构建Score Broadcast and Decorrelation（SBD）框架，推导通用损失下的三因子学习规则，并提出得分向量扩展技术增强广播信号。

Result: SBD在CIFAR-10和Tiny ImageNet上显著优于现有广播方法，得分向量扩展进一步提升性能，验证了理论框架的有效性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了损失得分作为广播信号的核心作用，提供了跨损失类别的理论支撑，推动了生物启发式学习规则的发展。

Abstract: We introduce Score Broadcast and Decorrelation (SBD), a principled framework for broadcast-based credit assignment for general families of differentiable losses. Error broadcast is a biologically plausible alternative to backpropagation that sends output information to hidden layers without weight transport. The Error Broadcast and Decorrelation (EBD) framework, recently introduced for the mean-squared-error (MSE) setting, grounded this mechanism in the stochastic orthogonality of optimal estimators, under which the optimal residual is orthogonal to functions of the input. We generalize that foundation by introducing an orthogonality principle between the output score (the gradient of loss with respect to the final-layer output) and hidden-layer activations, which holds whenever the optimal score has conditional mean zero. This single principle unifies broadcast-based credit assignment across the standard differentiable-loss families, including cross-entropy, Bregman divergences, proper scoring rules, and exponential-family negative log-likelihoods. The framework supplies a theoretical grounding for the three-factor learning rule under general losses, with the neuromodulatory factor derived as the broadcast loss score. We derive the cross-entropy case explicitly, characterize the admissible loss class, and introduce a score vector expansion technique that enriches the broadcast signal while preserving the orthogonality framework. Experiments on CIFAR-10 and Tiny ImageNet show that SBD substantially improves over existing broadcast approaches, with score vector expansion delivering further gains. Overall, this work identifies the loss score as the signal to broadcast, supplies the orthogonality theory and theoretical grounding for the three-factor learning rule from neuroscience, and shows how score vector expansion enriches the decorrelation directions of the resulting objective.

</details>


### [213] [CSULoRA: Closest Safe Update Low-Rank Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30640)
*Oleksandr Marchenko Breneur,Adelaide Danilov,Aria Nourbakhsh,Salima Lamsiyah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CSULoRA是一种后处理方法，通过最近安全更新估计来修正训练好的LoRA适配器。它从对齐模型与基础检查点之间的权重位移中估计一个安全对齐子空间，并将每个LoRA更新分解为完全对齐、部分对齐和非子空间成分。不同于直接丢弃子空间外的成分，CSULoRA通过闭式惩罚最小变化问题，在保留完全对齐成分的同时，平滑衰减潜在不安全方向。在对抗性微调实验中，CSULoRA显著降低攻击成功率，同时保留了标准LoRA微调的大部分性能增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的安全保护LoRA方法依赖于硬性干预（如投影、剪枝、阈值或额外训练目标），虽然能抑制不安全更新方向，但可能移除任务相关信息或需要额外调参。因此，亟需一种更高效且不破坏任务性能的安全修正方法。

Method: CSULoRA通过分析对齐模型与基础模型间的权重位移，估计一个安全对齐子空间；随后将每个LoRA更新分解为三类成分：完全对齐、部分对齐和离散成分；采用闭式惩罚最小变化优化，保留安全成分并平滑衰减不安全方向。

Result: 在对抗性微调实验中，CSULoRA显著降低了攻击成功概率，同时几乎完全保留了标准LoRA带来的性能提升，证明其在保持模型效用的同时有效增强了安全性。

Conclusion: CSULoRA提供了一种无需额外训练、不破坏任务性能的后处理安全修正机制，可有效应对不安全或对抗性微调数据带来的风险，是参数高效微调中提升模型安全性的有效方案。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation has become a standard method for parameter-efficient fine-tuning of large language models, but even small amounts of unsafe or adversarial fine-tuning data can substantially weaken the safety behavior of aligned models. Existing safety-preserving LoRA methods often rely on hard interventions such as projection, pruning, thresholding, or additional training objectives. While these methods can suppress unsafe update directions, they may also remove task-relevant information or require extra tuning. We introduce CSULoRA, a post-hoc method for correcting trained LoRA adapters through closest safe update estimation. CSULoRA estimates a safety-aligned subspace from the weight displacement between a safety-aligned model and its corresponding base checkpoint. It then decomposes each LoRA update into fully aligned, partially aligned, and off-subspace components. Instead of discarding components outside the estimated safety subspace, CSULoRA solves a closed-form penalized minimum-change problem that preserves the fully aligned component while smoothly attenuating potentially unsafe directions according to their relative energy. In adversarial fine-tuning experiments, CSULoRA substantially reduces attack success rate while preserving most of the utility gains obtained from standard LoRA fine-tuning.

</details>


### [214] [Diffusion Models Preferentially Memorize Prototypical Examples or: Why Does My Diffusion Model Love Slop?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30642)
*Marta Aparicio Rodriguez,Anastasia Borovykh,Grigorios A. Pavliotis,Daniel J. Korchinski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现，生成模型更倾向于首先记忆常见子串而非罕见样本，即使数据点完全唯一，去重也无法提供有效隐私保护。在长尾分布数据中，罕见样本的记忆被延迟，且高层生成规则引入长尾会加剧这一现象。此外，存在部分记忆的中间阶段，导致生成内容趋于平庸，即‘平均回归’式的单调性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决生成模型因记忆训练数据而引发的法律风险与创意多样性下降问题，探究哪些样本更容易被记忆及其条件。

Method: 在随机层级模型（RHM）生成的字符串上训练扩散模型，分析不同数据分布下样本的记忆顺序，考察常见子串与罕见样本的记忆优先级，并观察生成过程中的部分记忆现象。

Result: 常见子串优先被记忆，罕见样本记忆延迟；高层规则引入长尾会放大延迟效应；训练中途停止会导致生成内容趋于平庸。

Conclusion: 数据集的多样性，尤其是在抽象层级上的多样性，对延缓模型记忆至关重要；仅在数据点层面去重不足以保障隐私，需关注更高层次的结构特征。

Abstract: Generative models have a persistent limitation: their tendency to memorize training data can create legal liabilities and erode creative diversity. Understanding which samples are memorized in whole or in part, and under what conditions, therefore remains an important open problem. Here we answer the question "Are atypical or rare samples memorized first?" in the negative. We train diffusion models on strings generated according to the production rules of the Random Hierarchy Model (RHM), and find that samples composed of common substrings are preferentially memorized. This holds true even if the training data consists of entirely unique samples, indicating that deduplication at the data point level does not provide a meaningful privacy guarantee. Correspondingly we predict, then observe, delayed memorization for fat-tailed datasets (i.e., those with more atypical samples). This effect is amplified when fat-tails are introduced into high-level production rules. These together suggest that dataset diversity, particularly at higher levels of abstraction, plays an important role in staving off memorization. Finally, we identify an intermediate regime of partial memorization in which common substrings are learned first and subsequently overproduced during generation. If training is stopped in this regime, models will exhibit the reversion-to-the-mean blandness often derided as "slop".

</details>


### [215] [BOKBO (Best of K Bad Options): Calibrated Abstention for VLA Policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30660)
*Anya Singh,Cabrel Happi,Jai Relan,Varun Nair,Vidyut Baradwaj*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: BOKBO 是首个用于 K-样本视觉-语言-动作（VLA）推理的置信区间拒答层，提供有限样本、无分布假设的执行违规率保证。它包含全局和按任务（Mondrian）变体，后者显著提升最难任务的条件置信度。研究发现现有方法中策略内部非一致性分数在扰动采样下存在结构性缺陷：其与动作噪声参数σ高度相关（0.98），但与真实安全违规相关性极低。通过对比不同采样机制，发现该问题具有机制特异性，并在基于策略随机性的采样下部分缓解。结合语义视觉特征和任务身份的违规预测器实现紧密校准，在ε=0.05时，条件覆盖率为78%，净任务成功率达70%。Mondrian-BOKBO 将最低任务级条件保持率从0.71提升至0.93。结果在5个训练种子下稳定，可在多种分布偏移下复现。此外，研究还识别并纠正了一个方法论误区：全局设定的力阈值远低于专家典型操作力，导致正常操作被误判为不安全，使违规率虚高5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA政策在测试时采用K样本采样并选择验证器最佳动作，但当所有候选均不安全时，系统仍会执行违规动作且无预警。缺乏对执行违规率的可靠控制，限制了其在安全关键场景中的应用。需要一种可提供有限样本、分布无关保证的拒答机制，以确保安全性与可靠性。

Method: 提出BOKBO，一种基于置信区间理论的拒答层，支持全局与按任务（Mondrian）两种配置。利用学习的违规预测器，结合视觉语义特征与任务身份，实现对安全性的精确校准。通过在多个基准上进行多轮实验，评估其在不同采样策略下的鲁棒性与有效性。同时，重新审视并修正了力阈值设置不当带来的方法论偏差。

Result: BOKBO 在 libero_object_temp_x0.1 上实现 78% 的条件覆盖率和 70% 的净任务成功率，ε=0.05；Mondrian-BOKBO 将最小任务级条件保持率从 0.71 提升至 0.93。结果在5个训练种子下稳定，跨多种分布偏移保持一致。纠正力阈值设置后，违规率虚高问题得到解决，表明原方法存在严重误判。

Conclusion: BOKBO 有效提升了 VLA 政策在测试阶段的安全性与可信度，首次实现了对执行违规率的有限样本、分布无关保证。研究揭示了当前 K-样本方法在非一致性评分上的结构性缺陷，并提出了可信赖的解决方案。同时指出并修正了重要方法论误区，推动了 VLA 安全评估的规范化发展。

Abstract: Test-time scaling for vision-language-action (VLA) policies, methods such as RoboMonkey, SEAL, MG-Select, and V-GPS, samples K candidate action chunks at inference and executes the verifier-best. When all K candidates are unsafe, the system executes a violating action with no warning. We propose BOKBO, the first conformal abstention layer for K-sample VLA inference, providing finite-sample distribution-free guarantees on executed-violation rate. We provide both global and per-task (Mondrian) variants, with the per-task variant closing the conditional gap on the hardest tasks.
  Our analysis exposes a structural failure of policy-internal nonconformity scores under perturbation-based K-sampling: the base-policy confidence proxy and K-sample disagreement correlate at 0.98 with the action-noise hyperparameter $σ$, while correlating at the noise floor with actual safety violations. We test the failure's scope by replicating the analysis under token-level temperature sampling and find the failure is mechanism-specific and partially mitigated under policy-stochasticity-based sampling. A learned violation predictor conditioned on semantic visual features and task identity supports tight calibration: at $ε$ = 0.05 on libero_object_temp_x0.1 with OpenVLA-OFT, the conditional CRC bound holds on 86% of bootstrap splits with 78% coverage and 70% net task success. Mondrian-BOKBO raises the minimum per-task conditional hold fraction from 0.71 to 0.93. Results are stable across 5 training seeds, replicate within bootstrap noise on $π_0$-FAST, hold on libero_spatial_temp_x0.1 as a co-equal benchmark, and survive four within-suite distribution shifts. We additionally identify and correct a methodological pitfall: globally-set force thresholds well below expert-typical manipulation forces conflate unsafe behavior with normal manipulation, inflating violation rates by $5\times$.

</details>


### [216] [Universal Decision Learners](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30694)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种通用的范畴论框架——通用决策学习者（UDL），将局部信息扩展为全局一致的行为。通过左凯恩扩展（rollout、聚合、候选生成）和右凯恩扩展（一致性、约束满足、不动点语义）统一多种决策理论，如规划、强化学习、因果干预、在线学习和博弈均衡。论文证明了该构造的普遍比较性质，并定义了凯恩不变的行为等价与最小抽象，展示了贝尔曼方程、规划递归、因果干预、在线后悔和均衡如何作为特例出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有决策理论（如规划、强化学习、因果干预、在线学习、博弈论均衡）虽方法各异，但均试图从局部信息推导出全局一致行为。本文旨在揭示这些不同理论背后的共同数学结构，提出一个统一的范畴论框架以实现形式化统一。

Method: 采用范畴论中的左凯恩扩展和右凯恩扩展作为核心工具，构建通用决策学习者（UDL）模型。通过两个通用构造实现从局部决策数据到新情境的自然外延，并证明其普遍性与唯一性。进一步引入凯恩不变等价与最小抽象概念，用于分析行为一致性与简化模型。

Result: 成功将贝尔曼方程、规划递归、因果干预、在线后悔、博弈均衡等经典决策机制形式化为凯恩扩展的特例；证明了UDL具有唯一性与普遍比较性质；提出了可解释的最小抽象与行为等价标准。

Conclusion: 尽管不同决策问题不共享相同算法，但它们都可被建模为同一类普遍问题：在保持一致性前提下，对局部行为数据进行自然外延。该框架提供了一种统一的语言与工具，有助于理解并整合各类决策理论。

Abstract: Many theories of decision making -- planning, reinforcement learning, causal intervention, online learning, and game-theoretic equilibrium -- turn local information into globally coherent behavior. This paper proposes a common categorical formulation: a Universal Decision Learner (UDL) extends a partially specified decision functor from observed contexts to new contexts by a pair of universal constructions. Left Kan extensions express rollout, aggregation, and candidate generation; right Kan extensions express consistency, constraint satisfaction, and fixed-point semantics. The central claim is not that every decision problem has the same algorithm, but that many decision formalisms instantiate the same universal problem: extend local behavioral data canonically, then characterize the globally coherent extensions. We give the abstract UDL construction, prove its universal comparison property, define Kan-invariant behavioral equivalence and minimal abstractions, and show how Bellman equations, planning recursions, causal interventions, online regret, and equilibria arise as special cases. The supplementary material develops the reinforcement-learning specialization in more detail.

</details>


### [217] [A Context-Aware Middleware for Medical Image Based Reports: An approach based on image feature extraction and association rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30699)
*Erick O. Rodrigues,Jose Viterbo,Aura Conci,Trueman Mac Henry*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种上下文感知的中间件，用于优化医疗工作流程并提高效率。该中间件能够根据医疗人员的历史分析数据和当前临床情境，智能推断最适合处理特定医学图像的医生或技术人员，从而减少手动分配时间，提升诊疗效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在医院、实验室和远程放射学公司中，医生和技术人员通常专注于特定类型的诊断或分析，导致医学图像需要频繁手动转发给特定人员。这一过程耗时且低效，尤其是在判断谁是最合适的人选以及其是否在岗时，存在大量重复性决策。因此，亟需一种自动化机制来优化图像分配流程。

Method: 设计并实现了一种上下文感知的中间件，通过收集每位医疗人员的历史分析数据，并结合当前的临床情境（如工作负荷、可用性等），利用推理算法自动识别最合适的接收者。

Result: 实验结果表明，该中间件显著减少了图像分配所需的时间，提高了工作流的响应速度与整体效率，同时降低了人为错误率。

Conclusion: 所提出的上下文感知中间件有效解决了医疗图像分配中的效率瓶颈问题，具备良好的可扩展性和实用性，为智慧医疗系统提供了有力支持。

Abstract: This work proposes a context-aware middleware for medical workflow organization and efficiency improvement. In hospitals, laboratories and teleradiology companies, each physician or technician is specialized in a specific kind of diagnosis or analysis. Therefore, certain types of medical images are often forwarded to a certain physician or a certain group. This forwarding is time consuming. That is, repeatedly deciding who would be the best physician, whether he is available at a certain moment given a certain context is exhaustive and may be very inefficient. Thus, the proposed middleware has the ability to process and collect data from images analyzed by each medical staff. Based on the collected data and current clinical context, the middleware is able to infer who would be the best fit staff to receive a certain incoming medical image.

### [218] [Diversity Matters: Revisiting Test-Time Compute in Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30713)
*Yijie Tong,Yifan Hou,Shaobo Cui,Antoine Bosselut,Mrinmaya Sachan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了测试时计算（TTC）在视觉-语言模型（VLMs）中的应用，发现特征评分方法失效，单一模型投票仅带来微小提升。由于输出高度相关，缺乏预测多样性限制了投票效果。为此提出基于熵的TTC（ETTC），通过预测熵选择最自信的输出，在单模型下退化为多数投票，但在多模型集成中利用置信度差异优先强模型。理论与实证均表明ETTC优于多数投票及最优单模型，且小模型可协同增强大模型性能，实现传统策略无法达到的集成增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索测试时计算（TTC）在视觉-语言模型（VLMs）中的潜力，解决现有方法在单模型设置下效果有限的问题，尤其是因预测相关性高导致的多样性不足。

Method: 提出熵基测试时计算（ETTC），利用预测熵衡量模型置信度，动态选择最可信输出；在多模型集成中，通过置信度差异优先强模型，实现更优决策。

Result: ETTC在多个基准上显著优于标准多数投票和最佳单模型，且小模型能有效增强大模型表现，实现非线性协同增益。

Conclusion: ETTC是一种高效、通用的TTC方法，能充分挖掘多模型集成的潜力，尤其在小模型与大模型协同场景中展现突出优势，为提升VLM推理能力提供了新范式。

Abstract: Test-time compute (TTC) strategies have emerged as a lightweight approach to boost reasoning in large language models (LLMs). However, their application and benefits for vision-language models (VLMs) remain underexplored. We present a systematic study of TTC across seven VLMs and six benchmarks, specifically analyzing feature-based scoring and majority voting methods. We find that feature heuristics fail and voting yields only modest gains in single-model settings. We theoretically show that this limitation stems from a lack of prediction diversity: when outputs are highly correlated, voting provides little benefit. In contrast, multi-model ensembles offer richer diversity, yet standard majority voting fails to account for varying model capabilities. To address this, we propose Entropy-based TTC (ETTC), which selects the most confident prediction based on predictive entropy. Our method reduces to majority voting in the single-model case, but in model ensembles, it leverages confidence disparities to prioritize stronger models. We prove that ETTC outperforms majority voting under mild assumptions and empirically demonstrate that it consistently surpasses both voting and the best individual model. Crucially, our results show that smaller models can synergistically enhance larger ones, unlocking ensembling gains not achievable with standard strategies.

</details>


### [219] [When are LLMs Sufficient Policy Optimizers for Sequential RL Tasks?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30719)
*Stephane Hatgis-Kessell,Emma Brunskill*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型（LLM）在强化学习任务中作为黑箱策略优化器的有效性，提出一种名为Prompted Policy Optimization（PromptPO）的迭代方法。该方法通过自然语言提示（Python描述状态空间、动作空间和奖励函数），让LLM生成并根据环境反馈迭代优化可执行策略。在复杂探索环境、Meta-World机器人任务及多个真实世界控制问题中，PromptPO性能常优于或相当于传统RL基线，且所需环境交互次数显著减少。所生成策略可从比例控制器到基于规划的算法（如值迭代），表明其能利用先验知识进行优化。但在MuJoCo连续控制领域表现不佳，说明其在精细连续控制任务中存在局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大语言模型是否可替代传统强化学习算法，作为高效的黑箱策略优化器；解决传统RL需要大量环境交互、设计复杂的问题。

Method: 提出Prompted Policy Optimization（PromptPO）方法，通过自然语言提示（以Python形式描述状态、动作、奖励函数），引导LLM生成并基于环境反馈迭代优化策略，实现无需显式编程的策略自动构建与改进。

Result: 在硬探索环境、机器人任务和现实控制问题中，PromptPO性能接近或超过标准RL基线，且环境交互次数远少于传统方法；策略输出涵盖比例控制器、规则计划、规划算法等，体现其灵活性和知识利用能力；但在需要精细连续控制的MuJoCo任务中表现较差。

Conclusion: LLM-based policy optimization在具备环境先验知识或优化策略知识时足够有效；然而在需要高精度连续控制的任务中仍存在局限，表明当前技术尚未完全替代传统强化学习。

Abstract: We study when large language models (LLMs) can serve as effective black-box policy optimizers for reinforcement learning (RL) tasks, i.e., when can we replace classical RL algorithms with an LLM? We explore this question by introducing Prompted Policy Optimization (PromptPO), an iterative method that prompts an LLM with Python descriptions of the state space, action space, and reward function, then has it generate and refine executable policies based on rollout feedback. Across hard exploration environments, Meta-World robotics tasks, and several real-world control problems, PromptPO often matches or exceeds the performance of standard RL baselines while using substantially fewer environment interactions. To maximize expected return, and without further explicit prompting, the policies PromptPO outputs range from tuned proportional controllers or rule-based plans to policies that run planning algorithms like value iteration. Our results demonstrate that LLM-based policy optimization is sufficient when the LLM can leverage prior knowledge about the environment or optimization strategy. PromptPO underperforms standard RL baselines in MuJoCo domains. This demonstrates possible limitations of LLM-based policy optimization to settings that requiring fine-grained continuous control.

</details>


### [220] [Kalimati Vegetable Price Index Forecasting with a Momentum Corrected Online Stacking Ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30720)
*Sahaj Raj Malla*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种新的反波动加权复合指数——加利马蒂蔬菜价格指数（KVPI），基于尼泊尔首都加德满都十年间135种每日批发商品数据，旨在降低个体作物建模中的噪声。通过构建64个因果有效的特征，包括节日前后效应、滚动统计量和日历变量，评估了14种涵盖统计模型、树模型、深度学习、混合及变压器架构的预测模型。树模型集成表现尤为稳健，而经典统计模型和复杂变压器在噪声数据上表现不佳。所提出的动量修正在线堆叠集成模型在90天预测期达到最低RMSE（1.771）、极低MAPE（0.68%）以及84.5%的方差解释率（R²=0.845），展现出卓越性能。该开源流程为尼泊尔及其他类似市场提供实用可靠的工具，助力政策制定者与供应链参与者预判价格波动，强化粮食安全。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在新兴经济体中，农业商品价格预测因高波动性、频繁的供应中断以及强烈文化因素对需求的影响而极具挑战。现有方法难以有效处理这些复杂因素，导致预测精度不足，影响粮食安全与政策制定。因此，亟需一种能提取稳定宏观信号、减少噪声干扰的新型指数与模型框架。

Method: 提出并应用卡尔马蒂蔬菜价格指数（KVPI），采用反波动加权方式整合135种每日批发商品数据；构建包含节日前滞后效应、滚动统计量、日历变量等在内的64个因果有效特征；评估14种不同类型的预测模型（统计、树模型、深度学习、混合模型、变压器架构），并在短（7天）、中（14/30天）、长（90天）三个时间尺度上进行比较；最终采用动量修正在线堆叠集成方法实现最优性能。

Result: 动量修正在线堆叠集成模型在90天预测周期中表现出最佳性能，获得RMSE为1.771，MAPE仅为0.68%，且解释了84.5%的方差（R² = 0.845），显著优于其他模型。树模型集成表现出较强鲁棒性，而传统统计模型和复杂变压器在高噪声数据下表现较差。

Conclusion: 本研究成功开发并验证了基于KVPI的高效价格预测框架，其开源特性可广泛服务于尼泊尔及类似新兴市场，为政策制定和供应链管理提供可靠的价格预判支持，有助于提升粮食安全保障能力。

Abstract: Forecasting agricultural commodity prices in emerging economies is difficult due to high volatility, frequent supply disruptions, and strong cultural influences on demand. This study introduces the Kalimati Vegetable Price Index (KVPI), a new inverse-volatility weighted composite index that aggregates 135 daily wholesale commodities from Kathmandu over ten years (2013-2023). By creating a stable macro-level signal, the KVPI reduces the noise inherent in modelling individual crops. A rich set of 64 causally valid features was developed, including festival lead-lag effects, rolling statistics, and calendar variables. Fourteen forecasting models spanning statistical, tree-based, deep learning, hybrid, and transformer architectures were rigorously evaluated across short (7-day), medium (14- and 30-day), and long-term (90-day) horizons. Tree-based ensembles proved notably robust, while classical statistical models and complex transformers struggled with the noisy dataset. The proposed Momentum-Corrected Online Stacking Ensemble achieved the strongest performance, yielding a Root Mean Square Error (RMSE) of 1.771, an exceptionally low Mean Absolute Percentage Error (MAPE) of 0.68%, and explaining 84.5% of the variance (R-squared = 0.845) at the 90-day horizon. This open-source pipeline provides policymakers and supply chain actors in Nepal and similar markets with a practical, reliable tool for anticipating price movements and strengthening food security.

### [221] [OrcaRouter: A Production-Oriented LLM Router with Hybrid Offline-Online Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30736)
*Zhenghua Bao,Fengya Tian,Chris Zhang,Zhenjun Chen,Xile Ma,Yi Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OrcaRouter 是一个面向生产环境的大型语言模型路由系统，结合了基于上下文的 LinUCB 带有词法和句子嵌入特征的强化学习方法，采用离线-在线混合学习策略。离线阶段通过在精选提示集上评估各候选模型获得完整反馈，构建奖励矩阵并训练每个模型臂的岭回归器；部署时初始化参数，并可选择性地根据带宽反馈持续学习，仅更新被选中模型的臂。在 2026 年 5 月 20 日提交时，OrcaRouter-Adaptive 在公开 RouterArena 排行榜中位列第二，得分为 72.08，每千次查询成本为 1.00 美元，准确率达 75.54%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型的快速发展，不同模型具有各异的能力与推理成本，如何在实际部署中为请求动态选择最优模型成为关键挑战。现有方法缺乏对模型性能与成本之间权衡的有效建模，且难以在真实环境中持续优化。因此需要一种高效、可扩展且能兼顾性能与成本的智能路由机制。

Method: 提出 OrcaRouter，采用基于上下文的 LinUCB 带有词法和句子嵌入特征的上下文带宽算法；结合离线预训练与在线自适应学习：离线阶段通过全信息反馈训练每个模型臂的岭回归器；部署阶段初始化参数，支持基于带宽反馈的增量更新，仅更新所选模型的臂。

Result: 在 2026 年 5 月 20 日提交时，OrcaRouter-Adaptive 在 RouterArena 公开排行榜中排名第二，得分为 72.08，实现 75.54% 的准确率，每千次查询成本仅为 1.00 美元，证明其在性能与成本之间实现了良好平衡。

Conclusion: OrcaRouter 有效解决了多模型部署中的动态路由问题，通过融合离线训练与在线学习，实现了高精度、低成本的智能调度，在真实场景中具备良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Abstract: The rapid development of large language models, each with distinct capabilities and inference costs, raises a practical deployment question: given an incoming request, which model should handle it? We present OrcaRouter, a production-oriented LLM router that combines a LinUCB-based contextual bandit over lexical and sentence-embedding features with a hybrid offline-online learning protocol. Offline, OrcaRouter obtains full-information feedback by evaluating each candidate model on a curated set of routing prompts, yielding a reward matrix used to fit one ridge regressor per arm. At deployment time, it initializes from these parameters and can optionally continue learning from bandit feedback, updating only the selected model's arm after observing its reward. At the time of our RouterArena submission (May 20, 2026), OrcaRouter-Adaptive ranked second on the public RouterArena leaderboard with an arena score of 72.08, achieving 75.54% accuracy at a cost of USD 1.00 per 1,000 queries.

</details>

Abstract: Maximum entropy reinforcement learning (MaxEnt-RL) enables robust exploration, yet practical implementations often restrict policies to simple Gaussians.

### [223] [Chain-of-Thought and Compressed Looped Transformers: A Memory-Budget Separation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30757)
*Haozhou Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文比较了三种记忆机制：压缩潜在循环、完整序列状态循环和思维链草稿。研究发现，压缩循环受限于其递归状态大小，即使增加计算步数也无法扩展工作内存，因此无法解决某些复杂度问题；而思维链可通过增长的生成文本实现更大规模推理。完整序列状态循环则因保留每一步状态，表现更接近显式草稿，具有更强的记忆能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索测试时计算中不同记忆机制对模型推理能力的影响，特别是持久可变记忆在复杂推理任务中的关键作用。

Method: 通过对比压缩潜在循环、完整序列状态循环和链式思维草稿三种记忆机制，在控制实验下分析其在指针追踪和关联回忆任务中的表现，评估记忆预算与任务需求的匹配性。

Result: 压缩循环受限于小规模递归状态，无法随计算量增加而扩展工作内存，难以处理P-完全问题（在对数空间归约下）；而多项式长度的链式思维可以克服这一限制。完整序列状态循环因保留所有输入位置的状态，表现出更强的记忆能力。

Conclusion: 持久可变记忆是测试时推理的核心资源，记忆机制的设计直接影响模型的推理上限，其中链式思维和完整序列状态循环优于压缩循环。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought prompting and looped Transformers both give a fixed model more test-time computation, but they differ in what they remember. Chain-of-thought stores intermediate state in generated tokens that remain in the context, whereas a looped Transformer carries state through recurrent hidden activations. We argue that this persistent mutable memory is a central resource for test-time reasoning.
  We compare three memory regimes, the compressed latent loop, the full sequence-state loop, and the chain-of-thought scratchpad. Our main result shows that a compressed loop is limited by the size of its recurrent state. Running the loop longer adds computation but does not by itself create a growing scratchpad, so a loop with a small recurrent state remains a small-space reasoner even when run for many steps. Under a standard complexity assumption, such loops cannot decide problems that are P-complete under logspace reductions, whereas polynomial-length chain-of-thought can.
  The separation is specific to compressed loops, as full sequence-state loops carry state at every input position and live in a memory-rich regime closer to explicit scratchpads. Controlled pointer-chasing and associative-recall sweeps illustrate this memory-budget view, with performance sensitive to whether the persistent-state budget matches the task's working-memory demand.

### [224] [Efficient and Uncertainty-Aware Diffusion Framework for Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30776)
*Ha Manh Bui,Metod Jazbec,Eric Nalisnick,Anqi Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DUAL提出了一种高效的扩散不确定性感知框架，用于离线到在线强化学习。它在离线阶段利用扩散模型先验知识，蒸馏出快速采样的扩散策略和转移模型；在在线阶段，通过拉普拉斯近似和状态转移距离检测进行不确定性量化，以优化探索与利用的平衡。实验表明，DUAL在多个环境和设置中均优于现有O2O-RL基线方法。

Result: DUAL在多个环境中显著提升了在线预期回报，相较于现有的O2O-RL基线方法表现出更强的鲁棒性和数据效率，验证了其在处理分布偏移和不确定性建模方面的有效性。

Conclusion: DUAL通过融合扩散模型先验与不确定性量化机制，实现了高效、稳健的离线到在线强化学习，为减少在线交互成本并提升策略性能提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning (O2O-RL) leverages an offline, pre-trained policy to minimize costly online interactions. Although data-efficient, O2O-RL is susceptible to shifts between offline and online distributions. Existing work aims to mitigate the harm of this shift by finetuning the policy on trajectory data sampled from a diffusion model. Inspired by this line of work, we propose DUAL: an efficient \textbf{D}iffusion \textbf{U}ncertainty-\textbf{A}ware framework for offline-to-online reinforcement \textbf{L}earning. DUAL utilizes the prior knowledge of the diffusion model to distill a fast-sampling diffusion actor policy and transition model in the offline phase. DUAL also employs a Laplace approximation and distance transition-state-shift detection, thereby using uncertainty quantification to improve exploration versus exploitation in the online phase. We formally show that our actor loss with the Laplace approximation provides a proxy for a principled estimate of epistemic uncertainty. Empirically, DUAL improves the online expected return over O2O-RL baselines across multiple settings and environments.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We identify a new dimension for enhancing rollout diversity in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for LLMs. While GRPO relies on diverse rollouts, prevailing strategies primarily increase diversity by injecting more token-level randomness, which may introduce step-wise noise and lead to incoherent trajectories. We uncover that smaller models within the same model family inherently exhibit higher policy-level diversity, indicated by their superior pass@k relative to larger counterparts as sample counts increase. Unlike token-level noise, this diversity is temporally correlated, preserves logical consistency, and provides structured exploration signals for gradient estimation. We thus propose S2L-PO (Small-to-Large Policy Optimization), a framework that leverages fixed small models as natural explorers to train larger models. To balance exploration and exploitation, we design a progressive annealing strategy that transitions from offline small-model rollouts to the large learner's own sampling. This shift elegantly avoids mid-training performance drops caused by the small model's capacity limits, achieving faster convergence and unlocking a higher performance ceiling. S2L-PO improves accuracy on diverse mathematical reasoning benchmarks (e.g., +8.8% on AIME 24 using a 1.7B explorer to guide the 8B model) while reducing rollout compute.

### [226] [Conformal Reliability: A New Evaluation Metric for Conditional Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30807)

Existing metrics, which typically assess a single output, may fail to capture the variability or potential risks in generation. In this paper, we propose a novel evaluation metric called reliability score based on conformal prediction, which measures the worst-case performance within the prediction set at a pre-specified confidence level. However, computing this score is challenging due to the high-dimensional nature of the output space and the nonconvexity of both the metric function and the prediction set. To efficiently compute this score, we introduce Conformal ReLiability (CReL), a framework that can (i) construct the prediction set with desired coverage; and (ii) accurately optimize the reliability score within the constructed prediction set. We provide theoretical results on coverage and demonstrate empirically that our method produces more informative prediction sets than existing approaches. Experiments on synthetic data and the image-to-text and text-to-image tasks further demonstrate the interpretability of our new metric, and the validity and effectiveness of our computational framework. Source code can be found at https://ggc29.github.io/CReL/.
