### [282] [When Are Multimodal Predictions Biologically Supported? A Diagnostic Evaluation Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31504)
*Dylan Steiner,Gustavo Arango-Argoty,Gerald Sun,Etai Jacob*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DECAT是首个模型无关的后处理评估框架，可对多模态模型在肿瘤学中的表示进行分类，识别出共享生物学、单模态生物学或虚假相关性等四种诊断情景。通过五种零参照度量和基于规则的决策流程，无需知道具体混杂因素即可检测隐藏的混杂效应，且在证据不足时返回不确定结果。在合成数据（超2500个模型）和真实TCGA数据（8979例患者）上验证，发现如CLIP等纠缠模型虽能精准识别共享生物，但在无共享生物时仍会错误声称存在，且随着混杂强度增加，错误率上升，大样本和强表示反而增强错误信心。该方法在无配对RNA情况下成功检测到传统AUROC无法发现的混杂现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态模型在肿瘤学中虽能准确预测，但其预测准确性无法揭示模型是否学习了跨模态共享生物学、单模态特异性生物学，还是仅捕捉了由混杂因素引起的虚假相关性。因此需要一种能够区分这些情况的评估工具，以确保模型真正理解生物学机制而非依赖表面关联。

Method: 提出DECAT框架，基于五种零参照度量与规则决策流程，分析多模态模型的嵌入表示，将其归类为四种诊断情景：1）共享生物学；2）单模态生物学；3）虚假相关性（混杂）；4）无法判断。该框架不依赖模型结构，适用于任何预训练或多模态模型，无需已知混杂因子标签。

Result: 在合成数据和真实TCGA数据上的实验表明：1）纠缠模型（如CLIP）在有共享生物学时表现优异，但多数情况下在无共享时仍误判为存在；2）错误判断率随混杂强度升高而上升，即更大规模数据集和更强模型反而更自信地犯错；3）在无配对RNA条件下，DECAT成功识别出传统评估指标（如AUROC）无法察觉的隐藏混杂因素，经事后分层验证确认。

Conclusion: DECAT提供了一种有效、通用的后处理评估手段，可揭示多模态模型的真实学习机制，避免因虚假相关性导致的误导性结论。其应用表明，当前主流多模态模型在实际临床场景中可能因未被察觉的混杂因素而产生不可靠推断，强调了在模型部署前进行深入解释性评估的重要性。

Abstract: Multimodal models in oncology can produce accurate predictions, but accurate prediction does not reveal whether the model has learned biology that is shared across modalities, biology confined to one modality, or spurious correlations that reflect confounders rather than genuine biology. We introduce DECAT, a model-agnostic post-hoc evaluation framework that classifies multimodal representations into four diagnostic scenarios for a given task and modality, using five null-referenced metrics and a rule-based decision procedure. The framework operates on learned representations, requires no knowledge of which specific confounder is present, and returns indeterminate when the evidence is insufficient. We validate DECAT on synthetic data across four multimodal model classes (over 2,500 trained representations) and on real data from 8,979 TCGA patients, evaluating both multimodal embeddings and five pretrained pathology foundation models. Entangled models (e.g., CLIP) achieve near-perfect shared biology detection but falsely claim shared biology in the majority of cases where it is absent on real foundation model embeddings. This false claim rate increases with confound strength so that larger cohorts and stronger representations produce more confident but still incorrect diagnoses. Applied to both multimodal TCGA embeddings and five pathology foundation models without paired RNA, DECAT detects confounding invisible to AUROC without requiring the confounder labels, as confirmed by post-hoc stratification.

### [284] [Value Functions as Supermartingale Certificates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31524)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文建立了随机系统的形式化验证与强化学习之间的新理论联系：在适当的奖励函数下，几乎必然满足ω-正则性质的策略所对应的值函数可编码为该规范的Streett超鞅证书。这一结果在有限、可数无限和连续状态空间中均成立，为通过强化学习合成验证证书提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有认证方法虽能提供对ω-正则性质的充分证明规则，但强化学习方法通常缺乏形式化保证，尤其在非有限状态空间中无法确保策略满足规范。因此需要建立两者之间的理论桥梁。

Method: 通过分析策略值函数与Streett超鞅证书之间的关系，证明在特定奖励设计下，满足ω-正则性质的策略其值函数即为有效的超鞅证书，并在有限马尔可夫决策过程上进行实验验证。

Result: 证明了值函数作为超鞅证书的有效性，且该结论适用于有限、可数无限及连续状态空间；实验验证了方法的可行性。

Conclusion: 该研究为基于强化学习的自动证书合成提供了新的理论路径，实现了形式化验证与强化学习的有机结合。

Abstract: Certification methods for stochastic systems provide sufficient proof rules, based on real-valued supermartingale certificates, to determine the almost-sure satisfaction of $ω$-regular properties (and therefore of linear temporal logic) over general state spaces, encompassing both countably infinite and continuous state spaces. Conversely, reinforcement learning (RL) methods for $ω$-regular tasks have received considerable attention, but they typically lack formal guarantees that the learned policy satisfies the specification, except possibly for finite state and action spaces. We bridge these two lines of research by establishing a novel theoretical connection: under an appropriate reward, the value function associated to a policy that almost surely satisfies an $ω$-regular property encodes a Streett supermartingale certificate for that specification. Our results, validated experimentally on finite Markov decision processes, hold for finite, countably infinite, and continuous state spaces, suggesting a principled route to certificate synthesis via RL.

### [285] [The Dynamic-Probabilistic Consistency Gap in Chaotic Surrogate Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31547)
*Andre Herz,Matthijs Pals,Daniel Durstewitz,Georgia Koppe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了动态系统重构（DSR）中的不确定性估计问题，揭示了动态-概率一致性（DPC）缺口：追求有限时间的概率目标可能导致动力学退化或使预测不确定性与局部切线动力学脱节。作者识别出三种导致该缺口的机制：核心坍缩、噪声掩盖和盲不确定性。针对此问题，提出KAFFEE框架，基于可微分扩展卡尔曼滤波器，在局部预测残差上评估似然，并通过学习到的局部雅可比矩阵传播协方差。在随机超混沌Lorenz-96系统中，KAFFEE有效缓解了失败模式，提升了动力学不变量的重建效果，同时保持了竞争性的预测性能。此外，在13个混沌系统上的实验表明，KAFFEE支持上下文内贝叶斯滤波，同时基本保留零样本动力学特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态系统重构方法在追求概率性目标时，常导致预测不确定性与真实动力学行为不一致，尤其在混沌系统中，这种不一致性会削弱模型的物理意义和可靠性。因此需要一种能够保证不确定性与局部动力学紧密耦合的方法。

Method: 提出KAFFEE框架，结合可微分扩展卡尔曼滤波器，利用局部预测残差（innovations）计算似然，并通过学习的局部雅可比矩阵精确传播协方差，从而实现动态与概率的一致性建模。

Result: 在超混沌Lorenz-96系统上，KAFFEE显著减少动态失效模式，提升对动力学不变量的重建能力，同时保持良好的预测性能；在13个混沌系统的迁移任务中，成功实现上下文内贝叶斯滤波并维持零样本动力学特性。

Conclusion: KAFFEE通过强化动态-概率一致性，有效缓解了传统开放环概率目标带来的建模偏差，为动态系统重构提供了更可靠且物理意义明确的不确定性估计方案。

Abstract: Dynamical systems reconstruction (DSR) aims to learn surrogate models that capture the dynamics underlying time-series data. Reliably deploying these surrogates requires uncertainty estimates consistent with the learned dynamics. We expose a dynamic-probabilistic consistency (DPC) gap: the pursuit of finite-horizon probabilistic objectives can degrade dynamics or decouple predictive uncertainty from the local tangent dynamics it ought to reflect. We isolate three mechanisms behind this gap: core collapse, noise masking, and blind uncertainty. Specifically, we show that open-loop Gaussian rollout objectives can penalize Jacobian-generated covariance growth in chaotic systems, encouraging optimization shortcuts that weaken physical expansion or decouple uncertainty from it. To mitigate this gap, we propose KAFFEE (Kalman-Aware Framework For Ergodic Emulation), a differentiable extended Kalman filter-based training framework that evaluates likelihood on local predictive residuals (innovations) while transporting covariance through learned local Jacobians. On stochastic hyperchaotic Lorenz-96, KAFFEE reduces the identified failure modes, improves reconstruction of dynamical invariants relative to open-loop objectives, and maintains competitive predictive scores. We further show that the DPC gap appears when probabilistically adapting a DSR foundation model across 13 chaotic systems, where KAFFEE enables in-context Bayesian filtering while largely preserving zero-shot dynamics.

### [286] [Functional Attention: From Pairwise Affinities to Functional Correspondences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31559)
*Jiefang Xiao,Maolin Gao,Simon Weber,Guandao Yang,Daniel Cremers*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Functional Attention，通过将注意力重新解释为自适应基之间的函数对应关系，替代传统的逐标记注意力，从而在连续场中捕捉全局依赖性，并实现分辨率不变的紧凑表示。该方法在求解PDE、3D分割和回归等任务中表现优异，且对离散化变化具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的算子学习方法通常将连续函数空间视为离散标记，忽略全局函数结构，导致性能受限于离散化方式。需要一种能保留函数整体结构并具备泛化能力的新机制。

Method: 引入Functional Attention，用结构化的线性算子替代softmax亲和度，将注意力机制建模为自适应基之间的函数对应关系，从而显式捕捉全局依赖性，实现分辨率无关的表示。

Result: 在多个算子学习任务（如求解偏微分方程、3D分割、回归）中达到或超过现有最优性能，且对不同网格离散化保持稳定。

Conclusion: Functional Attention通过重新定义注意力为函数级对应关系，提供了一种更本质、更通用且可推广的算子学习框架，尤其适用于需保持函数结构一致性的场景。

Abstract: Learning mappings between infinite-dimensional function spaces, or operator learning, is essential for many machine learning applications. Although transformer-based operators are popular, they often rely on token-wise attention. These methods treat continuous fields as discrete tokens and usually ignore the global functional structure. We introduce \emph{Functional Attention}, which reinterprets attention as a functional correspondence between adaptive bases. Inspired by geometric functional maps, our method replaces softmax affinities with structured linear operators. This yields a compact, generalizable, resolution-invariant representation that explicitly captures global dependencies. Experiments demonstrate that \emph{Functional Attention} can match state-of-the-art performance in many operator learning tasks, including solving PDEs, 3D segmentation, and regression, while remaining robust to varying discretizations. Project page is available at https://github.com/xjffff/FUNCATTN.

</details>


### [287] [Effective Biological Representation Learning by Masking Gene Expression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31562)
*Kian Kenyon-Dean,Alina Selega,Ihab Bendidi,Jordan M. Sorokin,Luca Bertinetto,David Errington,Hayley Donnella,Oren Kraus*

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种新的自监督模型TxFM，通过针对多样化的RNA-seq计数数据设计的掩码自动编码方法，实现对转录组数据的有效建模。研究发现，经过精心设计的模型架构与高质量的数据集（DiverseRNA-1.4M）结合，可显著提升基因表达表示的质量，优于在规模大100倍的数据库上训练的现有基础模型。结果表明，在适当的架构和数据清洗条件下，归纳式自监督学习在转录组学表征中具有明显优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有转录组基础模型在技术噪声和实验批次效应下表现不佳，其性能甚至不如线性基线模型，这引发疑问：深度表示学习是否真能超越直接使用原始转录本计数？因此，亟需探索更有效的自监督学习范式以提升转录组数据建模能力。

Method: 提出TxFM模型，采用专为多样化RNA-seq计数数据设计的掩码自动编码机制；通过消融实验确定关键架构配置；构建并使用公开的大型训练语料库DiverseRNA-1.4M进行训练与评估。

Result: TxFM在所用数据集上生成了高保真度的基因表示，其性能超越在规模超过100倍的图谱级数据集上训练的基础模型，证明了归纳式自监督学习在转录组学中的有效性。

Conclusion: 在合理的设计模型架构与严格的数据集清洗前提下，归纳式自监督学习是转录组学表示学习的一种可行且高效的建模方法。

Abstract: RNA sequencing produces rich and diverse datasets of gene expression, offering compelling insights into cellular state and function that have many applications in drug discovery. Modeling such data is challenging due to inherent technical noise and experimental batch effects, as evidenced by many existing transcriptomic foundation models (FMs) underperforming relative to linear baselines. Such results raise the question of whether deep representation learning provides a distinct advantage over the direct use of raw transcript counts. Our work explores this by developing a new self-supervised model, TxFM, with a focus on inductive representation learning evaluations. TxFM employs a masked autoencoding approach tailored to diverse RNA-seq count data, and our ablation study empirically identifies crucial architecture configurations required for strong transfer performance. Additionally, we curate a public training corpus, DiverseRNA-1.4M, and find that TxFM trained on this curated dataset yields high-fidelity gene representations that outperform FMs trained on atlas-scale corpora over 100x larger. Overall, our results indicate that inductive self-supervised learning is a viable modeling approach for transcriptomics representation, provided a careful synthesis of model architecture and training data curation.

### [288] [Giving Sensors a Voice: Multimodal JEPA for Semantic Time-Series Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31580)
*Utsav Dutta,Gerardo Pastrana,Sina Khoshfetrat Pakazad,Henrik Ohlsson*

TL;DR: CHARM 是一种用于异构多变量时间序列的通用表示学习模型，通过将通道级文本描述融入 Transformer 编码器，实现对通道顺序的等变性。采用联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）和新型损失函数，使嵌入具备信息量且时序稳定。通过潜在空间预测增强对传感器噪声的鲁棒性，通过描述感知门控提升可解释性。在异常检测、分类及短/长期预测任务中，仅用线性探测器即取得优异性能，主要得益于 JEPA 目标与条件架构，文本描述则作为跨数据集泛化的通道标识符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于 Transformer 的架构虽在语言和视觉序列建模中取得进展，但针对异构多变量时间序列的通用表示学习仍缺乏有效方法。现有方法难以处理通道间异质性与顺序敏感性问题，且缺乏可解释性与跨数据集泛化能力。因此亟需一种能融合通道语义信息、保持等变性并支持高效下游任务的表示学习框架。

Method: 提出 CHARM 模型，利用通道级文本描述作为语义先验，嵌入到 Transformer 编码器中，确保对通道顺序的等变性；采用联合嵌入预测架构（JEPA）进行无监督预训练，并设计新型损失函数以促进嵌入的信息性与时序稳定性；引入描述感知门控机制以揭示通道间关系，提升可解释性；通过潜在空间预测增强对传感器噪声的鲁棒性。

Result: 在异常检测、分类、短期与长期预测任务中，基于 CHARM 学习的嵌入仅使用线性探测器即达到高性能；实验表明，性能主要由 JEPA 目标与条件架构驱动，而文本描述在跨数据集泛化中起到关键作用，作为通道标识符帮助模型迁移知识。

Conclusion: CHARM 为异构多变量时间序列提供了有效的通用表示学习方案，结合文本描述与等变 Transformer 架构，在多种下游任务中展现出强泛化能力与可解释性，验证了语义先验与结构约束在复杂序列建模中的重要性。

Abstract: Transformer-based architectures have advanced sequence modeling in language and vision, yet general-purpose representation learning for heterogeneous multivariate time series remains underexplored. We introduce CHARM (Channel-Aware Representation Model), which incorporates channel-level textual descriptions into a Transformer encoder equivariant to channel order. CHARM is trained with a Joint Embedding Predictive Architecture (JEPA) and a novel loss promoting informative, temporally stable embeddings; latent-space prediction encourages robustness to sensor noise while description-aware gating provides interpretability through learned inter-channel relationships. Across anomaly detection, classification, and short- and long-term forecasting, the learned embeddings achieve strong performance using only a linear probe. Performance is driven primarily by the JEPA objective and conditioning architecture, with text descriptions serving as channel identifiers for cross-dataset generalization.

### [289] [A Tight Theory of Error Feedback Algorithms in Distributed Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31594)
*Daniel Berg Thomsen,Adrien Taylor,Aymeric Dieuleveut*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对两种主流的误差反馈算法——经典误差反馈（EF）和EF21进行了紧致的收敛性分析，通过识别最优步长并构造针对每种方法的最优李雅普诺夫函数，实现了在多智能体环境下与单智能体情形下最优收敛保证一致的理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通信开销是分布式学习和一阶优化中的主要瓶颈，虽然梯度压缩可缓解该问题，但通常会损害梯度方法的收敛性。误差反馈机制虽能有效弥补这一缺陷，但其多种变体的性能对比尚不清晰。因此亟需对主流算法进行严格的理论分析以明确其性能边界。

Method: 通过构建针对不同误差反馈算法（EF 和 EF21）的定制化李雅普诺夫函数，并结合最优步长选择策略，进行紧致收敛性分析。

Result: 证明了在任意数量智能体下，该分析均能恢复单智能体场景下的最优收敛率，且为现有文献中最佳保证。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了误差反馈算法在分布式优化中的理论极限，提供了统一且紧致的收敛性分析框架，有助于理解并指导实际应用中算法的选择与参数设计。

Abstract: Communication costs are a major bottleneck in distributed learning and first-order optimization. A common approach to alleviate this issue is to compress the gradient information exchanged between agents. However, such compression typically degrades the convergence guarantees of gradient-based methods. Error feedback mechanisms provide a simple and computationally cheap remedy for this issue, but numerous variants have been proposed, and their relative performance remains poorly understood. This paper provides tight convergence analyses for two of the main error-feedback algorithms from the literature, the classic Error Feedback method (EF) and Error Feedback 21 (EF21), by identifying optimal step-size choices and constructing optimal Lyapunov functions tailored to each method. The results hold independently of the number of agents and recover the known best guarantees possible in the single-agent regime.

</details>

### [290] [PhyDrawGen: Physically Grounded Diagram Generation from Natural Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30512)
*Nafiul Haque,Syed Nazmus Sakib,Shifat E Arman*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PhyDrawGen 是一种神经符号框架，用于从文本生成符合物理定律的物理图。它通过大语言模型提取场景图，再由确定性求解器将其转换为平面直线图（PSLG），精确编码力平衡、光路和场拓扑等约束。最后，使用微调的 Qwen-VL 模型进行视觉引导的“提出-验证”循环以纠正偏差。在涵盖力学、光学和电磁学的 1,449 个问题上评估，显著优于 GPT-5-image、Gemini 2.5 Flash 和 Gemini 3 Pro，尤其在罕见物体问题上表现出强鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型虽能产出视觉上合理的物理图，但常出现力矢量幻觉、违反守恒定律及几何约束等问题。为实现真正的物理准确性，需要将语义理解与物理约束满足解耦，确保生成结果不仅美观且严格遵循物理规律。

Method: 采用神经符号架构：首先用大语言模型构建带类型的场景图；然后由确定性求解器将其转化为平面直线图（PSLG），将力平衡、光路、场拓扑等作为精确几何原型表达；最后利用微调的 Qwen-VL 模型执行视觉引导的迭代式‘提出-验证’修正过程，确保所有物理约束被满足。

Result: 在 1,449 个跨领域的物理问题测试中，PhyDrawGen 在物理准确性上显著优于 GPT-5-image、Gemini 2.5 Flash 与 Gemini 3 Pro，尤其在处理包含罕见或复杂对象的问题时表现更优，证明其在真实物理建模中的高可靠性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: PhyDrawGen 成功实现了从文本到物理一致图的生成，通过解耦语义理解与物理约束满足，结合符号推理与视觉反馈机制，在多个物理领域展现出卓越的准确性和鲁棒性，为未来可信赖的物理生成系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Generating physics diagrams from text requires strict adherence to physical laws. While current generative models produce visually plausible outputs, they systematically hallucinate force vectors, ignore conservation laws, and violate geometric constraints. We present PhyDrawGen, a neuro-symbolic pipeline that decouples semantic scene understanding from physical constraint satisfaction. First, a large language model extracts a typed scene graph from the problem text. A deterministic solver then converts this graph into a Planar Straight-Line Graph (PSLG), encoding force balance, optical paths, and field topologies as exact geometric primitives. Finally, a fine-tuned Qwen-VL model implements a visually grounded propose-verify loop to iteratively correct any constraint violations. Evaluated on a benchmark of 1,449 problems spanning mechanics, optics, and electromagnetism, PhyDrawGen significantly outperforms GPT-5-image, Gemini 2.5 Flash, and Gemini 3 Pro, demonstrating robust physical accuracy even on unusual-object problems.

</details>


### [291] [Physically Viable World Models: A Case for Query-Conditioned Embodied AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30542)
*Adam J. Thorpe,Stepan Tretiakov,Cheng-Hsi Hsiao,Su Ann Low,Xingjian Li,Hassan Iqbal,Neel P. Bhatt,Ufuk Topcu,Krishna Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出，具身人工智能的世界模型必须具备物理可行性，即能够通过表征决定行动结果的物理结构来回答干预查询，而非仅仅预测未来观察。现有观测预测型模型虽能生成视觉上合理但物理错误的推演，其根本问题在于结构缺陷：不同物理系统可能外观相同，但在干预下表现迥异。作者通过受控基准测试验证此问题，发现此类模型可能推荐不可行动作、误判交互结果或认证危险行为。为此，提出需构建基于最简物理抽象的世界模型，该模型由环境表示、隐状态与参数估计、动作定义、干预动力学和查询响应等模块组成。一个自主协调器应根据查询选择合适的抽象并组合学习与结构化组件。当无法获得解析物理规律时，过渡模型可为分析式、模拟式、学习式或混合式，但必须保持决定干预结果的结构。这种分解使模型可解释、各组件可验证、输出可审计，并为新模型设计提供原则，同时作为现有模型的可行性检验标准：正确抽象并非最详细模型，而是保留查询相关区别的最简模型。文中展示了该方法在现有系统无法正确回答的问题上的应用，并概述了协调器如何动态组装和调整物理可行模型以支持规划、控制与验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型仅关注预测未来观测，导致生成的推演在视觉上合理但物理上错误，尤其在干预场景中表现不佳。这限制了具身智能系统的可靠性与安全性，亟需一种能准确反映物理结构、支持干预推理的世界模型。

Method: 提出基于最简物理抽象的世界模型框架，包含环境表示、隐状态与参数估计、动作指定、干预动力学与查询响应等模块；引入自主协调器动态选择与组合组件；采用受控基准测试验证模型在干预下的表现；设计可解释、可验证、可审计的结构化建模方式。

Result: 所提框架能正确处理现有系统失败的干预查询，避免推荐不可行动作、误判交互结果或认证危险行为；模型具备可解释性、可验证性和可审计性；为新模型设计提供明确原则，也为评估现有模型提供可行性测试标准。

Conclusion: 具身人工智能需要的不是最详细的模型，而是最简且能保留查询相关物理差异的模型。通过模块化结构与协调机制，可实现物理可行的世界建模，提升规划、控制与验证的安全性与可靠性。

Abstract: World models for embodied AI must be physically viable: constructed to answer intervention queries by representing the physical structure governing action outcomes, rather than merely predicting future observations. Existing observation-predictive world models can produce visually plausible but physically wrong rollouts. This failure is structural; distinct physical systems can look identical yet diverge under intervention. We expose this problem with controlled benchmarks that fix the visible scene while varying latent physics. We show that such models may recommend infeasible actions, mispredict interaction outcomes, or certify unsafe behavior. We argue that embodied AI requires world models that identify the simplest physical abstraction sufficient to answer an intervention query. Such a model comprises modular components, including environment representation, latent state and parameter estimation, action specification, interventional dynamics, and query-level response. An autonomous orchestrator should identify the relevant abstraction and compose compatible learned and structured components per query. When closed-form physics is unavailable, uncertain, or costly, the transition model may be analytic, simulated, learned, or hybrid, but it must preserve the structure that determines interventional outcomes. This decomposition makes the model interpretable, its components verifiable, and its outputs auditable against the query. It also provides a design principle for new world models and a feasibility test for existing ones: the right abstraction is not the most detailed model of the world, but the simplest model that preserves the distinctions relevant to the query. We demonstrate this approach on queries that existing systems fail to answer correctly, and outline how an orchestrator can dynamically assemble and adapt physically viable models for planning, control, and verification.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate the application of MAP-Elites (a well-known quality diversity algorithm) to design levels for First-Person Shooter (FPS) games. ### [294] [EHRBench: An Automated and Reliable EHR-based Benchmark for Clinical Decision Making with LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30637)
*Yuzhang Xie,Keqi Han,Yunpeng Xiao,Hejie Cui,Guanchen Wu,Ziyang Zhang,Kai Shu,Jiaying Lu,Xiao Hu,Carl Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出EHRBench，一个基于电子健康记录（EHR）的自动化、可靠且可扩展的临床决策（CDM）评估基准，用于评估基于大语言模型（LLM）的临床决策能力。通过EHR-LLM-KB交互流程，将患者就诊轨迹自动转化为结构化模板，并生成近100万条涵盖诊断、治疗和预后三类任务的问答数据。同时结合知识库进行验证与增强，确保数据质量。在该基准上对30多个主流LLM进行了评测，结果揭示了模型性能的一致趋势，验证了基准可靠性，并指出了当前LLM在临床应用中的关键差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在真实临床决策任务中的可靠性尚不明确，缺乏一个既大规模又高质量、基于真实EHR数据的评估基准，难以有效衡量其在实际医疗场景中的表现。因此亟需构建一个自动化、可靠且与真实临床实践紧密结合的评估体系。

Method: 采用EHR-LLM-KB交互管道：首先使用专用LLM将个体患者就诊记录转化为结构化模板；然后基于模板自动生成标准化问答对；同时利用知识库对生成内容进行系统性验证与纠错，剔除幻觉或模糊关系，提升数据可靠性。整个流程实现高效、可扩展的数据构造。

Result: 成功构建包含960,067个高质量问答项的EHRBench基准，覆盖诊断、治疗和预后三大临床推理任务。在该基准上对超过30个代表性LLM进行评测，结果显示模型性能趋势一致，证明了基准的可靠性和有效性，并揭示出当前LLM在临床推理中仍存在显著不足，为未来改进提供方向。

Conclusion: EHRBench是一个高效、可靠、基于真实EHR数据的临床决策评估基准，能够有效支持大规模LLM评测。其构建方法具有可复制性，所揭示的模型短板也为开发更可信的临床AI系统提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Clinical decision-making (CDM) is central to real-world clinical workflows, where clinicians infer diagnoses, select treatments, or anticipate future health outcomes under incomplete evidence. LLMs are increasingly used to support these decisions due to strong language capabilities, broad biomedical knowledge, and efficiency, yet the reliability of LLMs on real-world clinical decision tasks remains insufficiently understood. To evaluate CDM models, especially LLM-based models, an ideal and practical medical decision benchmark should be constructed via an automated yet reliable pipeline to ensure both scale and quality. Moreover, the grounding of a CDM benchmark in real patient EHRs can better support evaluation on practical CDM tasks that require substantive biomedical knowledge and clinical inference. To fill the gaps, we introduce EHRBench, an automated and reliable EHR-grounded benchmark for evaluating LLM-based clinical decision-making at scale. To ensure scalability and reliability, EHRBench is constructed through an EHR-LLM-KB(knowledge-base) interaction pipeline. For efficiency, we use a specialized LLM to automatically convert encounter-level EHR trajectories into structured templates and deterministically instantiate the templates into QA items. In parallel, we apply systematic KB-based verification and enrichment to filter hallucinated or ambiguous relations and to improve reliability. Using this pipeline, we construct nearly 1M (960,067) QA items spanning three core inference-required clinical decision tasks: diagnosis, treatment, and prognosis. We benchmark more than 30 representative LLMs on EHRBench and provide detailed analyses of performance and robustness. The results show consistent capability trends across settings, further validating the reliability of EHRBench and highlighting actionable gaps toward clinically reliable LLM systems.

### [295] [Structure-Induced Information for Rerooting Levin Tree Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30664)
*Jake Tuero,Michael Buro,Laurent Orseau,Levi H. S. Lelis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于学习的‘重根器’（rerooter）来改进基于子目标的策略树搜索，通过隐式分解问题为软子任务，避免了显式生成子目标带来的高开销，提升了可扩展性。提出了三种重根器设计：基于聚类、基于启发式和混合方法，显著降低计算开销，并在复杂环境中实现优于现有方法的在线训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于子目标的策略树搜索依赖显式子目标生成，导致计算开销大且难以扩展，尤其在复杂环境中表现不佳。因此需要一种无需显式子目标、能高效分配搜索资源的新方法。

Method: 引入$\sqrt{\text{LTS}}$算法训练一个学习型重根器，通过隐式分解状态空间为软子任务；设计三种重根器：基于聚类以利用全局状态结构、基于启发式使用学习的成本到目标估计、以及结合两者的混合方法。

Result: 所提方法在复杂环境中表现出更强的可扩展性，解决了传统子目标方法无法处理的问题；在多个测试领域中实现了当前最优的在线训练效率，且计算开销显著降低。

Conclusion: 通过学习重根器实现对问题的隐式分层分解，有效克服了显式子目标生成的瓶颈，为复杂单智能体确定性问题提供了高效、可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Subgoal-based policy tree search, which uses a policy to guide search, is effective for complex single-agent deterministic problems but often relies on explicit subgoal generation that can incur substantial overhead and hinders scalability. In this paper, we overcome these limitations by using a learned ``rerooter'' through the recently-introduced $\sqrt{\text{LTS}}$ algorithm. A rerooter implicitly decomposes the problem into soft subtasks. While previous work focused on the formal guarantees for given or handcrafted rerooters, in this work we propose three rerooter designs: (i) a clustering-based rerooter that exploits global state-space structure, (ii) a heuristic-based rerooter that leverages learned cost-to-go estimates, and (iii) a hybrid that combines both signals. Our framework avoids having to explicitly reconstruct and reason over generated subgoals, thereby enabling scalable allocation of search effort with significantly lower computational overhead. Empirically, our rerooting-based methods scale to complex environments where subgoal-based policy tree search fails, and achieve state-of-the-art online training efficiency on the domains tested.

An incentive sweep recovers classical health-economics findings as adjacent regimes -- up-coding and low-complexity-patient selection under profit pressure, and Goodhart-style drift where measured performance becomes anti-correlated with true outcomes -- and a single audit lever exposes pressure migration: closing the coding channel more than doubles low-complexity selection. ### [298] [Generating Graph-like Rules for Knowledge Graph Reasoning via Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30747)
*Haoxiang Cheng,Yunfei Wang,Chao Chen,Kewei Cheng,Zhipeng Lin,Haoxuan Li,Changjun Fan,Shixuan Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GRiD 是一种用于发现图结构规则的框架，通过将规则发现重构为基于目标关系的离散生成过程，结合监督预训练与强化学习，有效解决传统方法在处理复杂图结构规则时的计算瓶颈和质量评估难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有规则挖掘方法主要关注简单的链式规则，忽视了知识图谱中丰富的图结构信息（如环路和分支），且受搜索空间组合爆炸限制，难以高效发现复杂规则；同时，生成模型如扩散模型因训练目标与规则质量不匹配、无法处理非可微的质量指标，难以直接应用于规则挖掘。

Method: GRiD 将图结构规则发现建模为条件离散生成任务，采用两阶段训练策略：首先通过监督预训练从知识图谱元图采样子图以学习结构先验；然后利用强化学习和策略梯度优化，直接以不可微的规则质量指标作为奖励信号进行微调。

Abstract: Logical rules constitute a cornerstone of knowledge graph (KG) reasoning, valued for their interpretability and ability to model relational patterns. However, existing rule mining methods predominantly focus on simple chain-like rules and therefore neglect the richer relational information encoded in graph-like structures, such as cycles and branches. This limitation is further exacerbated by computational bottlenecks caused by the combinatorial explosion of the search space, which is especially challenging for graph-like rules. Meanwhile, generative approaches such as diffusion models, despite their success in other domains, can not be directly applied to rule mining because their training objectives are not aligned with the goal of learning high-quality rules, and non-differentiable KG rule quality metrics cannot directly guide model optimization. To address these limitations, we propose GRiD, a framework that reformulates graph-like rule discovery as a discrete generative process conditioned on the target relation. GRiD employs a two-phase training strategy. First, supervised pre-training enables GRiD to capture structural priors from subgraphs sampled from the KG meta-graph. Subsequently, reinforcement learning is applied to fine-tune GRiD through policy gradient optimization guided directly by non-differentiable rule-quality metrics. Experiments on six benchmark datasets show that GRiD achieves competitive performance on KG completion tasks. Ablation studies confirm the efficiency and robustness of GRiD and further show that graph-like rules complement chain-like rules in KG completion. Our codes and datasets are available in https://github.com/Haoxiang-Cheng/GRiD

### [299] [PReMISE: Policy Rubrics as Measurement Specifications for LLM Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30803)
*Swastik Roy,Rajkumar Pujari,Tharindu Kumarage,Charith Peris,Rahul Gupta,Anna Rumshisky,Pradeep Natarajan,Venkatesh Saligrama*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出PReMISE框架，用于发现和审计LLM判别器所使用的评分标准（rubrics），解决现有评分标准在开放性回答评估中因模糊而被滥用的问题。通过分析人类偏好数据，PReMISE能自动发现高质量的政策级评分标准，并从结构合理性、可靠性、偏好匹配度和对抗鲁棒性四个维度进行审计。实验表明，无一现有评分源同时具备高可靠性、偏好预测性和抗攻击性；而高评分者间一致性并不意味着低可利用性。PReMISE是唯一在适用性、具体性和有效维度上均表现良好的评分源。研究还引入两种修复操作：偏好排序选择使判别准确率从65.0%提升至68.6%，可靠性约束优化将易攻破响应的高分率从46.4%降至36.0%，且对评分一致性影响极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM判别器在评估开放性回答时严重依赖评分标准，但模糊的评分标准（如‘有帮助且事实正确’）容易导致模型生成看似合理实则虚构或违背用户意图的内容。因此需要一种机制来发现并评估评分标准的质量，以确保评估结果真实反映响应质量。

Method: 提出PReMISE框架，基于成对的人类偏好数据，通过自动化方法发现政策层级的评分标准集，并设计四维审计指标（结构适切性、可靠性、偏好拟合度、对抗鲁棒性）对任意评分标准集进行评估。此外，引入两种修复操作：偏好排序选择与可靠性约束优化，以提升评分标准的有效性与安全性。

Result: 实验显示，所有现有评分来源均无法同时满足可靠性、偏好预测性和对抗鲁棒性；高评分者一致性不等于低可利用性。PReMISE是唯一在适用性、具体性和有效维度上均表现优异的评分源。偏好排序选择使判别准确率从65.0%提升至68.6%，可靠性约束优化将高分易攻破响应率从46.4%降至36.0%，且评分一致性变化极小（α从0.531降至0.519）。

Conclusion: PReMISE提供了一种系统化发现与审计评分标准的方法，显著提升了LLM判别器在开放性任务评估中的可信度与稳健性，为构建更可靠、可解释的自动评估体系提供了新范式。

Abstract: LLM judges are increasingly used to evaluate open-ended responses, but their scores depend strongly on the rubrics that condition them. A vague rubric asking for a response to be ``helpful and factual'' can reward polished answers that invent facts or violate user intent. We treat reusable rubrics as measurement specifications: changing the rubric changes the response quality measurement induced by a fixed judge. We introduce PReMISE, a framework that, given pairwise human-preference data, (i) discovers a policy-level rubric set, and (ii) audits any rubric set under LLM-judge use along four axes: structural adequacy, reliability, preference fit, and adversarial robustness. Across rubric sources no raw source is simultaneously reliable, preference-predictive, and adversarially robust; and high inter-rater agreement does not imply low exploitability. PReMISE is the only rubric source to score non-trivially on applicability, specificity, and effective dimensionality simultaneously. We contribute two audit-targeted repair operations: preference-rank selection raises judge accuracy on paired responses from $65.0\%$ to $68.6\%$, competitive with the strongest rubric-discovery baselines and leading on two of three judges in our cross-judge sweep; reliability-constrained refinement reduces the rate at which exploit responses receive high scores from $46.4\%$ to $36.0\%$ with little change in inter-judge agreement ($α{=}.531\to.519$).

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Deep research tasks require LLMs to plan what to investigate, retrieve evidence, and synthesize long-form answers across multiple branches of inquiry. Existing training paradigms either rely on short-form verifiable QA as a proxy or optimize monolithic long trajectories, which makes planning and execution difficult to disentangle and yields weak credit assignment for the planning process. We propose DecomposeR, a planner-centric deep research framework that represents research plans as typed directed acyclic graphs (DAGs), allowing planning to be made explicit, structured, and rewardable. We train a Qwen3-8B model in two stages: planner reinforcement learning (RL) first learns graph structure and query decomposition to improve research planning, and answerer reinforcement learning (RL) then learns branch-level execution and final synthesis conditioned on the learned plan. By assigning rewards to explicit planner tokens and structured components rather than to a flat trajectory, DecomposeR enables finer-grained optimization of planning while reducing the ambiguity of end-to-end training. Experiments show that DecomposeR-8B improves over strong comparable open baselines by 5.1-8.0 points on popular long-form benchmarks due to improved planning and answering capabilities.

### [301] [SLAT: Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming for Efficient CoT Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30832)
*Jian Yao,Xiongcai Luo,Ran Cheng,Kay Chen Tan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为SLAT（Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming）的强化学习框架，旨在解决大型推理模型中链式思维（CoT）生成存在的结构冗余问题（即过度思考）。传统方法使用统一的长度惩罚，难以区分有用推理与冗余内容。本文发现冗余集中在高概率但边际效用低的段落，并基于正确性-长度权衡目标，理论分析了段落次优性，进而设计了针对性剪枝策略。实验表明，SLAT在标准基准上显著降低50%的推理长度，同时保持竞争力的准确率，实现了更优的准确性-效率权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通过统一的长度惩罚来减少推理长度，但无法区分有用推理和冗余信息，导致可能抑制有效推理。本文旨在解决链式思维中因过度思考造成的计算开销大、效率低的问题。

Method: 提出一种基于段落级自适应剪枝的强化学习框架SLAT，利用对高概率但低边际效用段落的理论分析，识别并选择性抑制冗余推理段落，实现高效且不牺牲准确性的推理生成。

Result: 在多个标准基准测试中，SLAT相比未压缩基线将推理长度减少了50%，同时保持了较高的准确性，建立了更优的准确性-效率帕累托前沿。

Conclusion: 理论上合理的、段落感知的剪枝策略是提升大语言模型链式思维推理效率的有前景方向。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Reasoning Models have significantly improved chain-of-thought (CoT) capabilities via reinforcement learning (RL). However, generated reasoning chains frequently suffer from structural redundancy (i.e., \emph{overthinking}), incurring high computational overhead without improving answer correctness. Existing mitigation strategies typically rely on token-uniform length penalties, which provide coarse, segment-agnostic pressure toward shorter outputs and can inadvertently suppress useful reasoning alongside redundancy. To address this, we demonstrate that inefficiency concentrates in high-probability segments with low marginal utility. We derive a theoretical characterization of segment suboptimality under the correctness-length trade-off objective and propose \textsc{SLAT} (Segment-Level Adaptive Trimming), an RL framework that selectively suppresses redundant segments based on this criterion. Empirical results on standard benchmarks indicate that \textsc{SLAT} establishes a superior accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier, reducing reasoning length by $50\%$ relative to uncompressed baselines while maintaining competitive accuracy. Overall, our results suggest that theoretically grounded, segment-aware trimming is a promising direction for efficient CoT reasoning in large language models.

</details>

Method: 提出Feedback Distillation，利用语言模型生成的特权反馈作为指导信号，使模型在token级别学习其自身的条件分布，从而获得细粒度监督并引入外部知识。

Result: 在Lean4定理证明任务中，Feedback Distillation相比GRPO展现出更高的策略熵和更好的pass@k指标表现；结合两者初始化可进一步提升性能，表明二者具有互补性。

Abstract: Post-training for reasoning models typically combines supervised fine-tuning with reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards, most commonly with GRPO. However, this algorithm suffers from sparse rewards, limited exploration, and mode collapse. Building upon recent works on self-distillation, we propose Feedback Distillation, a training method where the model is trained to match, at the token level, its own distribution conditioned on privileged feedback produced by a language model. Feedback Distillation offers token-level supervision and can inject external knowledge. Evaluating our method for Lean4 theorem-proving, we find that Feedback Distillation maintains greater diversity in generated trajectories than GRPO, yielding higher policy entropy and better pass@k scaling. The two methods are complementary: initializing GRPO from a Feedback Distillation checkpoint outperforms either method alone. All in all, our results suggest a promising avenue to improve post-training for complex reasoning.

### [303] [UniScale: Adaptive Unified Inference Scaling via Online Joint Optimization of Model Routing and Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30898)
*Kaiyu Huang,Xingyu Wang,Mingze Kong,Zhubo Shi,Yuqian Hou,Hong Xu,Zhongxiang Dai,Minchen Yu,Qingjiang Shi*

TL;DR: 本文提出统一推理扩展（UIS），将模型路由与测试时扩展（TTS）整合到一个统一的优化空间中，以解决现有方法在推理质量与计算成本之间的粗粒度控制和效率瓶颈问题。通过将自适应推理建模为上下文多臂赌博机问题，提出UniScale框架，利用LinUCB进行在线学习，结合效率感知和成本建模，在高维动作空间中实现稳定、可扩展的优化。实验表明，该框架能有效利用UIS空间中的协同效应，在多种动态推理场景下实现更精细且一致的性能-成本权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法分别处理模型路由和测试时扩展（TTS），导致性能调整粗粒度、存在容量上限和收益递减问题，且缺乏对动态环境的适应能力。需要一种统一机制来提升推理系统的灵活性与效率。

Method: 提出统一推理扩展（UIS）框架，将模型路由与TTS纳入同一优化空间；设计UniScale框架，将其建模为上下文多臂赌博机问题，采用LinUCB算法进行在线学习，并引入效率感知学习与成本建模以应对高维动作空间挑战。

Result: UniScale在多样化动态推理场景中实现了更精细、更优的性能-成本平衡，显著优于传统分离式方法，展现出良好的协同效应与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 通过统一模型路由与测试时扩展，构建了更具适应性和效率的推理系统，证明了联合优化在实际部署中的有效性。

Abstract: In real-world deployments of large language models (LLMs), balancing inference quality and computational cost has become a central challenge. Existing approaches tackle this trade-off along two largely independent dimensions: model routing, which switches among models of different scales to match request complexity, and test-time scaling (TTS), which adjusts inference-time compute within a fixed model for fine-grained control. However, this decoupled design introduces inherent limitations. Model routing yields coarse-grained, discrete performance changes due to the sparse set of model scales, while single-model TTS often encounters capacity ceilings and exhibits diminishing returns as compute increases. Moreover, treating the two mechanisms separately restricts adaptability in dynamic inference environments. To overcome these limitations, we introduce Unified Inference Scaling (UIS), which unifies model routing and TTS in a single optimization space. Building on this formulation, we propose UniScale, an online framework that models adaptive UIS as a contextual multi-armed bandit problem and learns inference policies via LinUCB. The framework incorporates efficiency-aware learning and cost modeling to ensure stable and scalable optimization over high-dimensional action spaces. Evaluation shows that UniScale effectively exploits the synergy in the UIS space to deliver a fine-grained and consistently better quality-cost trade-off across diverse, dynamic inference scenarios.

The benchmark tests three abilities: (1) predicting ball-to-ball collisions, (2) reasoning about wall bounces, and (3) estimating final ball positions after motion stops. We evaluate recent MLLMs from the GPT, Claude, Gemini, and Qwen families. Performance drops as simulation time increases and scene geometry grows more complex. We also observe a consistent failure mode we call "stasis bias": when the correct physical outcome is harder to infer, models tend to predict no interaction. These findings show where current MLLMs break down on visual dynamics and point toward the need for better physical inductive biases in multimodal architectures.

We show that modern generative architectures can instantiate and maintain these evaluative personas with high consistency, enabling a form of pluralistic, perspective-dependent benchmarking that more closely reflects real-world consensus variability. However, we further analyze the stability of these simulated evaluators under sequential inference and stochastic prompt perturbations, revealing systematic degradation in persona coherence that manifests as state-space drift and semantic inconsistency. These findings suggest that static alignment constraints are insufficient for sustaining robust evaluative behavior over time. Instead, we argue for the necessity of embedding dynamic, viability-driven regulatory mechanisms within generative systems to preserve coherent cognitive emulation. ### [307] [GraphARC: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Graph-Based Abstract Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31031)
*Saku Peltonen,August Bøgh Rønberg,Andreas Plesner,Roger Wattenhofer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GraphARC 是一个针对图结构数据的抽象推理基准，扩展了 ARC 的少样本变换学习范式。它要求从输入-输出对中推断变换规则并应用于新图，涵盖局部、全局和层次化变换。相比基于网格的 ARC，GraphARC 可大规模生成不同家族和规模的实例，支持系统性评估泛化能力。实验发现当前先进语言模型在图属性问答上表现尚可，但在完整图变换任务中表现不佳，存在理解与执行之间的差距，且在更大实例上性能进一步下降，暴露了扩展瓶颈。整体上，GraphARC 结合节点分类、链接预测和图生成，为未来图基础模型提供了有前景的测试平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 语言模型在图属性相关问题上表现良好，但在完整图变换任务中普遍失败，显示出理解与执行之间的差距。随着图规模增大，性能显著下降，揭示出模型在扩展性上的局限。该基准有效暴露了现有模型在复杂图推理任务中的不足。

Conclusion: GraphARC 为图结构数据的抽象推理提供了一个可扩展、多样化且系统性的评估框架，能够有效揭示当前模型在图推理中的局限性，是未来图基础模型发展的重要测试平台。

Abstract: Relational reasoning lies at the heart of intelligence, but existing benchmarks are typically confined to formats such as grids or text. We introduce GraphARC, a benchmark for abstract reasoning on graph-structured data. GraphARC generalizes the few-shot transformation learning paradigm of the Abstraction and Reasoning Corpus (ARC). Each task requires inferring a transformation rule from a few input-output pairs and applying it to a new test graph, covering local, global, and hierarchical graph transformations. Unlike grid-based ARC, GraphARC instances can be generated at scale across diverse graph families and sizes, enabling systematic evaluation of generalization abilities. We evaluate state-of-the-art language models on GraphARC and observe clear limitations. Models can answer questions about graph properties but often fail to solve the full graph transformation task, revealing a comprehension-execution gap. Performance further degrades on larger instances, exposing scaling barriers. More broadly, by combining aspects of node classification, link prediction, and graph generation within a single framework, GraphARC provides a promising testbed for future graph foundation models.

### [308] [Vector Linking via Cross-Model Local Isometric Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31100)
*Ziying Chen,Yang Cao,He Sun,Beining Yang,Tianjian Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Vector Linking的方法，用于在不同黑箱编码器生成的嵌入云之间，仅通过向量恢复跨模型对象对应关系。该方法基于对比编码器具有局部几何一致性（短距离近似保持，长距离因模型特异性失真而不可靠）的发现，设计了一种基于参考的迭代几何嵌入哈希算法，利用少量成对锚点种子集，通过哈希空间匹配和贝塔-伯努利后验聚合证据，逐步提升链接置信度。实验表明该方法在多种基准和模型组合下具有高精度与鲁棒性，适用于向量数据库集成和跨模型聚类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以在无监督条件下从不同模型产生的嵌入空间中恢复跨模型对象对应关系，尤其当模型独立训练且数据部分重叠时。本文旨在解决这一问题，实现高效、准确的跨模型向量对齐。

Method: 提出一种迭代的参考式几何嵌入哈希方法：将每个向量表示为到采样成对锚点的距离；通过哈希空间匹配生成候选链接；利用贝塔-伯努利后验聚合多视角证据，逐步将高置信链接作为新锚点进行迭代优化。

Result: 在多个基准数据集和模型对上验证了该方法的有效性，表现出良好的准确性与鲁棒性，即使在低重叠率、小种子预算及域外锚点条件下仍表现优异，成功应用于向量数据库集成与跨模型聚类任务。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了对比编码器间的局部几何一致性现象，并提出了有效的向量链接框架，为跨模型嵌入对齐提供了新的解决方案，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: We study Vector Linking: given two embedding clouds produced by different black-box encoders over partially overlapping datasets, recover cross-model object correspondences using only vectors. Empirically and theoretically, we show that independently trained contrastive encoders exhibit local geometric consistency: short-range distances are approximately preserved up to a scale factor, while long-range distances are not due to model-specific distortion. Building on this, we propose an iterative, reference-based geometric embedding hashing that recovers vector links from a tiny seed set of paired anchors. It represents each vector by distances to sampled paired anchors, proposes candidate links via hash-space matching, and aggregates evidence across views in a Beta-Bernoulli posterior to bootstrap high-confidence links as new anchors. Experiments across multiple benchmarks and embedding model pairs demonstrate accurate and robust linking under varying overlap, seed budgets, and out-of-domain anchors, with applications to vector database integration and cross-model clustering. Code is available at https://github.com/DBgroup-Edinburgh/VecLinking.

### [309] [LLM-FACETS: A Privacy-Preserving Framework for Evaluating LLM Transparency and Accountability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31167)
*Tom Lucas,Alessio Buscemi,Alfredo Capozucca,German Castignani,Barbara Delacroix*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLM-FACETS 是一个开源、浏览器可访问的框架，旨在为非技术从业者提供对大语言模型（LLM）的事实性、认知校准性和方法可复现性的评估能力。它通过插件架构支持三种用户角色（技术专家、领域专家、合规官），并遵循欧盟人工智能法案和NIST AI风险管理框架。数据流透明：确定性指标在自托管服务器内运行，不外传数据；LLM评判指标需显式连接外部API，用户自主控制凭证。框架通过词元级概率可视化、多评判者共识和RAG三联度量（忠实性、答案相关性、上下文相关性）实现透明性，支持任意新指标或数据集的无缝集成。通过18个指标与标准库的交叉验证，证明其可靠性与可复现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: LLM-FACETS成功实现了对18种不同评估指标的交叉验证，结果与标准参考库高度一致，证明其准确性与可复现性；框架具备良好的用户体验、安全性与可扩展性，显著降低非技术用户参与AI评估的门槛。

Conclusion: LLM-FACETS为非技术从业者提供了安全、透明、可复现的LLM评估解决方案，有效推动了负责任AI的落地，尤其适用于需要合规审查和多方协作的场景。其开源特性进一步保障了评估过程的可信度与独立性。

Abstract: Assessing whether Large Language Models outputs are factually grounded, epistemically calibrated, and methodologically reproducible is a prerequisite for responsible AI deployment. Yet auditing LLMs remains inaccessible to non-technical practitioners: existing tools require programming expertise and non-trivial environment setup, and cloud-hosted platforms transmit evaluation data to external services, creating barriers for domain experts and compliance officers legally responsible for AI oversight. We introduce LLM-FACETS (LLM FActuality Cross-EvaluaTion System): an open-source framework with a browser-accessible interface and a plugin architecture, structured around three practitioner profiles (technical experts, domain experts, compliance officers) that mirror the stakeholder categories identified in the EU AI Act and the NIST AI Risk Management Framework. The architecture makes data flows explicit: deterministic metrics (BLEU, ROUGE, BERTScore) run entirely within the self-hosted server with no outbound transmission; LLM-judge metrics contact external APIs explicitly, with users retaining full credential control. The framework operationalizes transparency through three mechanisms: token-level log-probability visualization for epistemic uncertainty, multi-judge consensus to mitigate judge bias, and RAG Triad metrics (Faithfulness, Answer Relevance, Context Relevance) to detect and localize hallucinations. A plugin architecture allows any new metric or dataset to be integrated without modifying the evaluation pipeline. The open-source implementation enables cross-checking across multiple metrics targeting the same property, ensuring reproducibility and decoupling AI accountability from the teams building the systems assessed. We verify the framework through cross-validation of 18 metric implementations against canonical reference libraries.

</details>

We identify conditions under which these implications depend only on a causal abstraction defined by the pathway of rare events, rather than on the full causal graph of the underlying system. Accordingly, we introduce an abstraction of causal structure to pathways of rare events that bridges simple verbal causal explanations and detailed causal modeling.

### [311] [TraceGraph: Shared Decision Landscapes for Diagnosing and Improving Agent Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31308)
*Junjie Nian,Kang Chen,Ge Zhang,Yixin Cao,Yugang Jiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TraceGraph 是一种基于图的框架，将多模型智能体的交互轨迹转化为共享的决策景观。它通过构建包含可观测动作-观察状态的图，并叠加结果导向的高效核心与陷阱区域，对每个轨迹进行三类事件（访问、陷阱暴露、修复）的总结。该方法揭示了传统聚合评分掩盖的导航差异，发现不同基准测试更侧重避免陷阱或从陷阱中恢复。此外，基于 TraceGraph 的陷阱感知恢复流程在 SWE-bench 上提升了修复率，表明其能有效指导模型改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体评估常将轨迹简化为通过率或奖励分数，忽略了丰富的交互过程信息；需要一种新方法来揭示任务中的决策模式和失败机制，以更深入理解模型行为差异并指导改进。

Method: TraceGraph 构建跨模型轨迹的图结构，基于可观测状态建立节点与边，识别出高效核心与陷阱区域，并将每条轨迹分解为访问、暴露于陷阱、修复三个事件；同时引入运行时陷阱检测器和轻量级延续策略，实现针对性修复。

Result: 在五个基准分割上，TraceGraph 揭示了隐藏在平均指标下的导航差异；在 SWE-bench 上，使用陷阱感知恢复策略后，官方解决率分别提升至 43.5%（按提供方触发子集）和 44.8%（常见触发实例），且存在提供方特异性优化效果。

Conclusion: TraceGraph 提供了一种统一的流程语言，用于分析智能体基准测试的本质、模型间的分歧点以及如何利用失败区域驱动后续改进，具有显著的分析与优化价值。

Abstract: Agent benchmarks increasingly record rich interaction trajectories, yet evaluation often reduces each rollout to a pass rate or reward score. We introduce TraceGraph, a graph-based framework that turns released multi-model agent trajectories into shared decision landscapes. For each task, TraceGraph builds a graph over observable action-observation states from pooled rollouts before model identity is introduced. It then overlays outcome-informed productive cores and trap regions, and summarizes each rollout with three events: Access, Trap exposure, and Repair. Across trajectories spanning five benchmark splits, TraceGraph profiles reveal navigation differences hidden by aggregate scores and show that splits differ in whether they reward avoiding traps or recovering from them. The same TraceGraph landscape also motivates a trap-aware recovery pipeline for SWE-bench: aruntime detector fires on states matching historical trap regions, then lightweight continuation policies are evaluated from the same prefix. On fired states, the best pooled single-factor policy raises official resolved rate from 40.4% to 43.5% on the per-provider fired subset and from 41.0% to 44.8% on common-fired instances, with provider-specific active components. Overall, TraceGraph provides a process vocabulary for asking what agent benchmarks test, where models diverge on a shared landscape, and how failure regions can guide downstream improvement.

### [312] [HypoAgent: An Agentic Framework for Interactive Abductive Hypothesis Generation over Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31370)
*Yisen Gao,Yixi Cai,Tianshi Zheng,Jiaxin Bai,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HypoAgent是一个用于知识图谱上交互式归纳推理的智能体框架，通过三个智能体（意图识别、假设生成、根因分析）解决现有方法在多轮对话中难以对齐自然语言意图及失败假设诊断不足的问题。实验表明其在常识与生物医学知识图谱上均达到先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可控假设生成方法在交互场景下难以处理多轮对话中的动态意图，并且在生成假设失败时缺乏细粒度诊断能力。

Method: 提出HypoAgent框架，包含三个智能体：意图识别智能体将用户话语和对话历史转化为可执行的知识图谱条件；假设生成智能体根据提取的意图进行可控假设生成；根因分析智能体诊断不可靠假设片段并利用知识图谱邻域探测识别可支持的修正方案。

Result: 在常识和生物医学领域知识图谱上的单轮、多轮及无条件设置下，HypoAgent在语义相似度方面达到当前最优表现。

Conclusion: HypoAgent有效提升了知识图谱上交互式归纳推理的能力，具备良好的可解释性与适应性，为复杂场景下的假设生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Abductive reasoning over knowledge graphs aims to generate logical hypotheses that explain observed entities or facts. Existing controllable hypothesis generation methods allow users to guide this process with explicit conditions, but they remain limited in interactive settings: they struggle to ground evolving natural-language intents across multi-turn dialogues and provide little fine-grained diagnosis when generated hypotheses fail. To address these limitations, we propose HypoAgent, an Agentic framework for interactive abductive Hypothesis Generation over knowledge graphs. HypoAgent integrates three agents: an Intent Recognition Agent that grounds user utterances and dialogue history into executable KG conditions, a Hypothesis Generation Agent that performs controllable hypothesis generation according to the extracted user intention, and a Root Cause Analysis Agent that diagnoses unreliable hypothesis fragments and leverages KG neighborhood probing to identify supported refinements. Experiments on commonsense and biomedical domain-specific knowledge graphs demonstrate that HypoAgent achieves state-of-the-art semantic similarity under single-turn, multi-turn, and unconditional settings. Our code is available at https://github.com/HKUST-KnowComp/HypoAgent.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在Blocks World和Minigrid两个案例研究中，基于ASP的CARCASS实现了有效的抽象，表明该方法在具备领域知识的情况下对强化学习具有显著潜力。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) enables autonomous agents to learn policies from experience, but realistic problems often involve enormous state spaces, making learning and generalisation challenging. Abstraction and approximation are therefore essential. Relational Reinforcement Learning (RRL) offers a way to reason about objects and their relations, and the CARCASS framework by Martijn van Otterlo demonstrates how logical representations can model Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) in first-order domains. Originally implemented in Prolog, CARCASS leverages domain knowledge to create powerful abstractions. We explore Answer-Set Programming (ASP), which is a rich and, contrary to Prolog, fully declarative modelling language, to realise CARCASS abstractions. We evaluate our ASP-based implementation in case studies of two domains, viz. Blocks World and Minigrid. Our results indicate that CARCASS with ASP provides a promising approach to constructing abstractions for RL, especially when domain knowledge is available.

### [315] [AutoSci: A Memory-Centric Agentic System for the Full Scientific Research Lifecycle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31468)
*Weitong Qian,Beicheng Xu,Zhongao Xie,Bowen Fan,Guozheng Tang,Jiale Chen,Xinzhe Wu,Mingtian Yang,Chenyang Di,Jiajun Li,Lingching Tung,Peichao Lai,Yifei Xia,Ziyi Guo,Yanwei Xu,Yanzhao Qin,Shaoduo Gan,Xupeng Miao,Bin Cui*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AutoSci 是一个以记忆为中心的智能体系统，旨在实现科学研究全生命周期的自动化。它包含四个模块：SciMem（结构化研究记忆）、SciFlow（五阶段研究流程）、SciDAG（基于有向无环图的多智能体协作）和 SciEvolve（基于反馈的持续进化机制），支持跨项目持久记忆与自我优化，填补了现有系统在完整性与持续性上的空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统科研依赖人力，耗时长且环节分散；尽管大模型驱动的科研智能体兴起，但现有系统无法完整覆盖研究全流程，缺乏持久记忆与自我改进能力，因此亟需一个统一、可演化的自动化科研系统。

Method: AutoSci 采用四模块架构：通过 SciMem 实现长期知识与项目级记忆分离；利用 SciFlow 控制从文献理解到反驳的五阶段流程；引入 SciDAG 的 DAG 多智能体结构提升复杂任务处理能力；通过 SciEvolve 将用户、实验、评审等反馈转化为对记忆结构、流程技能和模板的版本化更新，实现系统持续进化。

Result: AutoSci 实现了一个具备执行、记忆与自我演化能力的持续性科研环境，能够跨项目运行并不断优化自身研究策略，为自动化科研提供了可扩展、可维护的框架。

Conclusion: AutoSci 提出了一种面向全生命周期科学研发的内存中心型智能体系统，解决了现有系统在完整性、持久性和自进化方面的不足，为未来自动化科研奠定了坚实基础。

Abstract: Scientific research has traditionally been human-intensive, requiring researchers to coordinate literature, ideas, experiments, manuscripts, and review responses across long project cycles. The rise of LLM-based scientific agents creates an opportunity to automate this process. Such a system must support the full research lifecycle, maintain structured persistent memory across projects, and improve its own research procedures over time. However, existing systems either partially satisfy or fail to satisfy these requirements, leaving a gap for a unified automated scientific research system. As a result, we present AutoSci, a memory-centric agentic system for the full scientific research lifecycle. AutoSci is organized around four modules. SciMem provides schema-governed research memory, separating Long-Term Knowledge Memory for reusable scientific knowledge from Active Research Memory for project-level artifacts such as ideas, experiments, manuscripts, and reviews. SciFlow executes a five-stage lifecycle from literature understanding to rebuttal through a harness that controls state, context, verification, feedback, and orchestration. SciDAG augments difficult skills with DAG-shaped multi-agent operators and reusable stage-specific templates. SciEvolve converts feedback signals from users, experiments, reviews, and external environments into versioned updates to SciMem organization, SciFlow skills, and SciDAG templates. Together, these modules make AutoSci a persistent research environment that can execute, remember, and evolve across research projects. The code repository is available at https://github.com/skyllwt/AutoSci.

### [316] [LinTree: Improving LLM Reasoning with Explicitly Structured Search Histories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31492)
*Liwei Kang,Yee Whye Teh,Wee Sun Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型（LLM）在解决推理问题时如何利用搜索历史。通过对比基于搜索轨迹的条件策略与仅依赖当前局部状态的LLM启发式方法，发现仅拥有搜索历史并不足以超越传统启发式搜索。进一步分析表明，LLM推理轨迹中隐式表示的搜索树结构是限制性能的关键因素，因为回溯或切换分支时无法明确标识所重新访问的先前状态。为此，研究提出显式添加父指针以构建线性化树（LinTree）结构，结果表明该方法显著提升了任务表现和搜索效率，证明当搜索历史的树结构被显式表达时，其优势才能充分发挥，从而推动更结构感知的LLM推理表示设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索大语言模型在推理过程中是否能有效利用完整的搜索历史，相较于仅依赖当前局部状态的传统启发式方法，以提升搜索效率与任务性能。

Method: 在三个受控推理环境（积木世界、网格导航、推箱子）中，比较基于完整搜索轨迹的条件策略与仅基于当前状态的LLM启发式方法；引入显式父指针构建线性化树（LinTree）结构，评估其对性能的影响。

Result: 原始搜索历史的使用未能稳定优于启发式搜索；而引入显式父指针的LinTree结构显著提升了任务表现与搜索效率，优于隐式推理模型和基于LLM启发式的搜索。

Conclusion: 搜索历史只有在树结构被显式表达时才真正具有价值，这为开发更具结构感知能力的大语言模型推理机制提供了重要方向。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) often solve reasoning problems by generating intermediate traces that explore and revise partial solutions. From a search perspective, these traces can be viewed as linearized search trees, where the model extends a partial solution, abandons it when it fails, and backtracks to try alternatives. Compared with traditional heuristic-guided search, such a policy has a potential advantage: it conditions on the whole search trace rather than only on the current local state. We first test whether LLMs utilize this advantage by comparing trace-conditioned reasoning policies against best-first search equipped with an LLM heuristic that only observes the current local state. Across three controlled reasoning environments, Blocks World, grid Navigation, and Sokoban, we find that raw access to search history alone is not enough to reliably outperform heuristic search. We then study one possible reason: in LLM reasoning traces, the underlying search tree is only implicitly represented, and when the model backtracks or switches branches, the trace does not explicitly identify which earlier search state is being revisited. We show that adding simple parent pointers to explicitly represent the linearized tree (LinTree) structure improves both task performance and search efficiency relative to implicit reasoning models and LLM-heuristic-guided search. These results suggest that search history becomes most useful when its tree structure is made explicit, motivating more structure-aware representations for LLM reasoning.

</details>
